1.1 Wunnanumau missinnin noh matta paumshadt ukkunnoosoowaonkannoowout matchetooog, asuh matta neepauook ummayeuout matcheseaenuog, asuh matta apegk wutappuongaanoowout mamanowontamwaeninnuog.
1.2 Qut wuttapeneamooonk ohteau wuttenaumatuonkanit Jehovah, kah ut wuttinnaumatuoonganit nonatwontam kesukodtaeu kah nukkonaeu.
1.3 Kah pish ogqueneunkqussu mehtugqut ahketeamuk kishke sepupogqut, ne pautunk ummeechummuonk ut wuttuttoocheeyeumut: ooneepog wonk matta pish uppoopohtanoo, kah wame uttoh asit pish missegen.
1.4 Matchetukeg matta ne wuttogqueneunkqusseinneau: qut ogqueneunkqussuog wossadteamunit, uttiyeu tooanontog waban.
1.5 Newaje matchetukeg matta pish nepauooog wussittumooonganit, asuh matcheussecheg ut ummukkinneonganoowout wunnomwaeussecheg.
1.6 Newutche Jehovah oowahteauun ummayeu sampweussecheg: qut ummayeu matchetupanatogig pish awakompanomoo.
2.1 Tohwaje wutohtimoinneash musquantamooe wogkouehettit, kah missinninnuog unnantamohettit tahnooche teaguas?
2.2 Ketassootamwog ohkeit chipapheaog wuhh√≥gkauh, kah nananuacheg moaeu kenoonittuog ayeuuhkone Jehovah, kah ayeuuhkonittue sasequnonche, {noowaog}.
2.3 Paskuhkommuttuh wuttahtagkuppissooongash, kah amauhteatuh uppemunohtonooash wutch kuhogkanonut.
2.4 Noh apit kesukqut pish ahhanu: Lord pish ummameshananumwehtauuh.
2.5 Neit pish ukkenoonuh ut ummoosquantamooonkanit, kah wuttuhquantamweheuh ut kussopetae ummusquantamooonganit.
2.6 Qut onch nussussequnnop nukketassootamoom ut noonetupanatamwe wadchumut Sion.
2.7 Noowahteauwahuwam kesantamooonk: Jehovah nuttugkup, Ken nunnaumon, yeu kesukok koonaumoniyeumsh.
2.8 Wehquetumah, onk kuttinnumoush Wuttohtimmoinneash wutche kookompachasoom, kah wehquohkeyeuuk wutche kutohtoonk.
2.9 Pish kussukquttahwhoog nashpe moohshogque sauoppunk, pish kussoohquohkonog onatuh ahkuhqueteaenin oowisquadt.
2.10 Newutche waantamook woi Ketassootamwog, kuhkootammonteakq kenau ohkee wussittumwaeninnuog.
2.11 Wuttinninnumuhkohkq Jehovah nashpe wabesuonk, kah wekontamook nashpe nunnukshaonk.
2.12 Chipwuttoonapook wunnaumoniin ishkont musquantam, kah kuppagwanimwoo wutch mayut: ummusquantamooonk wepe oggusse nashqunnag wunnanumoog wame nag paubuhtanumoncheg.
3.0
3.1 Jehovah, toh inne kootneyeuooog neg wadtamehetcheg? monaog neg ayeuohkone waabehtunkqueoneg.
3.2 Monaog anoowacheg papaume nukketeahogkou: matta ahtoou aninnumoadtuonk ut Godut. Selah.
3.3 Qut ken woi Jehovah, ogqunneg wutche neen, nussohsumooonk, kah noh tohshinuk nuppuhkuk.
3.4 Nummauunitteauop Jehovah nashpe noowadtauwohtunkqussuonk, kah nunnootunkup wutch oonetupanatamwe wadchumut. Selah.
3.5 Nussepsinup, kah nukkouep, nuttookep, newutche Jehovah nukqukqununukup.
3.6 Matta woh noowabesuonoh piogque muttannunganogkussuog missinninnuog, nag ayeuuhkone weenuhkiitcheg.
3.7 Neepaush, Jehovah, wadchaneh woi num-Manittoom, newutche ken kuttogkomomp wame nummatwomog ut wannoonauukannooout: kuppuhquetahhamup weepittoowoash matchetukeg.
3.8 wadchanittuonk wutchaiyeumoo JEHOVAHUT: koonaneteaonk ohteau kummissinninnumehtu. Selah.
4.0
4.1 Nootah wehquetumon woi Manit na wadchiyeumoouk noonomwaeusseonk, kuppohquahwussip nanakuhpunnaon, kitteamonteanumeh, kah nootash nuppeantamooonk.
4.2 Woi kenaau wunnaumonauh wosketompaog tohsohkee kukqunnuppunumuneau nussohsumoonk en akodchinat? tohsohkee koowomantamumwoo tahnoocheyeuuk, kah kenatinneahamumwoo Pannoowaonk? Selah.
4.3 Qut wahteauook, Jehovah wutchippeponamonuh wanetupanatamunetcheh: Jehovah nunnootunk wehquetumauog.
4.4 Wabesek, kah ahque matchesek, kekuttoohkauook nehenwonche kuttahhoo ut kutappinnaout, kah chequnniekq. Selah.
4.5 Sephausekq wunnomwausseae sephausuonk, kah pabuhtanumoohk Jehovah.
4.6 Monaog noowaog, howan nahtinukqueog wanegik? Jehovah tahshinumaiinnean ooweequaioom kushkesuk.
4.7 Kummagun weekontamowonk ut nuttahut, moocheke onk monakish ooweatchiminnoooash kah oowineneumoo.
4.8 Naneese wunohteae nusseepsin, kah nukkouem, newutche webe ken Jehovah kootohkeahhe nanauiyeuonkganit.
5.0
5.1 Nootash nukkuttoowongash, woi Jehovah, natwontash nunnatwontammoowonk.
5.2 Kukkeihtash noowadtauatonkqussue mauwonk, nuk-Ketassootamoom, kah num-Manittoom; newutche kuppeantamoush.
5.3 Noowodtauatonkqussuonk pish kenootam nompoaeu, woi Jehovah; nompoaeu kussampwunnumauunun nuppeantamoonk, kah nuttushpoquaim.
5.4 Newutche ken Manit, matta kuttapeneumooh matchetoowonk: onk matta kooweetomukooh matcheseonk.
5.5 Asookitcheg matta pish neepauooog anaquabean, kussekeneau wame anakausitcheg matcheseonk.
5.6 Pish kuppaguanoog nag pannoowacheg, Jehovah kogkoanumau nushehteaenuh kah asookekodteaenuh.
5.7 Qut neen, pish nuppetutteam keekit ut monagish kummonaneteaonganash, kah koowabesuonitteaonganit, nowauwussummoowam unnogque kooneetupanatamukommukqut.
5.8 Sagkompaguneh, woi Jehovah, ut koonomwausseonganit, newutche nummatwomog; sampweteaush kummay ut anaquabeh.
5.9 Newutche matta wunnomwayeuonganinnoo wuttoonoowout, wuttinnomiyeumoo ahche matchetooonk, ukquttunganoo woshwi weenohkeyeuoo, wawetimmoowaog nashpe weenannu.
5.10 Paguas naghog, woi God, penushahettich nashpe nehenwonche ukkenoonittuonganoowoash: sohwohteash ut monakish ummatcheseonganooash, newutche kutchekehtunkquog.
5.11 Qut wame yeug paubuhtanumukqueaneg, weekontamohettich, nagwutteaeu weekontamoe mishontoowahettich, newutche nag kukkinhamauoog: wonk nag womontogeg koowesuonk weekontamowonukquish.
5.12 Newutche ken, Jehovah, koonanum wanomwae ussecheg: nashpe koowomoausuonk kooweenuhkauoog onatuh ogqunneg.
6.0
6.1 Woi Jehovah, ahque auskomeh ut kummusquantamowonganit, onk ahque sasamakouwheh ut kussopetae kumusquanetamoowonganit.
6.2 Monanumeh, woi Jehovah, newutche nunnoochumwes, woi Jehovah, neetskehheh, newutche nishkonash unkquanumwehtosooash.
6.3 Nukketeahogkou wonk mishe wuttamehpunnau: qut ken, woi Jehovah, tohuttooche?
6.4 Quinnuppish, woi Jehovah, pohquahwus nukketeahogkou: woi wadchaneh, newutche kummonaneteaonk
6.5 Newutche napumukish matta kummequanumitteoh: ut weenohket howan tabuttantamunkquean?
6.6 Nussauunnum nashpe nuttauohkontoowaonk, qunnenuhkon nutaiyum nutapin poomonsoowemou: nashpe nussuppequash nuttogquehchippadtoh nutappin.
6.7 Nuskesuk mohtupaemoo nashpe neuantamooonk: nano wussesekshau newutche wame nummatwomog.
6.8 Amaeitaegk, wame anakauseogish matcheseonk: newutche Jehovah nootamup nummauongane wadtauatunkqussuonk.
6.9 Jehovah nootamup nooweehquetumowonk; Jehovah pish neemunnum nuppeantamowonk.
6.10 Nummatwomog wame akodchehettich, & onkapunnahettich, & agodhettich tiatche.
7.0
7.1 Woi Jehovah num-Manittoom: kupbaubuhtanumoush, wadchaneh wutch wame neg noswehtahhukqueoneg, kah pohquahwusseh.
7.2 Ishkont sohkwushonau nukketeahogkounuh, onatuh qunnonou, sohkshadtunk, na matta adt pohquahwunnittumuk.
7.3 Woi Jehovah num-Manittoom, yeu usseos, matcheseonganoooouk ut nunnutchekonut.
7.4 Onkquodtauogis machuk noh wanuhkosuhp (nux, nuppohquohwhunop noh tohnooche wamatwomeomp)
7.5 Matwau wunnamatuhkauonch nukketeahogkonuh, kah tohqunonch, nux, taskuhkodch nukketeaonk ohkekontu, kah sepshittauutch nukquehtianumitteaonk puppissiyeuut. Selah.
7.6 Waapish, Woi Jehovah, ut kummusquantamooonganit: waabin kuhhog, newutche kogkeae ummusquantamooonkannoo nummatwomog: kah tookeansheh en ne wussittumoonganit ne anooteamweoph.
7.7 Nemehkuh mukkinneongane missinninnuog pish kooweenuhkongquog: newutche nag wutche qunnuhquiyeue qushkish.
7.8 Jehovah pish wussumau missinninnuh; wussumeh, woi Jehovah, neaunag noonomwausseonk, kah neaunag nuppannuppittahhaonk ne appehtunkqueh.
7.9 Woi ummatchetooonganoo matchetooog wohkukquohsitch, qut menuhkeh sampwesecheg; newutche sampweseae God qutchehtau metahhash, kah muttoounussoh.
7.10 Nuttongkooohqussoo wutch Godut, noh wadchanont sampwuttahonutcheh.
7.11 God wussumau wunnomwausseaenuh: kah God musquanumau matchetowoh asekesukogish.
7.12 Matta quinnuppekompauuk, pish kehtadtau wuttogkodteg, onchippinnau wutohtompe kah ukquoshwunnuh.
7.13 Kah wonk ukquoshwunnumauuh nuppooe auwohteaongash: ukquoshwuhqunnumauuh noswetahhoowacheg.
7.14 Kusseh, onkquamamooe kodnekehteau matcheseonk, wompequaou woskeheuwaonk, kah pannoowayeuonk neechau.
7.15 Wonteauh, kah ukkuthamun, onk petshau wonogqut ne kezteunkup.
7.16 Oowoskhuwaonk pish quinnuppemoo en nehenwonche uppuhkukqut, kah wutcheke usseonk pish pogkishin nehenwonche kodtantupont.
7.17 Nuttabuttantamau Jehovah neaunag oonomwausseonk: kah nuttinnoohumom oowesuonk Jehovah noh anue quanunkquapit.
8.0
8.1 Woi Jehovah, num-Manittoomun, uttoh unnukkukque wunnegen koowesuonk mamusse ohkeut: kupponam kussohsumoonk ongkouwe kesukqut.
8.2 Wutch wuttoonoowout mukkiesog, kah noonukeg kukkuhquttumup menuhkesuonk, newutche kummatwomog, onk woh kutchequnneh matwau onk anootont.
8.3 Moninneamon kukkesukkumash, kuppuhkukquanutchee anakausuonganash, nahnepaushadt, & anogqsog nish kukkeihtimopanneg.
8.4 Howan wosketomp woh mehquanumadt? kah wosketomp wunnaumonuh woh nadtauheadt?
8.5 Newutche kukkezheop ut agwesu Angelsog: & kutcheetuhquabinop nashpe sohsumoonk & quttianittuonk.
8.6 Kunnanaunumwahheop kenutchegane anakausuongash, kupponamup wame teanteaquassinash agwe wusseetash.
8.7 Wame sheepsog & oxenog, nux, kah ohteuhkone puppunashimwog.
8.8 Mamahchekesukque puppinushaog, kah ketahhane, namohsog, kah nishnoh pomushomoouk kuhtahhane mayut.
8.9 Woi Jehovah num-Manittoom uttoh en muttae wunneken koowesuonk ut mamuse ohkeut.
9.0
9.1 Koowawenomush, woi-Jehovah, nashpe mamusse nuttah, nunnahtutteam wame kummonchanatamwu anakausuwongash.
9.2 Nooweekontam & kummuskouanatamoowonsh: nuttinnoohomom koowesuong, woi ken anue quanunkquappean.
9.3 Ut wuttomponcheonkannoo nummatwomog, nag pish penashaog, & paguanuog ut anaquabean.
9.4 Newutche kutanumwontamiip nussampwiyeum, kah nootsinnoowong, kutapip wussittamooe appuonganit, sampwe wussittumunat.
9.5 Kuttaushkomomp penuwohteaog, kuppaguanomp matcheetowog, kutjiskhomup oowesuonganoo micheme & micheme.
9.6 Woi ken matwau, pagwanooonganash wohkukquoshinneash yauyatcheh: & kuppahpaguodtoh kehtootanash, mehquanumaonganoo ooweche nuppoomukqunneau.
9.7 Qut Jehovah pish michemeyeuoooo, quaquashweetamup wutapuonk wutche wussittumoowonk.
9.8 Kah pish sampwe wussittum muttaok, pish wussumau missinninnuh ut sampwiyeuut.
9.9 Jehovah wonk, spuhhoowaonkanuoo wutche sanukkuhkauutcheg spuhhoowaonkanuoo watammehpunnamukish.
9.10 Kah nag wahteunkig koowesuonk kuppabuhtanumukquog: newutche ken Jehovan matta kenukkonoog neg natinneahhukqueaneg.
9.11 Ketoohomok Jehovahut, noh watohkit Sionut, washadtauook wuttusseongash kenugke missinninnuog.
9.12 Natootomohteadt wutche wishqueheonk, ummehquanumuh nahog, matta wannantammoo ummauonganoo ohhohpanutcheh.
9.13 Monanumeh woi Jehovah, moninneash nootamehpunnaonk nashpe nag sekeneunkqueoneg, ken tahshinnean wutch nuppooongane squatamash.
9.14 Onk woh nunnahtehteam wame koowowenomitteaonk ut oosquantamash wuttaunoh Sion: pish nummishkauantam ut koowadchanuaonganit.
9.15 Penuwohteaog quttoushopanneg wonateaheganit ne kesehtouhitteup: wanahshahitteupoh, ahpeheonoh upputhukouoh ut nehenwonche wusseetuout.
9.16 Jehovah waheau nashpe wussittumooongash nish aseche, matchetou puttahwhou ut nehenwonche wunnutchegane usseonganit. Higgaion. Selah
9.17 Matchetowog pish qushkoohkauoog en chepiohkomukqut, wame wutohtimoinneash wananumoncheg Goduh
9.18 Newutche quenawehhikooenin matta pish nagwutteaeu wannanumou: wutannoosuonk matcheku, matta pish nuppoomunoo micheme.
9.19 Omohkish, woi Jehovah, ahque sohkositch missinnin, penuwohteaog wussumunaj ut anaquabean.
9.20 Wabesuah, woi Jehovah, onk woh wutohtimoinneash wahteauog nag webe wosketompoooog. Selah.
10.1 Tohwaje nepauwean noadut woi Jehovah, tohwaj puttogquean watammehpunnamukish.
10.2 Matchetoo ut uppehtu anumooonganit nooswetahwhau matchekuoh: nag tohqunnunnaj ut uppuhchuteaonganoo ne annantamwehhetteup.
10.3 Newutche matchetou mushkowau papaume wuttahhe kodantammooonk, kah wunnanumau iahchuwantam woh uttiyeuoh Jehovah uhquanummonche.
10.4 Matchetou ut uppehchuanumweneukqussuonganit, matta natinneawhoou Goduh, wame wuttinantamooongash matta Godunoo.
10.5 Ummayash nagwuteaeu unkqueneunkquodtash: koosittumoowongash wohqut ahtaash, wunnoonompatamunash; wame ummatwomoh, nah ummameshanimuh.
10.6 Unnoowop ut wuttahhut, matta pish nuttontsappu; ne wutche matta pish noowawuttamehpunoh micheme.
10.7 Wuttoon numwohteau matchenaneteaonk, kah asookekodteamooonk & puhchuteaonk: agwu weenannuut na woskehuwaonk kah tahnoocheyeuoouk.
10.8 Appu ut ootanamese onkkauompamukquodtash, assampamukquodtit wuttit nushon matta woskehuanutche: wuskesukquash ayeuuhkone kemompamau matchekuoh.
10.9 Keme askuhwheteau onatuh qunnonou ut oowonogqut: ashkuhwheteau tohqunnonat matchekuoh: tohqunau matchekoooh pasooont wuttahshabut.
10.10 Ohtaeu kah hohpaheau wuhhogkuh, onk woh matcheku penushau nashpe ummenuhkeseumoh.
10.11 Noowop ut wuttahhut, God mahche oowanatamun: puttoghum wuskesuk matta woh nanukqut naumoo.
10.12 Omohkish, woi Jehovah, woi God tohshinush kenutcheg: ahque wananum hohhohpacheg.
10.13 Tohwutch matchetou meshananumont Goduh? noowop ut wuttahhut, matta koonompagunnumooun.
10.14 Kenaumunap, newutche kenaumun woskehuwaonk, kah jishanumowaonk, onkquatontamunat nashpe kenutcheg: matchekuenin kuttahtuhshuk wuhhogkuh, ken aninnumauadt nag mat wadooshoogig.
10.15 Pohkshadtaush wuhpit matcheetou, kah matcheunniyeuwenin, natinnehash ummatchetoowonk no pajeh wane kenammehteooounat.
10.16 Jehovah ketassootammoooo micheme & micheme: mat-peantamookeg paguanuog wutch wutohkeit.
10.17 Jehovah, kenootamup ukkodtahtamooonganoo ohhohpacheg: pish kukquoshaeihtam wuttahhou, pish kunnootamohtoh kehtauog.
10.18 Wussummonat mat wadooshoogig, kah unkapunnanutcheg, onk muttaohke wosketomp, woh matta wonk unkapunnahteooo.
11.0
11.1 NUppaubuhtanum Jehovah, tohwaj unnog nukketeahogkou toowish onatuh psuksesit en koowadchumooout?
11.2 Newutche kusseh, matcheetoowog onchepunahteaog: quashinumwog ukkounkquodtou, ut wutahtumannoowout, onk woh keme pumwaog sampwutteahonutcheh.
11.3 Ohpohteashikish woskehteomuk toh woh wutusseneau sampweusseaenuog?
11.4 Jehovah appu wunnetupanatamwe wut-templeut, Jehovah wutappuonk ohteau kesukqut: wuskesukquash namoomooash, wanadteaskesukquash qutcheheau wunnaumonauh wosketompaog.
11.5 Jehovah qutcheheau sampweusseanuh, qut ukketeahogkounoh sekeneauau matchetoowoh, kah noh womontog chekeenehhuwaonk.
11.6 Matchetowoh pish wussokanummauoh ahpehhanoh, noohtau kah brimstone nashquttin: yeu wutchippiyeumooe ootattamwaechu.
11.7 Newutche sampweusseae Jehovah womantam sampweusseonk, wuttinnussuonk moninneamoomoo sampwuttahhonitcheh.
12.0
12.1 Anunnosish Jehovah, newutche wanne Manittoowompaunoowi; newutche paubuhtanumwaeninuog oggusseyeuoouk kenugke wunnaumonauh wosketompaog.
12.2 Unnoowaog tahnoocheyeuuk nishnoh howan weeche wetatteamungoh: nashpe waechummoowae mussisittoonash, kah nesinnue metah keketoohkaog.
12.3 Jehovah pish tummussum wame wawetimmuwae mussissittonash, kah meenan mahshoowomoouk.
12.4 Uttiyeug anoowohpanneg nashpe nenannunnonash pish nutomskosumun, nussissittoonunnonash nuttihenonash, howan wasantimameog?
12.5 Wutche onkapunnannaonk matchekoooh, kah ummishannomooonganoo quenauwehikqunnitche, yeuyeu nutomohkem (noowau Jehovah) nuppon nanauwiyeuut wutch noh mamishanumont.
12.6 Ukkuttoowongash Jehovah pahke kuttoowongash onatuh silver sabassumuk, ut ohkee sabassohsuonganit, nesausuk tahshit pahketeaumuk.
12.7 Pish koowadchanoog, woi Jehovah, kenanaiheoog yeu wutch pometuonganit micheme.
12.8 Matchetowog papomshaog nish noh ut, uhque matchetoowog ut kenugke wunnaumonauh wosketompaog tahshinnomuk.
13.0
13.1 TOhsohke pish koowananimeh (woi Jehovah) nagwutteaeu? tohsohke pish kupputtogkuhhumah kuskesuk.
13.2 Tohsohke pish nunnatwontam ut nukketeahogkounut? neuantamonish ut nuttahhut asekesukokish; tohsohke pish nummatwomog anue qunnuhqueheoog onk nen?
13.3 Natwontash kah nootah, woi Jehovah num-Manittoom, wequaiyeuhkontamah nuskesukquash; ishkont nukkouem nuppooe koueonk.
13.4 Ishkont nummatwomog noowaog, nutomskauop, kah yeug wadtammehukqueoneg muskouantamwog ontsappeon.
13.5 Qut nuppaubuhtantamup kummonaneteaonk, nuttah pish muskouantamoowontam koowadchanoowaonk.
13.6 Nukketoohomau Jehovah, newutche nukkogkutamunkquattunkup.
14.0
14.1 MAttamog noowop ut wuttahhut, wanne Godunoo, aninwog niskanakauseupaneg, wanne howan ooneusseu.
14.2 Jehovah womopoop wutch kesukqut ut wunnaumonaout wosketompaog; naumunat sun howan wohwohtam, asuh natinneawhon God.
14.3 Wame ammaook moeu niskeneunkqussuog: matta howan ooneussu, matta pasuk.
14.4 Sun wame anakausitcheg matcheseonk, matta oowohwohtammooonganeog? uttiyeug moohwhoncheg nummissinninnumoh, neane mechhettit petukqunneg, kah matta wehquetumauaoog Jehovah.
14.5 Na wuttut mishe wabesinnaop, newutche God appu ut uppometuonganit sampweusseanin.
14.6 Kutakodchehteomwoo ukkenoosoowaonk matcheku, newutche Jehovah wutushpuhhoowaonguh.
14.7 Howan pish makuk wadteanaonganoo Israel wutch Sionut? Jehovah qunnuppunnuk ummussinnoonkanoo ummissinninnumoh, Jakob pish muskauantam, kah Israel pish wekontam.
15.0
15.1 JEhovah, howan pish ayit kekit? howan pish wadohket kooneetupanatamwe wadchumut?
15.2 Noh pannuppeyeue pamshadt, kah anakausit sampweusseonk, kah noowadt wanum uhkuteyeuuk ut wuttahhut.
15.3 Noh matta noonimimonk nashpe wenan: asuh matta matchenehunk wetatteamunguh, kah matta nemunnumook kehkontooonk ayeuuhkone wetatteamunguh.
15.4 Noh wuskesukquash jishanumuksoowenin adt meshananumut; qut quhtianumau nag quohshoncheg Jehovah: chadchekewau en oowoskhukqunnat & matta osooweu.
15.5 Noh matta makook wutteaguash en sakepoowe anoohomooonganit, asuh neemunnummook onkquatonk ayeuuhkone noh matta woskhuadt, howan asit yeush matta pish ontsappu.
16.0
16.1 Wadchaneh, woi God: newutche kuppabuhtanumoush.
16.2 Woi nukketeahogkou, kittinnomp Jehovah, ken num-Manittoom: nooneetoowonk matta kootehtuhkonkkooun.
16.3 Qut ootehtuhkonkqunneau waneetupanatogig aiyitcheg ohkeit, kah wanekitcheg na ohtag wame nuttapeneamooonk.
16.4 Wunnoowantamooongannoowoash nano monatash kanuppe asuhkauoncheg onkatogeh manittooh, ootattamooe wusqueheonkane sephausuongash matta nussephausu, asuh nunneemunnumooh oowesuonganoo en nussissetoonit
16.5 Jehovah wutchippiyeum nutahtoonk kah nootattamwaitch: kenanaihteoh nuttittanohtoadtuonk.
16.6 Kuhkunnongash nootohtuhkonkqunash ut wunnegennue ohkeit, nux; wunnegen nutahtauonk.
16.7 Noonanum Jehovah noh kakahchummukqueomp: onk nuttoounissog nukkuhkootomunkquog ut nukkonnaeu uttoocheyeuash.
16.8 Nagwutteaeu nopponop Jehovah anaquabeh: newutche appu nuttinuhkounit, matta pish nutontsappu.
16.9 Newutche nuttah wekontam, kah nussohsumoonk mishkauanatamoomoo: kah nooweyaus pish anwohsinoomoo ut annoossuonkanit.
16.10 Newutche matta kenuhkonoh nukketeahogkou ut wenohkeit, asuh mat kuttinnanumoh kooneetupanatamwaeneum namunnat aninnooonk.
16.11 Pish koowahteauwahe may en keteaonganit: anaquabean wamat wekontamoonk, kuttinnohkounit wekontamoongash micheme kah micheme.
17.0
17.1 Nootash sampwiyeuonk, woi Jehovah, kuhkeitash nummauonk, nootash nuppeantamoonk, mat waj sohhamoomunoog eiantogkiyeue mussissittonut.
17.2 Noosummitteaonk sohhammoomooitch wutch anaquabean kuskesukquash naumoomooitch nish sampoiyeuukish
17.3 Kukqutchehteop nuttah, kenataaheup nukkonaeu kukquitchhip, kah pish monteag kummiskomoo: nukkesantam, nuttoon mat pish matcheyeumunnoo.
17.4 Papaume wosketompae anakausuongash, nashpe kussissittone kuttooongash, nunnanaweheomp nuhhog wutch ummayash asehtamwaenin.
17.5 Qukqunnunnush nuppomushaongash ut kummayash, onk woh matta nuttontannehtuogash toonukqushshanooash.
17.6 Koowehquetummauunup, newutche kenootah, woi God: ehquohtukquaeihtah, kah nootash nukkuttoowongash.
17.7 Nahtutteash monchanatamwe koowomoasooe usseonkash, woi ken wadchanadt nashpe kuttinohkou, nag paubuhtanumukqueoneg, wutch nag ayeuohkononcheg.
17.8 Wadchaneh neane mooeskesuk: puttogwheh agque wutonkouhtomut kenuppawhunash,
17.9 Wutch matchetoout nag onkapunnasitcheg, wutch nishehteae nummatwomog, nag weenuhkiitcheg.
17.10 Weyanehtunkqunneau nehenwonche oowesoo: nashpe wuttoonoo pittuanumweyeuog.
17.11 Yeuyeu noowenuhkunkqunnonog ut nuttontanehtuonganunnonut: wuskesukoowoash wunnauwakompattauunnaopash en ohkeiyeu;
17.12 Onatuh qunnonou kottuppooontog ne kodtohqunuk, kah onatuh wuskoshumwe qunnonou noh pattogque ayit assompamukquodtut.
17.13 Omkish, woi Jehovah, unnoh wuttameh, punuhteash: pohquahwhin nukketeahogkou wutch matchetoowut, uttiyeug wadtogkodteganean:
17.14 Wutch wosketompaog yeug wanitchegkanean, woi Jehovah, wutch yeu muttaohke wosketompaut, nag wachuppiyeumitcheg yeu ut pomantamooonganit, nag wunnogkuseuh namwamechumwehteaan, nashpe adtahtosooe kunnumpakoonash: wunnechanoowoh numwamechummooog, kah nukkodtumwog ne asqueyeuuk ummaumatchiyeumoowoash en uppeussesoommoowout.
18.0
18.1 Pish kummishe womonsh, woi Jehovah nummenuhkesuonk.
18.2 Jehovah nukqussukquanum, kah noowonkonous, nuppohquohwussuaeneum, num-Manittoom, nummenuhkesuonk noh pabuhtanumog: nuttogqunneg, kah wadchanittooe askon, kah nukqunnohque wonkonous.
18.3 Pish noowehkum Jehovah, noh tapenunkquissit waenomonat: nemehkuh pish nuppohquohwhunit wutch nummatwomut.
18.4 Nuppooe neuantamooongash mo noowenuhkunkup, kah wuttammagkonoomoooash matchetukeg mo noowapoowunnukquog.
18.5 Chepiohkomukque neuwantamooongash nukqunnuppuhkunkqunnapash: nuppooe ahpehhonah nuttiadche tohqunukqunapash.
18.6 Onkapunaon noowehquetumauop Jehovah, nummauonitteeuop num-Manittoom: nootamup noowadtauatongqussuonk wutch wut-Templeumut, & nummauonk peyaumooup anaquabit, en wuhtauogut.
18.7 Neit ohke nunnukshomoop, kah quequanup; wonk wadchue ohpohchashukkish ontohtopash kah quohquoshqushshopash, newutche musquanttmup.
18.8 Pukut uspemooup wutch wutchanit, kah noohteau wutch wuttoonut mahchukkussummoomooup; mahkohsaash ne nashpe noosuppasqunnanosoopash.
18.9 Wonk puskepuhkomup kesukquash, kah nookeep, kah pohkeniyeup agwe wussetut.
18.10 Kah noh nayeumukup cherub, kah tooweep: nux tooweep ut wunnupwhunut waban.
18.11 Pohkenai ootahsompamukquatuhkonap: week ne weenuhkunkup, pohkunuppogooup, kah kuhpogke mamahche kesukque mattogqsash
18.12 Waje wosuppaag ut anaquabit, kuhpoge mattogqsash pamemooash, mussegan, kah noohtae mohkossaash.
18.13 Kah Jehovah pataquohhannehteop ut kesukqut, noh quanuhquabit wadtauatunkqusseup, mussegan, kah noohtae mohkohsaash.
18.14 Nux pummoop ukkounkquodtash, kah wusseaoohkouopah; kah pepumoop kutshamun & wuttomskauopah.
18.15 Neit nippee passehtanash noquodtupash kah muttaohke ohpahteashikish pahke namunnapash, newutche kuttiuskomoowaonk woi Jehovah nashpe kutchanooe nashaonk.
18.16 Anooteamoop wutch wohqudt, nunneemunukup, nukkuhpunukup wutch monahkish nippeash.
18.17 Nuppohquohwhunukup wutch menuhkesue nummatwomut & wutch nag sekenaitcheg: newutche nag anue menuhkesuog onk neen.
18.18 Nunnekonuhkunkuppaneg ut nuttonkpunae kesukodtut; qut Jehovah noochetohkunkkanninnap.
18.19 Onk nussohhoowunukup en mummishkiyeuonkanit: nuppohquohwhunukup, newutche nooweteanumukup.
18.20 Jehovah nutonkquatonkup neaunag noonomwausseonk, neane pohkag nunnutcheganash nuttinnunkquatunkqunnap.
18.21 Newutche nunnanawehteop ummayash Jehovah, kah matta matchetooe nuttamaehtauop num-Manittoom.
18.22 Newutche wame oosittamooongash ohtopash anaquabeh, kah matta nuppogketamoop ukkuhkoowaongash.
18.23 Neen wonk nussamwesup anaquabit: kah nunnawehheomp nuhhog wutch nehenwonche nummatcheseonganit
18.24 Yowutche Jehovah nuttunkquattunkup neaunagup noonomwausseonk, neane pohkagup nunnutcheganash ut anaquabit.
18.25 Monaneteaeninyeuut pish kunnahtussoowam kummonaneteam, pannuppeyeueninyeuut, pish kenahtussoowam kuppannuppeyeuoo.
18.26 Pahkesooweninyeuut pish kenahtussowam kuppahkes, chenaosooweninyeuut pish kenahtussoowam nanuk kutchenaos.
18.27 Newutche pish koowadchanoog kuttumunge unkapunnae missinninnuog: qut kunnookunnoog pahtuanumweneunkqussitcheg.
18.28 Newutche ken pish kenashqussum noowequananteg: Jehovah num-Manittoom pish wequanantam nuppohkenaiyeuonk.
18.29 Newutche nashpe ken nuttasehtamup matwae chippanooog; kah nashpe num-Manittoom nukqueishontamup pummeneutunk.
18.30 God ummay pannuppeyeuoo: wuttinnoowaonk Jehovah pahkehteauun noh unkkoowohqussoooo en wame nag papahtanummoncheg.
18.31 Newutche howan Manittooit chippe Jehovah? asuh howan quasukquanuit chippe num-Manittoomun?
18.32 God nupputtukquabunuk menuhkesuonk, kah uppannuppehtauun nummay.
18.33 Nusseetash ogquehteau adtuhqusseetit, kah nupponuk ut nukqunuhquiyeuongash
18.34 Kuhkootumwontam nunnutchegash mattompagkuhkonat, kah mooohshogkquohtomp pohkunnosoo nashpe nuhpittenash.
18.35 Kah wonk kittinnumaiip koowadchanuae ogqunneg, kah kuttinnohkou nukqukqununukup, kah kummanunnissuonk nummishhukqunnap.
18.36 Kummishe kishkehtiup nuttontannehtuongash agwu nuhhogat, onk matta nuttoonukqussinoop.
18.37 Noonomatuhkouomp nummatwomog, kah nummattanopanneg: onk matta wonk nukqushkoop napajeh nuppagquannonaop.
18.38 Nutchadchetohwhopanneg onk matta tapenummoopanneg omohkenat; punnushopanneg agwe nusseetut.
18.39 Newutche kupputtukquoppinnip nashpe menuhkesuonk en ayeuwuttinat: nag ayeuuhkone nepaehtunkqueoneg, kenauwosikompauheopenneg agwe nuhhogkat.
18.40 Wonk kuttinnumaiup wussittuppukanoooash nummatwomog; onk woh nuppaguanoog neg sekeneaitcheg.
18.41 Mauoopanneg, qut matta howan uppohquohwhunnopah; nux, en Jehovah, qut matta wunnampohamauopah.
18.42 Neit nussukquhtahwhopaneg onatuh puppissi waban tooanontog: nussohwhohkonopanneg onatuh pussogq ut mayuhkontu.
18.43 Kuppohquohwussip wutch wuttaiyeuohkosoowaonkanoo missinninnuog: kah koopuhkuhhoowahhip penuwohteaog: missinninnuog matta wahheoogig pish nootinninneumuhkunkquog.
18.44 Quenau pittamwonukqueon pish nunnooswehtunkquog; penuwohteaog pish wonkummooe nutagquappehtunkquog.
18.45 Penuwohteaog pish mahchummooog pish wabesuog wutch wutassompamukquodtoomoooash.
18.46 Jehovah pomantam, & wunnanumunaj nukqussukquanum, kah tahshununnaj wadchanoowae num-Manittoom.
18.47 Unnoh God annootauanshikqueh, kah naosikompaaiheunt missinninnuh ut agwe nuhhogkat.
18.48 Nuppohquohwhunuk wutch nummatwomut; nux, kuttahshineh anue onk yeug nepauehtunkqueoneg, kuppohquohwussip wutch chekenehhoowaeninyeuut.
18.49 Newutche kuttabuttantamoush, woi Jehovah, ut kenugke wuttohtimmoinash; & nuttunoohhomom waenotooongash en koowesuonganit
18.50 Mishe pohquahwussuaong wuttinnumauon ukkehtassootamoomoh; kah nohtinau monanitteaonk sasequnonche, en David, kah en ooskanemunneoh micheme
19.0
19.1 Kesukquash onttuttumoomooash wussohsumoonk God. kah mamachekesuk nahtehteomoo wunnutchegane anakausuonk
19.2 Kesukodash hohsuhkoeu kuttoomooash kah nuhkonash hohsuhkoeu nahtehteomooash waehteoonk.
19.3 Wanne unnontoowaonkanunnoo asuh penoowontoowaonkanunnoo adt mo nootamoomuk ukkuttowonganoo.
19.4 Uppemunneohtono pannupshaumoop wame ohkeit, kah ukkuttoowonganooooash en wehqshik muttaohk; na ut upponamunap wetu wutche nepauzoh.
19.5 Uttiyeu aquinneunkquohk wussentamwaenyeuut waj sohhog wutchamberumut, kah mushkauanumoo onatuh munnehkesuenin quttomoshonat.
19.6 Wussohhamooonk wutch wahqshik kesuk, kah oowauweuhshaonk na en wehquohtag; kah moteag adtahtosunnoo wutch ukkussapsooonganit.
19.7 Wuttinnaumatuonk Jehovah panuppeyeuoo, quanuppinont keteahogkounoh; oowauwaonk Jehovah wunnamuhkuteyeuoo, waantamwaheont asootuoh.
19.8 Ukkuhkoowaongash Jehovah sampwiyeuash, mushkauantamwahteooomooash metah: wutanooteamoowonk Jehovah pohkoi, wequaiyeuhteomoouk muskesukquash.
19.9 Qushaonk Jehovah pohkoi, michemohteau: oosittummooongash Jehovah wunnamuhkuteyeuooash kah wame sampwiyeuooash moaeu.
19.10 Moocheke woh kodtantamunash onk ne gold, nux, onk moocheke wanegik gold; wonk anue wekonash onk ne hony, kah hony-combe.
19.11 Wonk nashpe nash kuttinninneum amomon: kah nesh nanawehteomuk mushonkquottunkanoooo.
19.12 Howan woh waehtunk uppanneusseongash? pahkhe wutch keme matcheseongash.
19.13 Wonk kogkanin kuttinninneum wutch mat qushe matcheseongash, ahque piahtimehhettich: neit pish nuppannuppeyeuoo, kah nuppahkes, wutch mahsag poohquenumoonganit.
19.14 Nuttoone kuttooongash, kah nuttahhe natwontamooongash tapeneunkquatitch ut anaquabean, woi Jehovah nukqussukquanum kah nuppohquohwussuaeninneum.
20.0
20.1 Jehovah namppoohamonkqush ut wuttammehpunnae kesukodut, ooweesuonk um-Manittoomoh Jacob qunuhquapehhukqush.
20.2 Anoononch aninnumoadtuonk wutch peantamwakomukqut: kah menuhkhukqush wutch Sionut.
20.3 Mehquantaj wame kummagooonganash; tapeneaj chikohtae kussephausuongash. Selah.
20.4 Uninnumungqush neaunag nehenwonche kuttah, kah usseetch wame kukkenoosoowaonk
20.5 Pish noowekontamumun koowadchanoowaonganit kah ut oowesuonganit num-Manittoomun nunnepattomun nummuttaagunun: Jehovah usseetch wame koowehquttumoowonganash.
20.6 Yeuyeu noowahteoun Jehovah wadchanau sasequnonche: pish wunnampoohammauuh wutch oonetupanatamwe kesukumut, nashpe wadchanoowae wuttinohkounne menuhkesuonk.
20.7 Nawhutch pabahtanittamwog chariotsash, nawhutch horsesoh: qut nenawun nummequontamumun oowesuonk Jehovah num-Manittoomun.
20.8 Nag nookeahheoog kah penushaog; qut nenawun nutomohkemun & nussampkompomun.
20.9 Wadchannuash Jehovah, kehtassoot nootunkquttuh wehqutteamweog.
21.0
21.1 KEtassoot pish muskouantam ut kummunihkesuonganit, woi Jehovah, kah ut koowadchanoowaonganit uttoh pish nukkukque muskouanatam!
21.2 Kuttinnumauop wuttahhe kodtantammooonk, kah matta kukkogkonumoop wussissitoone wehquetumooonk. Selah.
21.3 Newutche kunnogkuskomwah nashpe wunnetooe wunnanittuongash: kupponum pahke golde chetuhquap uppuhkukqut.
21.4 Koowehquetumunkup keteaonk, kah kittinnumauonap, sepepomantamooonk micheme kah micheme.
21.5 Wussohsumooonk missi ut koowadchanoowaonganit, quttianittuonk kah mamuttanittuonk kuppoonumauop.
21.6 Newutche kummoocheke wunnanumwaheop micheme: kummishe wekontamwaheop nashpe kuttinsuonk.
21.7 Newutche ketassoot pabahtanumau Jehovah, kah nashpe ukkitteamonteanitteaonk anue quanuhquabit noh matta pish ontsapooh.
21.8 Kenutcheg pish namehheau wame kummatwomoh, kuttinnuhkou pish namehheau yeug sekeneunkqueaneg.
21.9 Pish kuttogqueheoog kesompskittae ovenit musquantaman: Jehovah pish ummishashqunneuh ut ummoosquantammooonganit, & noohteau pish ummahchikkussoowooh.
21.10 Wutonsetuonganoo pish kuppagquodtoh wutch ohket, kah ooskannemunnoh wutch kenugke wosketompaog wunnaumonaont.
21.11 Kukkod matchenehhukkuppanneg; natwontamuppanneg woskehhuwae natwontamooonk, ne matta tappunnumhitteg ussenat.
21.12 Newutche pish kuttannummukkompawehheoog, quoshwuhqunuman ayeuuhkone nag wuskesukoowooh.
21.13 Qunnuhqhitteash, woi Jehovah, ut nehenwonche kummenuuhkesuonganit: ne mehkuh pish nukketoohommomun kah noowowenotumumun kummenuhkesuonk.
22.0
22.1 NUmmanittoom, num-Manittoom, tohwaj nukkossean? tohwaj noapean wutch noowadchanitteaonganit, kah wutch nummaue kuttooonkanash?
22.2 Woi num-Manittoom kesukodtae nunnanomponwam, qut matta kenootamuh, kah nukkonaeu, kah matta nuttohkoowoh.
22.3 Qut koonetuppanatamweyeuoo, woi ken watohkean oowawenomoowaonganoowout Israel.
22.4 Nooshunnonog kuppabahtanummukuppaneg, pabahtantamuppaneg, kah kuppohquohwhunopaneg.
22.5 Kummauunnittunkuppanneg, kah pohquohwunnopanneg; kuppabahtanumukuppaneg, kah matta ogkodchupaneg.
22.6 Qut nen nuttoohquau & matta noowosketompooo: wuttushpunnamooaonkannoo wosketompaog, kah nummeshannanumukquog missinninnuog.
22.7 Wame neg naitcheg, nummammohchanumehtunkquog: mommoshkuttoonaeog, nunnukukquoshaog, {noowaog},
22.8 Pabahtanumop Jehovah, uppohquohwunukqunat: pohquohwunonch newutche wuttapeneauuh.
22.9 Qut ken noh nemmunneohp wutch otomukut; kuttannoossoowahhip, nonontamon wussogkodtunkash noohkas.
22.10 Nuttunnuhkonteap kohhogat wutch otomukut: keen num-Manittoom wutch nohkas wunnogkussit.
22.11 Ahque nooosuhkah, newutche wuttamehpunnaonk paswohteau; newutche wanne howan nuttannumungkoo.
22.12 Monaog bulsog noowenuhkunkuppaneg: menuhkesooe Bashane bulsog noowenuhkunkupaneg.
22.13 Nuttoannehtunkuppanneg, onatuh moohmooshkuppooe kah nehnehteae qunnonou.
22.14 Nussookinnit onatuh nippe, kah wame nuskonash panikkonnaiyeuash: nuttah onatuh waxut, mahche soppahteau ut noeu nunnogkusseet.
22.15 Nummenuhkesuonk nunnohteau onatuh kodchuhkwishquadt, kah neenan pissogquemoo en nutompehkonit, onk kuppasooweh nuppooongane puppussiyeuut.
22.16 Newutche anumwog noowenuhkunkupanneg, matchetooe mukkunneonk noowenuhkunkup: kanitteukquamuppaneg nunnutchegash kah nusseetash.
22.17 Woh nutapogketam wame nuskonash: nukkehkinneungquog, kah nummosompamukquog.
22.18 Chachapenumoadtoopaneg nuttogoonash, kah wutche nuppetashqushaonk tummaskunnumoatoopanneg.
22.19 Qut ahque ken nooosuhkah, woi Jehovah, woi ken nummenuhkesuonk, teanuk aninnumah.
22.20 Pohquahwhus nukketeahogkou wutch togkodtega anit: nunnegonnoowomoneg wutch ummenuhkesuonganit anum.
22.21 Pohquahwusseh wutch qunonou wuttoonut: newutche kenootiip wutch wutaskonnoowout nukqutyeuunaog.
22.22 Nukkuhkootomau neematog koowesuonk: ut noeu mukkinneonganit koowawenomish.
22.23 Kenaau quoshagish Jehovah waenomoohk; wame kenau ooskannemunneoh Jacob, sohsumooonook; kah qushook, wame kenau ooskannemunneoh Israel.
22.24 Newutche matta meshannantamoop asuh jishantammoop ootammehpunnaonk wodtammehpunadt: asuh matta upputtoguhhumauoun wuskesuk, qut mauinittauont, nootamup.
22.25 Noowowenomoowaonk pish wutchiyeumoo kuhhogkat ut mishe mukkineonganit: pish nutatoehteam nukquoshomuwaongash nag anaquabhettit quoshoncheg.
22.26 Maninnissuog pish meetsuog kah tapepooog: nag pish wawenomaog Jehovah tiyeug natineawhoncheg; kuttahhoo pish micheme pomantamoomoo.
22.27 Wame wahqshikish muttaohk pish mehquontamwog kah quinnupeog en Jehovahut: kah wame wuttohtimmoine unnawatuongash pish wowussummuwaog ut anaquabean.
22.28 Newutche ketassootammoowonk ootihein Jehovah; kah nagum nanaunnuwaenin kenugke wutohtimoinneash.
22.29 Wame wonogqutcheg wosketohkeit pish meetsuog, kah wowussumoowaog: wame womsitcheg en puppissiyeuut, pish nauwaeog ut anaquabit, kah matta howan woh pomantamwaheooo nehenwonche ukketeahogkonoh.
22.30 Wuskanneem pish wuttinninneumuhkunk, ne pish ogquontamun en Johovahut wutche pometuonk.
22.31 Nag pish peyauog, kah pish wahteauwahuwaog wussampweusseonk en missinninnuut nag pish nekitcheg, newutche yeu wutussenap.
23.0
23.1 JEhovah nussohkommoonukkoowaeneum, matta pish nukquenawehuhkoo.
23.2 Nusseepsumwahik ashkoskuhkontu: nukkehchuwunuk manunushae nippeit.
23.3 Ompponchuwunnau nukketeahogkou: nutussoowunuk wunnomwausseongane mayut newutche oowesuonk.
23.4 Nux; tokonogque pomushaon onauuhkoiyeuut nuppoe onkauuhtaut, matta pish nukquehtamoo woskehittuonk: newutche koowetomeh, kuppogkomunk kah kutanwohhou nuttaphukqunash.
23.5 Koonechoohkah ut anaquabeh, anaquabhettit nummatwomog: kussissequnum nuppuhkuk nashpe pummee, nootattamwaitch pohponetupahshau.
23.6 Wunnamuhkut wunnayeuonk kah monaneteaonk pish nutasuhkonkqunash tohsahke pomantam: kah pish nuttaiin wekit Jehovah micheme.
24.0
24.1 OHke wuttaihe Jehovah, kah neadtahshimmechimik. muttaok kah neg na wadohkitcheg.
24.2 Newutche ukquenuhtauunap kehtahanit, kah ummunnuhkehtauunnap woskeche sepuut.
24.3 Howan pish kohkuhquet en oowadchumut Jehovah? kah howan nepauut ooneetupanatamwe ayeuonganit.
24.4 Noh pohpohkenutchont, kah pahketeahont; noh matta tatahshunnunk ukketeahogkonuh en tohnoocheyeuut, asuh aohsookohkodteamooe chachekeyeuadt.
24.5 Noh pish attumunum wunnanetuonk wutch Jehovahut, kah wunnomwausseonk wutch oowadchanuae Manittoomut.
24.6 Yeu uppometuonganoo nag natinneawhoncheg, natinneahogig kuskesuk, yeuuh Jacob. Selah.
24.7 Tahshinumook kuppuhkukooooash, woi kenau squontamash, kah tahshinnutteagk kenau michemohtae squontamash, kah sohsumoe ketassoot pish petutteau.
24.8 Howan yeuuh sohsumoe ketassoot? Jehovah noh manehkesit kah mamukquompaet, Jehovah mamukquompaet ut ayeuwuttuonganit.
24.9 Tohshinumook kuppuhkukooooash, woi kenau squontamash, kah tahsheg kenau michemohtae squontamash, & sohsumoe ketassoot pish petutteau.
24.10 Howan yeuuh sohsumoe ketassoot, Jehovah wattiyeuwehteomit ahhontanooongash, noh sohsumoe ketassoot. Selah.
25.0
25.1 KUttahshinnumaush nukketeahogkou, woi Jehovah
25.2 Woi num-Manittoom, kuppabuhtanumush, ahque akodchitti; nummatwomog ahque mushkoantammoowoshettich.
25.3 Nux, wanne howan akodchukitch nag pahtussuonukqueaneg; nag akodjhettich tahnooche matchesecheg.
25.4 Nahtusseh kummayash, woi Jehovah; kuhkootomah kuttaongash
25.5 Sagkompaguneh ut koonomwaonganit, kah kuhkootomah: newutche ken noowadchanitteae Manittoom, ken kuppahtussuonush mamusse kesukod.
25.6 Mehquontash, woi Jehovah, wohquanteae kukkuttummonteanitteaongash: kah koowomoausue monaneteaongash, newutche nish noadt aohtopash wutche michemeyeuut
25.7 Ahque mehquontash wuskenue nummatcheseongash; asuh nuppohqunnumooongash: neanag kummonaneteaonk unummehquanumeh, wutche konetooonk, woi Jehovah.
25.8 Wunnetou, kah sampwesoo Jehovah: yowutche pish kuhkootamauau matcheseaenuh ut mayut.
25.9 Pish sampoowunnau manunnissuoh ut wussittumooonganit: kah kuhkootomauau manunnissuoh ummay.
25.10 Wame ummayash Jehovah monaneteaonganuooash kah wunnomwaonganuooash, nah en nanaehtauunutcheh oonoowaonk, kah oowauwaongash.
25.11 Wutche koowesuonk, woi Jehovah, ahquoantamah nummatcheseonk: newutche ne missi.
25.12 Howan noh quoshont Jehovah? pish ukkuhkootomauuh ut mayut uttiyeu pish pepenog.
25.13 Ukketeahogkounoh pish ayeuoh wunnayeuonganit: kah ooskannem pish wutahtauinin ohke.
25.14 Jehovah ukkemeyeuonk oowechiyeumukqunnau neh quoshukqutche: kah pish wunnohtinuh oonoowaonk.
25.15 Nuskesukquash nagwutteaeu unnogquohtaash Jehovahut: newutche pish kodtinnum nusseetash wutch hashabpit.
25.16 Quinnupish en nuhhogkat, kah monanumeh: newutche nunonsiyeu kah nootamehpunam.
25.17 Nuttahhe wuttammehpunnaongash mishehtosooash: woi sohhoowuneh wutch nunnanakompanaonganit.
25.18 Moninneash nutonkapunnaonk, kah nutonkquomomoowonk, kah ahquoantamah wame nummatcheseongash.
25.19 Natwanum nummatwomog, newutche monaog, kah nutjishanumquog nashpe uhque jishanittuonk.
25.20 Woi nanaeh nukketeahogkou, kah pohquahwusseh: ahque akodchitti, newutche kuppabuhtanumush.
25.21 Panuppeyeuooonk, kah sampwesuonk wadchanhettich: newutche kuppahtussoowonush.
25.22 Pohquahwhus Israel, woi God, wutch wame ootamehpunnaongash
26.0
26.1 WUssumeh, woi Jehovah, newutche nuppompomusham ut nuppanuppeyeuonganit: kah nuppabuhtanumop Jehovah: newutche matta pish nuttoonequssinoo.
26.2 Natootomah, woi Jehovah, kah qutcheheh, qutcheh nuttoounnussog kah nuttah.
26.3 Newutche koowomoausuonk ohteau anaquahtag nuskesukquash: & nuppompomushop koonomwayeuonganit.
26.4 Matta nooweetapoomop tahnoocheyeuwutcheg, asuh matta pish nooweche petutteomoh eiantukiyog.
26.5 Nussekenamup ummukkinneonganoo matchesecheg: kah matta pish nooweetappumoh matchetoowog.
26.6 Pish nukkutshitto nunnutchegash pahkesooonganit: nemehkuh nukquinnupuhkom kut-Altaroom, woi Jehovah.
26.7 Onk woh noowashadtoh nashpe wadtauatongqussue tabuttantamoonk, kah nuttontuttumunash wame kummohchanatamwe anakausuongash.
26.8 Jehovah, noowomontamup keeke wuttohkeonk, kah ayeuonk uttoh wadtohkemoouk kussohsummooonk.
26.9 Ahque mukkin nukketeahogkou weeche matcheseaenuut, asuh nukketeaonk weeche nushehteaenuog.
26.10 Uttiyeug wunnutcheganooout woskehuaongayeuuk: kah wuttinnohkounnoo namwohtosik nashpe magkooonk.
26.11 Qut neen, pish nuppomuhsham ut nuppanuppeyeuonganit: pohquohwhunneh, kah monanumeh.
26.12 Nusseet ohteau tatuppahteaiyeuut: ut mukkinneonganit pish noonanum Jehovah.
27.0
27.1 JEhovah noowequaioom, kah noowadchanitteaonk, howan woh quoshog? Jehovah ummenuhkesuonk nukketeaonk, howan wohquoshog?
27.2 Matchetooe nummatwomog, kah ayeuuhkausitcheg nohkuhkoihettit meechinat nooweyaus, nag togkusitassunuppanneg kah punnishshopanneg.
27.3 Tohkonogque ahhunttanoowog ayeuuhkone weenuhkiehettjt, nuttah matta pish wabesu: tohkonogque ayeuwuttuonk waabehtunkqueon, yeu nuttut papahtantamun.
27.4 Pasuk nukkodtantamauop Jehovah, ne pish nunnatinnahamun, onk woh nuttaiin weekit Jehovah tosahke pomantam, naumunat oonisuonk Jehovah, kah nunnattoomuonat ut wuttempleumut.
27.5 Newutche wuttammehpunnae kesukodut pish nutadtashuk ut weekit, adt assompamukquohk uppeantamwakomuk pish nutadtshuk, pish nukquenapehuk qussukquanit
27.6 Kah yeuyeu nuppuhkuk pish tashunumun anue onk nummatwomog quanuppuhkiitcheg; newutche pish nussephas ut uppeantamwakomukqut wekontamoe sephausuongash, nukketohomom, nux nuttinnoohomom wawenomoowaogash en Jehovahut.
27.7 Nootash, Jehovah, mauon nashpe noowadtauatunkqussuonk: onk monanumeh, kah nampoohumah.
27.8 {Anoowaan}, natinnahamook nuskesuk; nuttah kuttukup, kuskesuk, woi Jehovah, pish nunnatinneoham.
27.9 Ahque puttogwhush kuskesuk wutch nuhhogkat, ahque kuttinninneum musquantamwe pogkes: ken mo nuttanumonteaonk, ahque nukkosseh, asuh ohquanummeh woi noowadchanitteae Manittoom.
27.10 Noosh kah nookas ahquanumehettit, neit pish Jehovah nunnemunuk.
27.11 Kuhkootomah kummay, woi Jehovah, kah ussoowusseh ut sampwe mayut, newutche nummatwomog.
27.12 Ahque magush nuhhog en wuttenantamooonganooout nummatwomog: newutche pannoowae wauwacheg noowaabehtongquog, kah noh nohnohshontog chekeusseonk.
27.13 {Woh nussauunumup}, matta wunnamptamoowous nunnaumunat oonissooonk Jehovah ut wutohkeout pamantogig.
27.14 Pahtussoowous Jehovah, wuttooantash, onk pish menuhkehteau kuttah: nissim, pahtussoowous Jehovah.
27.15 Qut nen, pish nummoninneam kuskesuk ut wunnomwaeusseonganit: pish nuttaphitch toohkeon ut kuttinsooonganit.
28.0
28.1 PIsh kummauunittaush, woi Jehovah nukqussukquanum, ahque chequnappehtah; ishkont chequnappehtiean, woh nutogqueneunkqus neg womussitcheg en passohtheganit
28.2 Nootash noowadtauatonkqussue peantamoongash, mauunnittauunon; uspunnumon nunnutchegash unnngque koonetuppanatmwe nampoohamooe ayeuonganit.
28.3 Ahque wechoowusseh matchetout, kah weeche anakausitcheg macheseonk; nag wunnohteae konnoononcheg weetatteamunganoouh, qut woskehuwaonk ohteau wuttahhoowout.
28.4 Nag ununumau neaunag wutusseonganoowoash, kah neane matchehk ukqutchunnitteaonk[a]nnoowoash: ununumau neanag wunnutchegane anakausuonganoowoash, nag unnunumau wuttunkquatonkanoo.
28.5 Newutche wanne tupantamooog wutanakausongash Jehovah, asuh wunnutchegane usseongash, pish uppaguanuh kah matta oowekuhkonuh.
28.6 Wunnanumaunach Jehovah, newutche nootamup wattauohtunkqussooe noowehquttummooonkash.
28.7 Jehovah nummenuhkesuonk, kah nuttogqunneg, nuttah uppabuhtanumopoh, kah nuttanumont: newutche nuttah mushkauantammoomoo, kah nashpe nukketoohhomaonk pish noowawenom.
28.8 Jehovah ummenuhkesuonganoouh, & sasequnonche wadchanuwae ummenuhkesuonk.
28.9 Woi wadchan kummissinninnumog, kah wunnantash kutahtoonk: sohkomoous wonk, kah tahshin micheme.
29.0
29.1 Uninnumohk Jehovah, (woi magassootamogish) uninnumohk Jehovah sohsumoonk kah menuhkesuonk.
29.2 Uninnumohk Jehovah OOwesooongane sohsummooonk; wawussumook Jehovah ut wunnetuppantamooe wunnetuonkanit.
29.3 OOwadtauatonqussuonk Jehovah ohteau woskeche nippekontu; sohsummooe God padaquohhaneteau, Jehovah woskeche mishe nippekontu.
29.4 OOwadtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah mishe menuhkoi, oowadtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah numwohteau mamuttanittooonk.
29.5 OOwadtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah poohquhtahham utchikkuppemusse: nux Jehovah sukquhtahham Lebannone utchikkuppemusse.
29.6 Wonk ukquehquesuhshahtauunash onatuh Calfsut: Lebanon, kah Syrion onatuh wuskunnukqutyeuun.
29.7 OOwadtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah chadchabenum noohtae noohnoounnaash.
29.8 OOwadtauatongqussuonk Jehovah nunnukeahtooomoo touohkomuk: Jehovah nunnukkeohto Kadeshe touohkomuk.
29.9 Oowadtauatongqussuonk Jehovah wunnechahukqunneau attuhquog, kah mukkukiyeuwehtomoo tououkamuk: kah ut weekit nish noh pasuk ooweogquttumun wussohsumowonk
29.10 Jehovah appu tomogkonehtu: nux, Jehovah kehtohsoottumwapoo micheme.
29.11 Jehovah uninnumauau ummissinninneumoh menuhkesuonk, Jehovah pish wunnanumau ummissinninneumoh nashpe wunohteaonk.
30.0
30.1 PIsh kutashinush, woi Jehovah, newutche kutashinnip, kah matta kuttiyeuomp nummatwomog nummushkauantammooonukqunnaout.
30.2 Woi Jehovah num-Manittoom, kummauunnitteanup, kah kenetskehip.
30.3 Woi Jehovah, kutashinomp nukketeahogkou wutch weenohkeet: kuppompomantamwahip woh mat noowomussenat en weenohket.
30.4 Ketoohomohk Jehovah (woi kenau oonetupanatamomoh) kah tabuttantamook, mehquantamog ooneetupanatamooonk.
30.5 Newutche ummusquantamooonk tiohqui; ummonaneteaonkanut keteaonkanyeuoo; mauonk mamiat woh nukqutukqunohteau, qut wekontammooonk pish peomoo nompoaeu.
30.6 Kah wanaeon nussip, matta pish nuttontsapoo micheme.
30.7 Jehovah, nashpe kummonaneteaonk kumminnehteukkompattauunnap noowadchoom: kupputtagkuhhumup kuskesuk, neit nunnooantamup
30.8 Kummauunnittauunup, woi Jehovah: kah en Jehovahut nuttiumup wehquttummooonk.
30.9 Toh unannoohhumoatuonkanyeuoo ut nooshqhunkanit, womusseon en pahsahthekonit? sun pish puppissai koowaeenomuk? sun pish ontuttummoomoo koonomwaonk?
30.10 Nootash, Jehovah, kah monanumeh: Jehovah annunossooweninyeuush en nohhogat.
30.11 Kukquinnuppinnumiip nummauonk en pummukkonat: kutamaunumaiip nummunnootionag, kah kupputtukquobsip miskouanatamooonk:
30.12 Onk woh nussohsumooonk kukkuttoohhumunkqun, kah matta chequnahtanoe. Woi Jehovah numManittoom pish kuttapattantumauush micheme.
31.0
31.1 WOi Jehovah, kuppabuhtanumush, ahque nanukqut akodchitti: pohquahwusseh ut koonomwausseonganit.
31.2 Ehquohtukquaehtah, teanuk pohquohwusseh: menuhke qussukquanyeuush en nuhhogkat, wutche ushpuhhoowaekomuk noowadchanukqunat.
31.3 Newutche ken nukqussukquanum kah noowohkonous: newaje wutche koowesuonk sagkompaneh, kah sampshaseh.
31.4 Kodtinneh wutch hashabput, uttoh keme ponummihetteup: newutche ken nummenuhkesuonk.
31.5 En kenutchaganit nuttohtosoowam nunnashauonk: kuppohquahwussip, woi Jehovah wunnomwae God.
31.6 Nussekeneauomp nag wadtoowontogig pannoowae tahnoocheyeuongash: qut nuppabahtanum Jehovah.
31.7 Pish noowekontam kah nummuskouantam ut kummonaneteaonganit: newutche kenatwontamup nootamehpunaonk: koowaheomp nukketeahogkou ut wuttamehpunaonganit.
31.8 Kah matta kukkuppaheup ut wunnutcheganit matwau: kupponamup nusseetash papahchiyeuut.
31.9 Monanumeh, woi Jehovah, newutche nootamehpunam: nuskesuk mohtupaemoo nashpe neuantamoowonk, nux, nukketeahogkou, kah nunnogkus
31.10 Newutche nukketeaonk sauunumoomoo nashpe neuantamoowonk, kah nukkodtummoomash nashpe mishanomooonk: nummenuhkesuonk sauunumoomoo newutche nummatcheseonk, kah nuskonash mohtupaemooash.
31.11 Nutushpunnamooonkanyeuup kenugke wame nummatwomog, qut nahnaunne kenugke neetatteamunganog, kah noowabesuonkanyeuup en netompaog: naehpaneg ut pukquatchut nooseemwehtuukuppaneg.
31.12 Noowannanummit onatuh nuppooe wosketomp matta mehquanummout: nutogqueneunkqus sukwishquadt.
31.13 Newutche nunnootamup ukkehkomoowaonkannoo monaog, wabesuonk quaqunnipe ohtop, moae kannoonitehettit ayeuuhkone nohhogat, natwontamuppanneg ammanumunnat nukketeaonk.
31.14 Qut kuppabahtanumunup, woi Jehovah: nussip, ken num-Manittoom.
31.15 Nutaquompayeumash ohtaash kenutcheganit: pohquahwusseh wutch wunnutcheganooout nummatwomog, kah wutch nag noswetohhukqueoneg.
31.16 Kuskesuk wossumwahteauush kittinneumut: wadchaneh wutche kummonaneteaonk.
31.17 Ahque akodchitti, woi Jehovah, newutche koowehquttumauunnup: matcheetowog akodjhettich, kah chequnnehhunnaj ut weenohket.
31.18 Pannoowae mussissittoonash chequnnehtositch: uttiyeush pahchuanumooe kah mamanowantamwe mamatcheunoncheg wunnomwaesecheg.
31.19 Woi toh unnukukqun koonetooonk, wadchanumauohp nag quoshukqueaneg, anakosoowehtauohp nag pabahtanumukqueaneg anaquabhittit wosketompaog wunnaumonauh.
31.20 Nag pish kuttadtashoog ut kuskesukque assompamukquodut wutch uppehtuanumooonkanit wosketomp: nag pish keme koowadchanoog ut wetuwomut, wutch ayeuohkosooe menanash.
31.21 Wunanumunaj Jehovah; newutche nunnahtunnukup monchanatamwe oowomoausuonk, ut menuhke otanat.
31.22 Newutche nissip ut noowapantamooonkanit, nuttumuhtahwhut wutch anaquabean: qut onch kenootamup wadtauatongqussue kenanampassumunooonkash, maunnitteauunon.
31.23 Woi wamonoohk Jehovah, wame kenau oonetupanatamoomoh: newutche Jehovah wadchanau pabahtanummuksitcheg, kah mishongquottauoh noh pahtuanumooe ousseet.
31.24 Minnehchantamook, kah noh pish minnehketeau kuttahhou, wame kenau anoonogish Jehovah.
32.0
32.1 WUnnanumau noh uppaneusseonk ahquantosig, kah ummatcheseonk padtagkuhwhosik.
32.2 Wunnanumau missinnin Jehovah matta ogquantamauunk ummatcheseonk, kah wunnahshauonkanit wanne asookekodteamooonkanuuk.
32.3 Matta kodtooon, nuskonash nonukkonukkannupash, nashpe nummauonk quinnikesuk.
32.4 Newutche kesukodtaeu kah nukkonaeu kenutcheg nuttuhkekookongqunap: nuttogkuskesuonk ohsoowemoo en neepune kunkanit. Selah.
32.5 Kussampoowontamauunup nuppaneusseonk, kah matta nupputtoguhhumoop nummatcheseonk: nussip, nussampooam nummatcheseongash Jehovahut; neit kutahquantamaiip uhquenunkque nummatcheseonk. Selah.
32.6 Newutche yeu, nish noh wunneetupanatamwenin pish kuppeantamunk, uttoh woh adtooche namehhunumuk: wunnamuhkut mishittomogkog matta pish uppasoosukauouh.
32.7 Ken nuttassampamukquodtoom, pish koowadchaneh wutch wuttamehpunaonkanit: pish koowenuhkah nashpe pohquahwunnittue ketoohomaongash. Selah.
32.8 Pish koowohtamwahush, kah kukkuhkootumauush ut mayut uttoh woh aoan: pish kussampshanush nashpe nuskesuk.
32.9 Ahque ogqueneunkqussek horsesut, asuh muleut matta ohtoookig wohwohtamooonk: wuttoonoo mos kashpussik nashpe bridle bit, ishkont, kuppasoosukkongquog.
32.10 Monatash uhkpunnaonkash pish wunnuhkuhkonkqunnau matchetowog: qut noh pabahtanumont Jehovah, monaneteaonk pish weenuhkunk.
32.11 Weekontamook Jehovahut, kah muskouantamook kenau sampweseogish: kah weekontamoe mishontoowag, wame sampwutteahheoogish.
33.1 MUskouanatamook Jehovahut, woi sampweseogish: tabattantamowonk oonekonkqunau sampwesitcheg.
33.2 Waenomoohk Jehovah nashpe harp: ketoohomohk nashpe psaltery, kah piogpepemunnohtonooe wohwunnonttoowohkodtomuk.
33.3 Ketoohamohk wuske ketoohomaonk: mishontoowae wunnuppuhpequagk.
33.4 Newutche wuttinnowaonk Jehovah sampwi: kah wame wutanakausuongash wunnamuhkuteyeuooash.
33.5 Womantam sampweusseonk, kah wussittamooonk: ohke numwohtau ummonaneteaonk Jehovah.
33.6 Nashpe wuttinnoowaonk Jehovah kesukquash kesehtauunapash, kah wame {kesukque} ahhontannooonk nashpe wuttoone nashauonk.
33.7 Muhmonum kehtohhane nippeash, onatuh kottonkquag: poonum moonoi momatchiyeukomukqut.
33.8 Wame ohke qushonch Jehovah: wame neg wadohkitcheg muttaohket wapissoowonahhittitch.
33.9 Newutche kuttoop, kah unniyeup: annoohteamoop kah menuhtikkompatop.
33.10 Jehovah moteaqunnehto ukkenoonittooonkannoo penoowahteaog: tohnoocheyeuweto wunnatwontammooonkannoowoash missinninuog.
33.11 Ukkenoosoowaonk Jehovah michemkompatteau wuttahhe unnantamooonkash en wame pometuonkanash.
33.12 Wunnantamun wutahtimoin wa-Manittoomut Jehovah: kah missinninnuh neh pepenauuhpoh wutche nehenwonche ootohtoonganinnuh.
33.13 Jehovah womompu wutche kesukqut, nauwau wame wunnaumonaoh wosketompaog.
33.14 Wutch menuhke wuttiyeuonkanit moninnauwau wame wadohkinutcheh ohket.
33.15 Wuttahhoowooh wuttatuppe kekkenawunumunash . natwontam wame wuttanakosooonkannoowoash.
33.16 Matta howae kehtahsoot wadchonoun nashpe mishe ohhuntannooonk: menuhkesoowenin matta pohquohwunnukkoo mishe menuhkesooonk.
33.17 Horsis tahnoocheyeuoo wutche wadchanittuonk: kah matta pish pohquahwunnuwooo nashpe ummishe menuhkesooonk.
33.18 Kusseh, wuskesuk Jehovah nannaompamau neh quoshhukqutcheh: neg anoositcheg ut ummonaneteaonganit:
33.19 Pohquohwunonat ukketeahogkonoouh wutch nuppooonkanit, kah nag pomantamwahonat mohshogquodut.
33.20 Nukketeahogkonun pahtissoowanau Jehovah: noh nuttanummonteaonkanun, & nuttogqunnekonun.
33.21 Newutche nuttahhun pish ooweekontamooonoh: newutche nuppabahtantamumunonup ooneetuparatamwe wesuonk.
33.22 Kummonaneteaonk, woi Jehovah, nuhkuhkongqutteuh: neane annoonunog.
34.0
34.1 Pish noonanum Jehovah nishnoh ohquompiyeuut: noh wawenomaonk pish naqutteahteau nuttoonit.
34.2 Nukketeahogkou pish miskowau Jehovahut: ohhohpacheg pish wuttunuhtamunau, kah pish wekontamog.
34.3 Woi mishehuk Jehovah weeche neen, kah moeu tahshinnumuttuh oowesuonk.
34.4 Nunnanompassumomp Jehovah, kah nunnootunkup: kah nuppohquohwhunukup wutch wame noowabesuongash.
34.5 Ummoninnauoopoh kah oowequaiyeumoopaneg: kah wuskesukkoowoash matta ogkodchumunnoopash.
34.6 Yeuoh kuttummunge wosketomp mauoop, kah Jehovah wunnootaopoh; onk uppohquohwhunopoh wutch wame ootamehpunnaongash.
34.7 Wut-angeloom Jehovah oowenuhkauuh nah quahshukqutcheh, kah uppohquohwhunnuh.
34.8 Woi qutchehtamook kah naumook Jehovah wunneetou: wunnanumau wosketomp noh pabahtanumont.
34.9 Woi qusheuk Jehovah kenau oonetupanatamoomoh: newutche nag quoshoncheg matta teag quenawehukkooog
34.10 Qunnonoowesog quenauwehukquog, kah pashkonnontamwog: qut nag natinneawhoncheg Jehovah, mat pish quenahukkooog ne teag wanegik.
34.11 Peyonk kenau peissesog, nootiegk, kukkuhkootomauunumwoo qushaonk Jehovah.
34.12 Howan noh kodtantog pomantomooonk, & womantog sepepomantamunat woh wunnaumunat wanegik?
34.13 Nanawehtauush kenan wutch matchitit, kah kussissittoonash eyeumunoohkitch asookekodteamoowonk.
34.14 Amaehtash machuhk, & wunneussish: natinneahash wunnohteaonk, kah asuhkash.
34.15 Wuskesukquash Jehovah nanaompamau sampweseaeninneuh: kah wehtauogash woshwohtaash en ummauonganooout.
34.16 Wuskesuk Jehovah wuttayeuohkonukqunneau matchesenutcheh; tummmehthamunat mehquanumaonkanoo wutch ohkeit.
34.17 Sampwesecheg mauog, kah Jehovah nootam; kah uppohquohwhunuh wutch wame ootamehpunnaonkanoowoash.
34.18 Jehovah uppasoosukauuh pohquetahhonitcheh: kah oowadchanuh nah ohhohpae nahshauonkanitcheg.
34.19 Monatash ootammehpunnaongash sampweseaenin: qut Jehovah uppohquowhunuh nish wutch wame.
34.20 Nanawehteau wame wushkonash: matta pasuk poohkshaunnoo.
34.21 Machuk pish wunnushukqun noh matchetuk: kah nag sekeneauoncheg noh sampweset pish konkewoiyeuooog.
34.22 Jehovah pohquohwhunau ukketeahogkounnoouh wuttinnumoh: kah nag pabahtanumoncheh, matta pish pasuk konkewoiyeuoo.
35.0
35.1 KEnootamwansheh, woi Jehovah, ayeuuhkone nag mekausitcheg: ayeukaus nag ayeuuhkonukqueoneg.
35.2 Neemunush ogqunneg kah musonkoo, kah neepaush wutche nuttanumonteaonk.
35.3 Kodtunush wonk konnukuhtohwheg, kah kuppohhash {may} ayeuuhkone nooswetohhukqueoneg: us nukketeahogkou, neen koowadchanitteaonk.
35.4 Nag chepshanunnaj kah akodchhennaj natineahwhoncheg nukketeahogkou: nag qushkeahhunnaj kah chephunnaj natwontogig noowoskhitteaonk.
35.5 Ogqunneungqussehettitch wossodteamunit tooantog waban: kah wut-angeloom Jehovah wunnomatoohkauonch.
35.6 Ummayeu pohkunnaj kah toonukquaj, & wut-angeloom Jehovah nooswehtahwhonch.
35.7 Newutche matta unnomaiyeue ut pasahtheganit nupponahshaponkuppanneg, ne matta unnomaiyeue wonnahteahhitteup wutche nukketeahogkou.
35.8 Paguanuonk nuhkuhkongqutch asq wahteoookup, kah wuttahshapoh ne wanahshahhitteupoh puttuhukquitch: ne piuhsuke ushpunnaonk nagum ushpunnaj.
35.9 Kah nukketeahogkou pish weekontam Jehovahut: pish muskouantam ut oowadchanoowaonganit.
35.10 Wame nuskonash pish unnoowomooash Jehovah, howan anunkquean, pohquohwhunont matcheku noh wutch anuwunuhkesumukqutcheh, nux matcheku kah quenawehukqut noh wutch waskhukqutcheh.
35.11 Pannoowae wawaeninyeuog waapoopaneg; noochumukuppaneg nish matta wahteauoouhpanish.
35.12 Nuttunkquattunkuppanneg machuhk wutch wanegik, en woskeheonat nukketeahogkou.
35.13 Qut neen, mahchenahhettit nuthogkup munnootionag: mat meetsue nuttohhohpahheomp nukketeahogkou, & nuppeantamoowonk qushkemoop en nehenwonche nuppoochenauonut.
35.14 Nutogque pomushop neane en netompaut, kah nematut: nunnooantamooe nauogkompop, onatuh maemont okasoh.
35.15 Qut onkapunaon weekontamuppaneg, kah muhmooopaneg: nux, matchetooog muhmooopaneg nutayeuuhkonukqunaout, kah matta noowahteauoounnap; nunnehnekshanukuppaneg, kah matta ahquepaneg.
35.16 Weeche eiantukoiyeue momonuhtuhsuenuog ut ummishadtupyooonkanoowout, nutchuhchuhquanehtunkuppanneg.
35.17 Jehovah, tohsohke pish kunnonamun? quehchuwus nukketeahogkou wutch oowoskhuaonganoo, neanadchanog wutch qunnonoout.
35.18 Kuttabuttantamauush ut mishe mukkinneonganit: koowaenomush, kenugke monaog missinninnuog.
35.19 Ahque pannoowae nummatwomog, muskauantammoooshettitch: kah ahque kehkehteukquaehtoadtehettich, tohnooche sekeniitcheg.
35.20 Newutche matta unnoowooowog wunnohteaonk, qut natwontamwog asookekodteamooe kuttooonkash ayeuuhkone nah manunniunitcheh ut ohkeit.
35.21 Nux, nuttayeuhkone mishshittoonaehtunkuppaneg, unnoowopanneg, Aha, aha, nuskesukqun wnnnamunnap.
35.22 Yeu kenaumunap, woi Jehovah, ahque chequnapish: woi Jehovah, ahque naoosukah.
35.23 Mamonchish, kah toohkish en noosummitteaonkanit, nux en nuppissaumatuonganit num-Manittoom kah nut-Jehovahoom.
35.24 Wussumeh, woi Jehovah, num-Manittoom, neaunag koonomwausseonk, kah ahque nag muskouantamwoshettich.
35.25 Ahque unnoowahettich wuttahhoowout, Aha, ne kodtantamogup: ahque unnoowahettich nummahche mishasqunnean.
35.26 Akodchhettich kah moeu chephunnaj mashkouwantamoowontogig noowoskhetteaonk: hogquehettich akodchuonk kah mishshananittuonk mashehhonche wuhhogkauh ayeuuhkone nuhhog.
35.27 Mishontoowae wekontamohettich, muskouantammohettich tapeneogig nussampweusseonk, nux nagwutteaeu noowahettich, mishehhunnaj Jehovah, noh wekontamoowontog ooneunniyeuonk wuttinnumoh.
35.28 Kah nenan pish weogquttummoomoo koonomwausseonk, kah koowowenomitteaonk neteagu.
36.0
36.1 UMmatcheseonk matchetoo unnoowomoo unnome nuttahhut, qushaonk God wanne ohtanoo anaquohtag wuskesukquash.
36.2 Newutche waechumau wuhhogkuh ut nehenwonche wuskesukqut, napajeh ummatcheseonk unnummiskomun jishanumukquodt
36.3 Wuttoone kuttoowonkash matchetooonkanuooash & asookekodteamooonkanuash: mahche nukkodtum waantamunnat, kah wunneussenat.
36.4 Natwontam woskehuwaonk ut wutappinneat, ponau wuhhogkuh matta wanegenunoog may; matta jishantamoo machuhk.
36.5 Kummonaneteaonk, woi Jehovah, kesukqut ohteau; kah koonummuhkutteyeuonk en matokqsut.
36.6 Kussampweusseonk ogqueneunkquodt mogkodchuut; koosittumoowongash mishe moonoiyeuash: woi Jehovah, koowadchan wosketomp kah puppinashim.
36.7 Toh unnukkukque wunnegen koowomoausue monaneteaonk, woi God! yowutche wunneechanoowooh wosketompaog pabahtantamwog agwe kenuppawhunne onkkauuhtaut.
36.8 Pish moocheke tapippooog nashpe keke wunnogooonk: kah pish kootattamheoog kussepue weekontamoowongash.
36.9 Newutche koowechiyeumukqun pomantamoe tohkekom: kooweequaioumut pish nuttut naumunnan wequai.
36.10 Woi nagwutteanumau koowomoausuonk neg wahikqueaneg; kah koonomwausseonk en neg sampwutteaheoncheg.
36.11 Ahque pittuanumwe musseet ayeuuhkositch, kah ahque wunnutcheg matchetoo ontsaphukquttai.
36.12 Anakausitcheg matcheseonk ne wuttit penushoneau: kepuhkonoog, kah matta pish tapenumooog omohkenat.
37.0
37.1 MOOshquehhuhkon kuhhog papaume matchesecheg, kah ahque iskaaus anakausitcheg matcheseonk.
37.2 Newutche pish teanuk tummehtahwhoog onatuh moskehtuut, kah pish uppoopassuog onatuh oskosqut.
37.3 Pabahtanum Jehovah, & wunnesish, neit pish kootohkin ohkeit, kah wunnamuhkut pish kussohkommoonit.
37.4 Tapeh kuhhog wonk Jehovahut, kah pish kittinninnumunk kuttahhe kodtantammooonkash.
37.5 Ahtahsoowash kummay Jehovahut: wonk pabahtanum, kah nagum pish wuttissen.
37.6 Onk pish wussuhwhuttauun koonomwauseonk neane wequai, kah koosittumooonk onatuh puhshaquodt.
37.7 Anwohsinooous Jehovah, menuhke pahtissoowos: mushquehhuhkon kuhhog newutche noh wanuhkommiadt ut ummayut, newutche wosketomp noh pakodchehtunk matche natwontomooonkash.
37.8 Netahhe musquantash, kah nukkodush kussop-moshquantammooonk: tohen moshquehhukkon kuhhog matcheussenat.
37.9 Newutche matchesecheg pish tummehtahwoog: qut pahtissoowonnoncheg Jehovah, pish wutahtauuneau ohke.
37.10 Newutche majish oggusohquompi, kah matchetoo pish ahquapu, nux, menuhke pish kenatwontam wutayeuonk, kah pish wanne ohtano.
37.11 Qut manunnissitcheg pish wutahtauuneau ohke: kah pish tapeneauwahheoog wohhogauh ut monahk wunnohteaonk.
37.12 Matchetoo wunnahsoowau ayeuohkone sampwesunnitcheh, kah wutchuhchuhquanehtauuh.
37.13 Jehovah pish wutahanehtauuh, newutche wunnaumun ukkesukodtum peyaumoo.
37.14 Matchetooog mahche kodtunumwog togkodteg, kah onchippinnahteaog penohkonat matcheku, kah quanauwehukquit, kah nushonat sampwe pomantamunnitcheh.
37.15 Wuttogkodteganoo pish pechemoo nehenwonche wuttahhoowout, wutahtompeyeuuh pish puhkqunnosooash.
37.16 Oggusin ne sampweseaenin ahtunk, anoohkommoomoo oowenawetuonkannoo monaog matchetooog.
37.17 Newutche wohpittenoowoash matchetooog pish pohkqunnosuash: qut Jehovah qukqununau wunnomwausseaenuh.
37.18 Jehovah wahteau ukkesukodtumoowoash sampwesenutche: kah wuttahtoonkanoo pish michemohteau.
37.19 Matta pish akodchuog ut matche ohquompiyeuut: kah ut mashogque kesukodash pish wamepooog.
37.20 Qut matchetooog pish onkuppunnaog, kah ummatwomoh Jehovah pish onattuhyeuog oowesoo Lambsog, nag pish mohtupaeog: pish pukutae mohtupaeog.
37.21 Matchetoo nogohkou qut matta wonk nompenummoo: qut wunnomwausseaenin, monaneteau, kah magoo.
37.22 Newutche neh wunanumonche pish wutohtauneau ohke: qut nag matchenanumoncheh pish tummehtahwhoog.
37.23 Wutontunehtuongash wunneetooomp ummenuhke wunnohtauunash Jehovah: kah noh wuttapinneamun ummay.
37.24 Tokonogque penushont, matta pish papequane punnuhkon: newutche Jehovah ukqukqunnunuh nashpe wunnutcheg.
37.25 Nooskenneuoop, kah yeuyeu nukkuhchiyeu: qut asq nunnawoh sampwesoo nukkonnou, asuh ooskannemunneoh oowowenuhshonau puttukquinneg.
37.26 Micheme monaneteau, kah nogkohkauwehhuwau: kah ooskannemuneoh wunnanummoog.
37.27 Amaehtash machuhk, kah wunnesish: & michemiish.
37.28 Newutche Jehovah womantam wussuttummooonk, kah matta nukkonau oonetuppantammoomoh, nag micheme wadchannoog: qut ooskanumunnuuh matchetooog pish tummehtahwhoog.
37.29 Sampwesitcheg pish wuttahtauunneau ohke, kah na pish ootahkenau micheme.
37.30 Wuttoon sampwesooenin yeumoo waantammooonk; kah wenan weogquttummoomoo wussuttummooonk.
37.31 Wuttinnaumatuonk ummanittoomoh ohteau wuttahhut, matta pasuk wuttontanehtuonk pish toonukquishau.
37.32 Matchetoo ashkuhwhau sampwesoowenin, kah ukkodtinneanuh.
37.33 Jehovah matta pish wunnukkonuh ut wunnutcheganit, asuh uppogkodchumuh wussumut.
37.34 Pahtissoowos Jehovah, kah muttumash ummay, kah pish kuttahshunuk ohtauunat ohke: matchetooog tummehtahwhut, pish kenaumun.
37.35 Nunnauomp matchetoo ut mishe menehkesuonkanit, kah penaekit onatuh askuhquamut ne nehenwonchekeg.
37.36 Qut onch ammaoop, kah kusseh matta appoop; nux, nunnatinneahwhop, qut nooninnunkquatup nameheonat.
37.37 Kuhkinneasish panuppe yeuenin, kah moninneau s[o]mpwesit: newutche oowohkukquosunnooonk noh wosketomp wunnohteaonganyeuoo.
37.38 Qut matcheussecheg pish moeu paquanoog, oowohkukquohsunnooonganoo matchetooog pish tummehtahhamun.
37.39 Qut wadchanaonkanoo sampwesitcheg wutchiyeumoo Jehovahut, noh nag ummenuhkesuonganoo ut wuttamehpunae ahquompiyeuut.
37.40 Kah Jehovah pish wuttanumauuh, kah uppohquohwhunnuh: pish uppohquohwhunnuh wutch matchetoout, kah oowadchanuh newutche uppabahtanumukquoh.
38.0
38.1 WOi Jehovah ahque auskome ut kummooshquantamooonganit: kah ahque sasamuhkuhwheh ut kussopetae kummooshquantamooonganit.
38.2 Newutche kukkouhquatumash sontikkompattaash nuhhogkat, kah kunnutcheg nuttuhque kenukquohkonkqun.
38.3 Wanne pasquanooonkanunoo nooweyauussut, newutche kummooshquantummooonk: kah wanne anwosinnoonganunnoo nuskonut, newutche nummatcheusseonk.
38.4 Newutche nummatcheusseongash anuwushshomooash nuppuhkuhk: onatuh tahkequog weanun wussaume tuhkequanuash wutche neen.
38.5 Nuttanhikash matchummunkquatash kah annitash: newutche nutasootuonk.
38.6 Nunnooehpunnanit, kah nummishe nauwanit; nummaue pomusham mamusse kesukod.
38.7 Newutche nusseganohtogquash numwohtosooash nashpe nehchepunaonk: kah wanne pasquannooonkanunnoo ut nooweyauussut.
38.8 Nunnoochumwehit kah nuttuhque sukquhkont: nummushohposup newutche nuttahhe wuttammantamoongash.
38.9 Lord, wame nukkodtantamooonk ohteau anaquabean: kah nutauwohkontoowaonk matta attahtosunoo wutch kuhhogkat.
38.10 Nuttah tehtequshshin, nummunnuhkesuonk nunukkonuk: kah nuskesukque wequai wonk nuttamehtunkqun.
38.11 Womonukqueoneg kah netompaog noukkompouog wutch nukkechesuonganit: kah anunkumogig nuppehchohkunkquog.
38.12 Nag wonk kodtinneanukqueoneg, nuppoonumunkquog ahpehpanoh: kah nag kodwoskehhukqueoneg, unnoowaog wohwoskehhuwomooukish & natwontamwog asookekodteamooongash nehteagu.
38.13 Qut nen, onatuh kakobsaenin matta nunnootamoop; kah nuttogquinneunkquissip matta kakuttook, noh matta woshwunnummook wuttoon.
38.14 Nemehkuh neaninneunkquissip mat nootammooenin, kah noh wuttoonut wanne auskomoowaonkanunook.
38.15 Newutche, woi Jehovah, kuttannoonsh: pish kenootam, woi Jehovah num-Manitoom.
38.16 Newutche nissip, nootah, ishkont nummushkouantamooonukquog: nusseet toonukqushik, nag mishshehheaog wuhhogkauh ayeuuhkone nuhhogkat.
38.17 Newutche nahen nukkehkeskwhisham, kah nunnooantamooonk naquahteahteau anaquabeh.
38.18 Newutche pish nuttontutum nummatcheusseonk; pish nunnooantam wutche nuppaneusseonk.
38.19 Qut nummatwomog kogkuttametuog, kah menukkesooog: kah nag tohnooche sekinneunkqueoneg monok.
38.20 Nag wonk onquatausitcheg machuhk wutche wanekuk, nutayeuohkonukquog: newutche nuttahsukkom ne wanegik.
38.21 Ahque nukkahseh, woi Jehovah: Woi num-Manittoom ahque nooosuhkah.
38.22 Kunnipish wutche nuttanumonteaonk, woi Jehovah, noowadchanitteaonk.
39.0
39.1 NIssip, pish nunnunukquissooontamunash nummayash, onk woh matta nummatchesu nashpe neenan: pish nunnanaehteoh nuttoon nashpe bridle, matcheetoo apbit anaquabeh.
39.2 Nutchequnnapooe matta kuttoop nukkehchuttahhomp wutch wanegik, kah nunnuantamooonk wogkouunnosoop.
39.3 Nuttah kussopputtop ut nuttunnomiyeumut, natwontamon nootau chikohtop: neit nukkeketookomp nashpe neenan.
39.4 Jehovah wahtouwahheh noowohkuhquoioom, kah uttoh sahchak nukkesukkodumask: onk woh noowahteo toh nuttine tiohquohquompunnam.
39.5 Kusseh, kuttogquehteoh nukkesukkodumash munnitcheg ne anukkuhque kushkag, kah nuttunukkuhquiyeuonk wanne teag ut anaquabean: wunnummuhkut nishnoh wosketomp, kasnehkesitcheh, panuppe tohnoocheyeuoo. Selah.
39.6 Wunnamuhkut nish noh wosketomp pomushau tahnooche unnompammukquissooonkanit: wunnamuhkut nag tahnooche wuttamantamwog: numwonkquottou weenauweetuonganash, kah matta wahteooo howane pish nash muhmounuk.
39.7 Kah yeuyeu Jehovah, teaguas nuppahtissoowontom? ken kuttannoonsh.
39.8 Pohquahwusseh wutch wame nummatcheseonganash, ahque ayeueh wutuspunamooonganoo asookutcheg.
39.9 Mat nukkaketoop, mat noowaoshwunnumop nuttoon; newutche kutussenap.
39.10 Amaunumah kuttogkommuwaonk: nummohchikonaim nashpe wuttogkomuaonk kenutcheg.
39.11 Auskomue sasamatahwadcheh wosketomp wutche ummatcheseonk, kummahchumwehtoh ooneetuonk onatuh mothut: wunnamuhkut nish noh wosketomp tahnoocheyeuoo. Selah.
39.12 Nootash nuppeantamoowonk, woi Jehovah, kah ahchusuttash nummauonk, ahque chequnapsh en nussuppequonut, newutche nuppenoowohteau ut anaquabean, kah nunnohkontamaeninnu neane wame nooshunnonog.
39.13 Woi ahkqheh onk woh nuttompontnehkes, asquam mamoncheon, kah aohquabeon.
40.0
40.1 Nuppompahheop Jehovah, kah nukkeihketunkup kah nootamup nummauonk.
40.2 Kah nukkuhkuhkoounukup wutch uhqueneungquotte pohsahtheganit, wutch wunnumwehchuae manonskut, kah ponumup nusseetash qussukquanit, kah menuhketeop nuppomushaongash.
40.3 Kah ponumup wuske unnoohomaonk nuttoonut waenomuwaonk en num-Manittoomunnonut: monaog pish wunnaumunneau, kah pish wabosuog, kah pish pabahtanumaog Jehovah.
40.4 Wunnanumon wosketomp noh nagwutteaeu pabahtanumont Jehovah: kah matta tohhentupanumonk pahtuannumwunitcheh, asuh yeuhoh quashkenutcheh en pannoowaeyeuonganehtu.
40.5 Monatash, woi Jehovah num-Manittoom, kummuhchanatamwe anakausuongash nish kesehtauohpash, kah kittinnanummuwonganunonash, matta woh koonogketammonteaunash: tohneit kod pohquttumon kah weogquttumon, nash wussaume monatash, matta woh waaketamunash.
40.6 Sephausuonk kah magooonk, matta kukkodtantammoop, nehtauogash kuppohquanumup: chikohtae-magooonk, kah matchuesseonkane Sephausuonk matta kookoowehquttumoop.
40.7 Neit nussip, Kusseh, nuppeom: koosuhquawhonganit tannussuhquahwhosoo papaume nen:
40.8 Noowekontam ussenat kuttinantamooonk, Woi num-Manittoom; nux kuttinnomatuonk ohteau unnome nuttahhut.
40.9 Nukkuhkootumwehteap Sampweusseonk ut mishe mukkinneonganit: kusseh, matta nutchequnnohtop nussustoonash, woi Jehovah, koowahteo.
40.10 Matta nuttattahtooop koonomwausseonk unnome nuttahhut, nuppahquttumup kuppahpahtanumukquissooonk, & koowatchanoowaonk: matta nupputtogkuhhumoop kummishe wamoahsooonk, kah koonomwayeuonk, wutch mishe mukkinneonkanut.
40.11 Kuppohhommiehkon kukkuttummonteanitteaonkash, woi Jehovah: kukkogkuttame wamoahsooonk, kah koonomwaeyeuonk naquahteae wotchanukquttuh.
40.12 Newutche woh mo tapaketamoomukish machuhkish noowenuhkunkup, nummatcheseonkash nuttahqunnukqunnapash, newaje matta nuttapunnummoo uspuhquaenat: nash anue monatash onk nuppuhkuhquash, newutche nuttah sauunnumoomoo.
40.13 Wekontash, Woi Jehovah, kuppahquahwussinnat: Woi Jehovah, kinnipish kuttanumiunnat.
40.14 Nag moae ogkodchhittich, kah chepshahhittitch, natinneahwhoncheg nukketeahogkou, oowoskehhonaout: nag ohsaoohkauunnaj, kah ogkodchhunnaj matcheunnanumukqueoneg.
40.15 Nag kokewoiyeuhittitch onkquattontamunnat wuttogkodchuonkannoo, annukqueoneg, aha, aha!
40.16 Wame nag natinneahhukqueaneg wekontamwehhittitch kah mishkouantamwehhittich ut kohhogat: nag wammontogig koowatchanuwaonk, naquahteae unnoowahhittitch, Jehovah mishshehhonnaj.
40.17 Qut nen nummatchek kah nukquenawehhuk, onch Jehovah nummehquanumuk; ken nuttanummonteaonk kah nuppohquahsooaeninneum; ahque putchunnoowoish, woi num-Manittoom.
41.0
41.1 Wunnannumou noh tahtuppanumont matchekooah; Jehovah pish uppohquohwunnuh, wuttamehpunnae ohquompiyeuut.
41.2 Jehovah pish oowatchonuh, pish uppomantamwaheuh kah noh pish wunnanumou ut Ohkeit; & matta pish kuppoonoh wuttinnantamooonkannoowout ummatwomoh.
41.3 Jehovah pish ummenuhkeheuh ut ummahchukannae appinneat: pish koonaskunum wame wuttapin mahchenadt.
41.4 Nissip, Jehovah, monanumeh; neetskeh nukketeahogkou, newutche kummatcheunnehhunup.
41.5 Nummatwomog nummatcheunnukquog: Toh ohquompi pish nup, kah oowesooonk nuppoomoo?
41.6 Kah nattauwahhit, unnoowau tohnoocheyeuuk: wuttah mukkunum matchittooonk nehenwonche en, ootohkont, wuttontuttumun.
41.7 Wame sekinniitcheg nummoeu kemoowaonukquog: nuttiyeuohkone natwontommunkquog noowoskhitteaonk.
41.8 {Unnoowaog}, matchepunnaonk menuhkohteau wohhogat; kah yeuyeu noh sapsuk, pish matta wonk omohkeu.
41.9 Nux, nehenwonche nannauanittoue netomp, noh pabahtanumogup, noh machuhp nupputtukquinneg, nukkenogquannaehtunkup.
41.10 Qut ken, Woi Jehovah, monanumeh, & omohkinneh, onk woh nuttunkquattauoog.
41.11 Yeu nashpe noowaehteauun koosikkittahaose; newutche nummatwom matta nummushkouantammooonukooh.
41.12 Qut nen, kuttahshinneh ut nuppanupwuttahhaonkanit: kah kuppooneh anaquapean micheme.
41.13 Wunnanumou Jehovah ummannittoomoh Israel, Wutch michemeyeuonkanit, en michemeyeuonkanit. Amen, kah Amen.
42.0
42.1 Neane iump nahnakiae kottantog sepoopagquash; nukketeahogkou ne kuttinne nahnakiae kottanumukqun, woi God.
42.2 Nuketeahogkou kuhkuttoon wutche God, pumantamwae God: toh ohquompi pish nuppeom, kah nunnoquis anaquabit God?
42.3 Nussipequonash noomechumminneapash kesukodae & nuhkonae, ne naquahteae ashittit, Tonoh kummanittoom?
42.4 Yeush mequantamon, nussookun nukketeahogkou ut nuttunnomiyeumut; newutche noowuhwowechaomp monacheg, noowechaopaneg en wekut God; nashpe mushkouantamooe kah waenomoowae wuttauohtunkquissooonk, weche monacheg nag nanawehtoguppaneg wunnetupantamwe Kesuk.
42.5 Tohwaje penuhkonitteaan, woi nukketeakogkou? kah tohwaje wuttamantaman ut nuttunnomiyeumut? Annoosish Godut, newutche pish aspume noowawenom, wutche wuskesukkooe anunnosooonk.
42.6 Woi num-Manittoom, nukketeahogkou punnuhkon ut nuttunnomiyeumut: newutche pish koowaanumish wutch Jordane, kah Hermonite ohkeit, kah wutch wadchuut Mizar.
42.7 Moonoi konummoomoo en moonoiyeuut ne kodtoomoouk sookemooe kunnippeum: wame kuttukkoomog, & kukkuhtonttukumog nuppaumuhkunkquog.
42.8 Qut Jehovah pish annootam wammoahsooe ummonaneteaonk kesukkodtae, & nuhkonae wuttunnoohomaonk pish noowetomuk, kah nuppeuhtammooonk en pomantamwae nummannittoom.
42.9 Pish nuttun God nukqussukquanum, Tohwaje wannanumean? tohwaje mauwe pummushshaon nashpe wuttuhquanummehhoowaonk Matwau?
42.10 Neane nashpe togketteg ut nushkonut, nummatwomog nukkehkomukquog; ne asekesukkohkish ashittit, Tonoh kummannittoom?
42.11 Tohwaje penuhkonitteaan woi nukketeahogkou? kah tohwaje wuttamantaman ut nuttunnomiyeumut? Anoosish Godut, newutche pish aspume noowauwenom, noh pamontamwahtunk nittinsooonk, kah wamannittoomeon.
43.1 WUssummeh, woi God, kah kenoottamwannisheh, aiyeuohkone matchetooe wuttahtimoin; Woi pohquahwusseh wutch ahsookohkodteae kah matta Sampwesooweninyeuut
43.2 Newutche Ken nummenuhkesooe Mannittoom, tohwaje ammauhkosean? tohwaje mauwe pomushaon nashpe wuttuhquanumwehhuwaonk matwau?
43.3 Woi annootash koowequaiyeum, kah koonomwaonk; nag sagkompagunehhittitch, passoowehhittitch en koonetuppantamwe wadchuut, kah en Kekash.
43.4 Neit pish nuttom wuttalteroomut God, en Godut nummishe wekontammooonk: nux, Harput pish koowauenomush, woi Manit, num-Manittoom.
43.5 Tohwaje penuhkonitteaan woi nukketeahogkou? kah tohwaje wuttamantaman ut nuttinnomiyeumut? Anoosish Godut, newutche pish aspume noowauwenom, noh pamontamwahtunk nittinsooonk, kah wamanittoomeon.
44.0
44.1 NUnnootamunnonap nashpe nehtauogunnonash, woi God, noohshunnonog nuttukqunnanonup; toh unannuhkoseas nag ut ukkesukkodtummooout, ut nowat ohquompiyeuash.
44.2 Toh ane suhhoohkouohp Penoowahteaog nashpe kunnitcheg, kah kuttahkehkonopaneg; toh ane uhkuppunnanohp missinninyeuog, kah suhwhuhkonohp.
44.3 Newutche matta ootahtoonkanenaop ohke nashpe nehenwonche wuttogkatekonnoo, kah nehhenwonche wehpittenoo matta wotchannukkoopaneg: qut kuttinuhkou kah kehpit, kah wequaiyeue kuttinnissooonk, newutche koosikkittaanumopaneg.
44.4 Ken nuk-Kehtahsoottumoom, woi God, annoohteamush pohquahwunnittooonkash wutche Jacob.
44.5 Nashpe ken pish nukkepuppissumun nummatwomunnonog; nashpe koowesooonk pish nuttahtaskuhkouononog nag ayeuohkone waapehtunkqueakeg.
44.6 Newutche matta pish nuppahpahtanatam nuttahtomp, asuh Nuttogkodteg matta pish noowatchonukkoo.
44.7 Qut Ken koowadchanumunnonup wutch nummatwomunnonut, kah kuttogkodchehhopaneg, nag sekinneunkqueogup.
44.8 Godut noowawenowamun mamusse kesukkod; kah noowawenotumumun koowesooonk micheme. Selah.
44.9 Qut kuppogkesumun, kah kuttogkodchehhumun; kah matta kooweche suhhommooh nuttahhontannooonkanunnonog.
44.10 Kukquishkeahhumun wutch matwaut: kah sekinnunkqueakig mukkookinnauwanushshaog nehhenwonche wohhogauh.
44.11 Kummagooosumunnonup neane Sheepsog woh mohhut: kah kussewhahumunnonup kunnukke penoowohteaut.
44.12 Kummog kummissinninyeumog wutche mo teag, kah matta kukkootenaetu nashpe neanoatehtit.
44.13 Kuttishpunnammmoowahimun en netateamonkanunnonut, meshannanittooonk, kah aionttuhkonittooonk en wame wenuhkkonkqueakig.
44.14 Kut-ontoowaonkannuwahhimun kunnukke penoowohteaog, nunnukukquashaonk kunnukke missininuog.
44.15 Nutchepshaanumooonk naquahteahteau anuhquabeh, kah nuskesukque ogkodchuonk nunnuhkuhkonk.
44.16 Newutche oowattauohtunkquissooonk noh ashpunnamooadt, kah mamatcheuttog; newutche matwau kah annootaenin.
44.17 Wame yeu nunnuhkuhkunkqunan; onch matta koowannannumunoomunnonup, asuh matta nuppannoowae ussemunnonup ut koonoowaonkanut.
44.18 Nuttahhun matta quishkemunnoop, asuh nuttontannehtuonkanunonash matta paneomunnoopash wutch kummayut.
44.19 Tokonogque kuttuhque poohqusshahsumunnonup ut wuttahtuout Dragonsog, kah kupputtogkuhhimunnonup wutonkauohtom Nuppooonk.
44.20 Wannantamogus Owesooonk num-Manitoomun, asuh uspunumauogus nunnitchekanun penoowe manit:
44.21 Sunummatta pish God yeu wunnattinnahhomun? newutche wahteau ukkemeyeumash muttah.
44.22 Nux wutche ken nunnishitchamun qunnekesukod; nuttagquanummitteamun onatuh Sheepsog woh nashitcheg.
44.23 Toohkish, tohwaje kauean, woi Jehovah? omohkish, ahque pogkesinnean micheme.
44.24 Tohwaje puttoghuman kuskesuk kah wannantaman nuttonkapunnaonkannun, kah nutonkquanumwehhitteaonkanun?
44.25 Newutche nukketeahogkonun nauanosu en puppisiyeuut; nunnogseun muhsogquemoo ohkehkontu
44.26 Omohkish wutche nuttanumonteaonkanun, kah pohquohwussinnean wutche kummonaneteaonk.
45.0
45.1 NUttah monchukkameteau wanegik: nissinneah aiumuhpash papaume kehtahsoot: nenan ummequnnoh kunnupsuhkwhosoowenin.
45.2 Kuttanooe wompes onk wunnechonoouh wosketompaog: wunnetuppantamooonk sookunnosoo en kussisuttoonut: newutche Manit koonanumukup micheme.
45.3 Puttukquapisish Kuttogkomooneg kehquawaut, woi masukkenan: weche kussohsumooonk kah mamuttanittooonk.
45.4 Kah kummamuttanissooonkanut wunnaiyeue naiyeumitteash, newutche wunnomwaeyeuonk, kah manunnissuonk, kah wunnomwaeseonk: kah kuttinnuhkou pish kukkuhkootumunk, uhquinneunkquohkish.
45.5 Kukkouhquadtash kenaiyeuash ut wuttahhoowout Ketahsoot ummatwomoh; ne nashpe penushahittit missinninnuog aque kohhogat.
45.6 Kutapuonk, O God, oiohteau micheme kah micheme: kukkehtahsootumooe anwohoo ne sampwiyeue anwohoo.
45.7 Koowomontam sampweusseonk, kah kussekinneam matchetooonk: newutche Manit kum-Manittoom kussussequnukup, nashpe wekontamwe pamme anue onk nag wechiyeumukqueaneg.
45.8 Wame kuttogkooonkash {ussummunkquatash onatuh} myrrh, kah alloes, {kah} cassia; wutch ivorye wetuwomash, ne nashpe nag wekontamwahhunumukup.
45.9 Kehtahsootumog wuttaunoowoh wechiyeumopaneg kukquehtianummukquissooe muttumwussissog: kuttinnuhkounut wunnepauinneap kehche sonkiskkq ut Golde ogkoounash wutch Ophirit.
45.10 Nootash, woi wuttaunin, kah natwontash, kah ahchusutash; wanamim wonk nehenwonche, kummissinninnumog, kah koosh week.
45.11 Neit pish kehtahsoot mishe kodtantam koonetuonk: newutche noh kum-Manittoom, & noh wawissim
45.12 Kah Tiree wuttaunin na pish wuttappin nashpe magooonk, {nux} wanawekitcheg kunnuke missinninyeuog pish wonkquttumog Kuskesuk.
45.13 Kehtahsoot wuttaunoh panuppe sohsummooneunkquissoo unnomut, wutogkooonkash assequosooe Gold.
45.14 Pish passoowau Kehtahsootut ut momonekukquosooe ogkoounut: penumpaog, noh wechiyeumoncheh neh assuhkunkqutcheh, pish kuppattonchannunk.
45.15 Pish wekontamwe kah mushkouantamwe passoowoog: nag pish pettutteaog Kehtahsoot oonekamukqut.
45.16 Kunnechonog pish nompkompauehtauaog Koohshog, nag woh Sontimmohteaan ut mamusse ohkeut.
45.17 Pish Nummehquantamwahhoowam Koowesooonk ut nishnoh pometuonkanut: newutche pish Missinninuog koowaenomukquog micheme kah micheme.
46.0
46.1 MAnit nuttutashpuhhoowaonkanun kah Nummenuhkesooonkanun, ahche kogkunupanunnosu wattammehpunnamukish.
46.2 Newutche matta pish noowapissoomun tokonogque ohke ontohtag, kah tohkonogque wadchuash kununumunash en noeu kehtahhahit.
46.3 {Tokonogque} nippeash naut mushshontoowomoouk, kah pukkuttippohhohk, {tokonogque} wodchuash quequohk nashpe uppookeonk {Kehtoh}. Selah.
46.4 Seipoooo, uppahteahtukquishomash wekontamwohtunk Wuttootan God: ne wunnetupantamwe aiyeuonkuttoh ohtog Wekash anue Quanuhquabit.
46.5 God appu wunnahshomut; matta pish ontsapu: Manit pish wuttanumauuh, ahche nompoaeu.
46.6 Penoowohteaog mooshkoowopaneg, ahsoottummooonkash ontsohtopash: muhshantoowop, ohke sunnuppaemoop.
46.7 Jehovah wattiyeuwehteomit ahhontanooongash noowettomukqun, um-Mannitoomoh Jacob nuttutashpuhhoowaonkanun. Selah.
46.8 Peunk, namook wuttanakosooonkash Jehovah, uttoh ane mahche: Tauishinyeuonkanehteadt ut ohkeut.
46.9 Wohkuhquoshehtoo aiyeuwittoooonkash en wahquohkeyeuuk, poohqunauohtompeh, kah tummussum konnuketuhwheg, chikohsum Chariot ut noohtaut.
46.10 Chequnniekq kah wahteoook nen num-Manitoo: pish nummishhit ut wuttohtimoinneat, pish nummishhit ohkeut.
46.11 Jehovah wattiyeuwehteomit ahhontanooongash noowetomukqun; um-Manittoomoh Jacob nuttutashpoohhoowaonkanun. Selah.
47.0
47.1 Puhpunknitchohuk, wame kenau missinninnuog: mushshontoowag en Godut nashpe sohkuhsue muhshontoowaonk:
47.2 Newutche Jehovah anue quannuhquabit uhqunneunkqussu; noh kehche Kehtahsoot ut manusse ohkeut.
47.3 Pish sohkauau missinninneuh aque nohhoganonut, kah wuttahtimonash aque nussettunonut.
