47.4 Pish nuppepenamanushukqun nookompohkeun, muttae oonetuonk Jacob neh wamonomp. Selah.
47.5 Manit uspei nashpe muhshontoowaonk, Jehovah nashpe wuttunontoowaonk monuppuhpekq.
47.6 Unoohomunk waenomaonkash en Godut; unoohomunk waenomaonkash: unoohomunk waenomaonkash en nuk-Kehtahsootumoomun, unoohomunk waenomaonkash.
47.7 Newutche God Kehtahsootumoooo ut mamusse ohket unnoohhomunk waenomaonkash nashpe wahwahtamooonk.
47.8 God nanawunau penoowohteaog: God appu wunnetupantamwe wuttapuonkanit.
47.9 Wussontimomoouh Missinninyeuog moeog, ummissinninyeumoh um-Manittoomoh Abraham: newutche mattaohke ogqunegash wutchiyeumooash Godut: noh moocheke mishehhau.
48.0
48.1 MUssugken Jehovah, kah woh mishe waenomou ut wuttootannat nummanitoomun, ut oonetupantamwe wadchumut.
48.2 Wunompomukquate aiyeuonkanut ohteau wadchu Sion, mamusse ohke oowekontammoowontamun, nanomuttiniyeu, wuttootan kehche Kehtahsoot.
48.3 God wahhou ut oonekamukqut, wutche tashpuhhoowaonk.
48.4 Newutche kusseh, Kehtahsootumog mooopaneg, moae paumushshopaneg.
48.5 Wunnamunaop, kah nemehkuh muhchantamuppaneg, wuttamantamupaneg, kah wussemoopaneg.
48.6 Wapissooonk na wuttut tohqunukqunaop, kah uhquomomooonk, onatuh kodtauegehhae muttumwussis.
48.7 Kuppoohqushshadtoh Tarshishe kehtoonogquash nashpe wutchepwosh.
48.8 Neane nootamogup, ne nuttine namunanonup, ut wuttootanat Jehovah wattiyeuehteomit ahhontanooonkash, ut wuttootanat Kum-Manitoomun, God pish ummunuhkehtauun micheme. Selah.
48.9 Nummequantamumunnanonup koowamoasooe kuttumonteanitteaonk, woi God, ut unnome Kut-Templeoomut.
48.10 Neanag Koowesuonk woi God, ne unni koowaenomitteaonk en wahquohkeyeuuk: kuttinuhkou numwohtau wunnomwausseonk.
48.11 Mushkouantaj wadchu Sion, wuttonninnunk Judah wekontamwehhittich, newutche koosuttumooonkash.
48.12 Wenuhkomook Sion, kah qunnupuhshotamook, aketamook ukqunuhquekamukquash.
48.13 Wae kehkinnasekq wunnaneutunkash, natwontamook oonekamukquash; onk woh kummushamunneau en pometuonkanut paomoouk.
48.14 Newutche yeuuh God kum-Manittoomun micheme kah micheme; noh pish nussompoowunukqun pache nuppooonkanut
49.0
49.1 YEu nootamook, wame missinninyeuog, kukkeihtamook wame wodohkeagish muttaohket:
49.2 Naneswe peonumukquissitcheg kah mashonumukquissitcheg, wanaekitcheg kah matchekitcheg moaeu.
49.3 Nuttoon pish weogquttum waantamooonk: kah nuttahhe natwontamooonk pish papaume wohwohtamooonk.
49.4 Pish nuttahchusittam kuhkinneasuonk; pish noowohshwunum nunnupwoaonk ut harput.
49.5 Tohwaj woh wapisse ut matche kesukodut, nogquanne matcheusseonk qunnupuhkonkqueon?
49.6 Nag pabahtontogik oowenawetuonganoo, mah mashkowacheg ut monahkish ummomatchiyeumoooash:
49.7 Matta woh howan {nag} tohen tapwhooo wemattoh, asuh ummagooanushuh mannoohwhuttooonk en Godut:
49.8 (Newutche mannoohwhaonk ukketeahogkonoouh mishoadtu, kah wohkuhkquohshin micheme )
49.9 Onk woh noh micheme pompumontam, kah matta namoo anunooonk.
49.10 Newutche naum waantamwoh nuppoooh, wonk assooke kah puppunashumwe wosketomp pagquanyeuog, kah nukkodumog oowenawetuonkanoo en onkatogik.
49.11 Keme unantamwog, wekoowoash pish michemahtaash kah ootahtuwonkanoowoash panupe wame pometuonkanash; huttamog wuttohkeyeuoash ne assooweshittit.
49.12 Qut, Wosketomp abit quehtiantuonkanit matta nukqutqunahteooo: ogquinnunkquissoo nuppoe puppinashimwut.
49.13 Yeu ummayeu wuttahsutuonkanoo; onch wunnechonoouh wuttapinneamunneau ne anoowahittit. Selah.
49.14 Onatuh Sheepsog sepsunog wenohkeit, nuppooonk pish ummomoohwhuh; kah sampwesitcheg pish wunnanawunouh mohtompahk, kah oonetuonkanoo pish mohtupaemoo ut wenohket, wutch ootohkeonkanoowout.
49.15 Qut Manit pish pohquohwhunau nukketeahogkou wutch ummenuhkesooonkanit wenohke; newutche pish nuttatumunuk. Selah.
49.16 Ahque wapissish howan wenaekehhit, Weeke sohsumooonk mishehtosik.
49.17 Newutche nupuk matta pish teag ootoooun: wussohsumooonk matta pish assuhkongkoo.
49.18 Tokonogque pamontog, wunnanumop ukketeahogkonoh: kah wosketompaog pish koowawenomukquog wunne unnehheadt kohhog.
49.19 Noh pish au uppometuonkanoowout ooshoh, nag matta pish nanukqut namooog wequai.
49.20 Wosketomp noh abit queihtianittuonkanit, kah matta wohtamook, ogquinneunkquissoo nuppooe puppinashimwut.
50.0
50.1 Masukkenuk Manit, Jehovah kuttoop, kah wehquttumup ohke waj pashpishont paje adt wayont.
50.2 Wutch Sionut, panupeyeue wunetuonkanit God wohsumup.
50.3 Num-Manittoomun pish peau, kah matta pish chequnapu: noohtau pish mahchukisoowomoo ut anaquabit, kah pish mishehtashin noh waenu.
50.4 Pish wehquttum en kesukqut wutch wohqut, kah en ohket, onk woh wussumau ummissinninyeumoh.
50.5 Muhmonumiekq noonetupantamoomog, nag wanoowohkonukqueomp nashpe sephausooonk.
50.6 Kah kesukquash pish nahtehteomooash wussampweusseonk: newutche God nehenwonche wussuttumaenyeuoo. Selah.
50.7 Nootamook, woi nummissinninyeumog, kah pish nukkekuttaohkam; Woi Israel, kah kuttiyeuohkonittooe wauwaonsh, nen Manit, {nux} kum-Manitoom.
50.8 Matta kuttaiuskomunooh wutche kussephausooonkash, newutche chikohtae kummagooonkash naquahteahtopash anaquabeh.
50.9 Matta pish nunemunoh nompohshim wutch kekut, asuh nompohshimwe-goat wutch kutchipinneutunkanit.
50.10 Newutche wame touohkamuque puppinashimwog, noottaiheneunk, puppinashimwog ut muttanonkane wodchuash.
50.11 Noowaehhoog wame wodchue puppinashaog: kah sassakussue ahteuhkone puppinashimwog nuttaiheog.
50.12 Kodtupweos, woh mo kuttinninooun, newutche muttaohk nuttaihe, kah neadtahshimmechumik.
50.13 Sun woh nummeech kouishine weyaus, asuh sun woh nootattam oosquehunkanoo Goatsog?
50.14 Sephausish en Godut tabantamooonk, kah oadtuhkau anue quanuhquabit kukquahshomaonkash.
50.15 Kah wehquttumah wuttamehpunae kesukodut, kah pish kuppohquohwunush, kah pish kussohsumoooneh.
50.16 Qut God unnau matchetoooh, Tohkuttinohto ontuttumunnat nukkuhkoowaongash, asuh {woh} kunnemunumnat noonoowaonk en kuttoonut?
50.17 Nean sekinneaman kuhkootumwehteaonk, kah unnuhteaan nukkuttooonkash kuppishquaniyeu.
50.18 Nauadcheh kummootoowaenin, neit koowetoowom, kah koowechuhhum mamossueninyeuog.
50.19 Kummag kuttoon en matchutut, kah kenan ayimoomoo ahsookohkodteamooonk.
50.20 Kunnummattapue mamatcheun kemat; kuppanoowaonchumooon koohkas wunnaumonoh.
50.21 Yeush kuttosenapash, kah matta toh nisseup: kuttinantamup nuppaiosukke unnisip neanussean: qut pish kuttaiuskomush, kah nash noonohtouunash anaquahtag kuskesukquash.
50.22 Yeuyeu yeu natwontamook, kenau wannanumogish God, ishkont kussukqshanumwoo, kah na matta pohquahsoowaeninyeunooh.
50.23 Howan maguk waenomuwaonk, nussohsumooonuk: kah noh {sampwe} wanohtunk, wuttisseongash pish nunnahtun oowadchanuwaonk God.
51.0
51.1 KUttumonteanumeh, woi God, neanag koowamoasue-monaneteaonk: neanag mataanuhkish kukkuttumonteaneteae monaneteaonkash cheskhash nummatcheseonkash.
51.2 Panupe kutchesumeh wutch nummatcheseonganut, kah pahkhe wutch nuppaneusseonganit.
51.3 Newutche nussompoowotam nuppoohqunumooongash: kah nummatcheseonk naquahteahteau anaquabeh.
51.4 Ken, ken webe kummatchenehhunup, kah nuttissep yeu machuhk ut kenamooonkanut: onk woh kussompsittont ketookoan, kah kuppahksittont wussuttuman.
51.5 Kusseh, nukkehkenawehhitteap ut matchetuppantamooonganut: kah ut matcheseonganut noowompukquaonukup nookas.
51.6 Kusseh, kukkodtantam wanumuhkiteyeuuk ut unnaumiyeuut: kah kemiyeuut pish koowahtauwahhe waantamooonk.
51.7 Pahkhe nashpe hyssop, onk pish nuppahkes: kutchissumeh, kah pish nutanue wompeseumkoon.
51.8 Nootamwahhe wekontamooonk kah mushkouantamooonk: onk woh mishkonash nish poohquehtohhomohpash wekontamoomooash.
51.9 Puttogwhush kuskesuk wutch nuppaneseonkanut; kah cheskhash wame nummatcheseonkash.
51.10 Kesehteah pahke muttah, woi God; kah sampwiyeue nashauonk wuskehteah.
51.11 Ahque pogeseh wutch anaquabean; kah ahque ammanumah koonetupantamwe nahshauonk.
51.12 Numpunnumah wekontamoe koowadchanuaonk: kah kogkanuneh nashpe kunnanaue nahshaunittoom.
51.13 Neit pish nukkuhkootumau paneusecheg kummayash, kah matcheseaninyeuog pish kuhqunnuppuhkompauehtunkquog.
51.14 Pohquahwusseh wutch wishquehheonkane kesuhkotamooonkanit, woi God, ken wadchanoowae nummanittoom: {kah} nenan pish mishontoowaoohhoomoo kussompweusseonk.
51.15 Woi Lord, woshwunish nussissittoonash, kah nuttoon pish nahtehteomoo koowawenomitteaonk.
51.16 Newutche matta kukkodtantamoo sephausuonk, asuh woh kuttinumauunnun: matta koowekontammooontamoo chikohtae magooonk.
51.17 Manittooe sephausooonkash poohquishae nahshauonk: poohquiyeue kah hohpoe muttah, woi God, matta pish kummeshanantammooh.
51.18 Wunneissish ut koone tapinneamooonkanit en Sionut: aiyeuush Jerusaleme qussukquanninneuttongash.
51.19 Neit pish koosikitteahhit nashpe sampweseae sephausooonkash, nashpe chikohtae-magooonk kah pasquiyeue chikohtae-magooonk: neit pish sephausuog oxinog ut kut-Alteroomut.
52.0
52.1 TOhwaje mushshoowaan ut woskehhoowaonkanit, woi munehkesooenin? ummonaneteaonk God michemohteau.
52.2 Kenan natwontam woskehhoowaonkash: onatuh kenehquog ne assookohkodteaanuhkosoomoouk.
52.3 Kutanue wamontam machuhk onk ne wanekik: kah panoowaeyeuonk anue onk sampwe unnoowonat. Selah.
52.4 Koowomantam wame woskehhoowae kuttooonkash, woi asookohkodteamooe menan.
52.5 God pish wonk kussunukkehthuk micheme, pish kuttammanuk, kah pish kukkodtunuk wutch kootahtuonganit, kah kunnooswomohhuk wutch wuttahtuout pamontogik. Selah.
52.6 Sampwesitcheg pish wonk naumog, kah wapissuog, kah pish wuttahhanehtauouh.
52.7 Kusseh, yeuuh noh wosketomp matta wamunehkesooonkanehteahp Godoh: qut pabatantamup monahkish oowenawetuonkash, kah munnehkehhop wohhoguh ut ummatchetooonkanit.
52.8 Qut nen nuttogquinneunkquis askuhquame oliveuhtuk ut wekit God: nuppabahtantam ummonaneteaonk God micheme kah micheme.
52.9 Pish micheme koowawenomsh, newutche kummahche usseen: kah pish nuppahtissoowontam koowesuonk, newutche wunekin anaquabhittit koonetupantamoomog.
53.0
53.1 MAttamog noowop ut wuttahhut, wanne Godunoo; aninwog, kah mahche usseog neskinneunkque Matcheseonk: matta pasuk ooneussu.
53.2 God womopoop wutche kesukqut ut wunnechonoowout wosketompaog, namunat sun howan wohwohtam, {kah} natinneawhont Godoh.
53.3 Nag nishnoh pasuk mahche quiskeog, nag moaeu neskinneunkquissook; matta howan ooneussu matta pasuk
53.4 Sun anakositcheg matcheseonk, matta oowohwohtamooonkaneog? uttiyeug moohwhoncheg nummissinninyeunumoh, neane mechhittit petukqunneg; nag matta wehquttumauaog Godoh.
53.5 Na wuttut mishe wabissinaop, na woh matta adt wapissoomukup: newutch God seahhomup wishkonash noh ayeuohkone wenukkonkquean, nag kutogkodchehhopaneg, newutche God nah ummeshananumopah.
53.6 Howan pish makuk wadchonaonkanoo Israel wutch Sionut! God qunnupunuk ummussunoonkanoo ummissinninyeumoh, Jacob pish muskouantam, kah Israel pish wekontam.
54.0
54.1 WAdchaneh, woi God, nashpe koowesuonk, kah wussumeh nashpe kummenuhkesuonk.
54.2 Notash nuppeantamooonk, woi God; ahchusuttash nuttoone kuttooonkash.
54.3 Newutche penoowohteaog nummahche nepauehtunkquog, kah uhquanumehhoowacheg natinneahwhoog nukketeahogkou; matta poonooopaneg Godoh anaquabhittit. Selah.
54.4 Kusseh, God nuttanunosooweninneum: Lord wetomau nag kogkanunocheg nukketeahogkou.
54.5 Pish matunkquattauoh nummatwomoh; nag tummehtah ut koonomwaeyeuonkanit.
54.6 Pish nanouwe kussephamauush; pish noowawenotum Koowesuonk, woi Jehovah, newutche wunnekin.
54.7 Newutche nuppahquahwhunukup wutch wame wuttamehpunaonganit: kah nuskesuk namup ukkodtantamooonk ut nummatwomut.
55.0
55.1 NOOtash nuppeantamooonk, woi God; kah ahque puttogwish wutch noowehquttumooonkanit.
55.2 Kehkehtah, kah nootah: nummom ut nootoowaonkanut, kah nutchequttum:
55.3 Newutche oowadtauohtunkqussuonk matwau, newutche wuttuhquanumehhoowaonk matchetoo: newutche nuttinuhkonkquog matcheseonk, kah moosquantamwe nussekinneunkquog.
55.4 Nuttah uhquamamoomoo ut nuttinomiyeumut: kah nuppooe saiaskshantuonkash nuppogshoqunash.
55.5 Wabesuonk kah nunnukshaonk nuppeaonukqunash, kah uhquehpunnatahhaonk nunnuhkuhkonk.
55.6 Kah nissip, woi ununnuppohwhunontuh wuskuhwhananut; onk woh nuttooem, kah nuttanwosun.
55.7 Kusseh, neit woh nunnanwusham en noadtit, & nuttoiap tauohkamukqut. Selah.
55.6 Woh nukkinnippehteo nuppohquahhamooonk wutch wapiyeue mishehtahshinit kah nashquitinit.
55.9 {Nag} Pagquas, woi Lord, {kah} chachapunush wenannuoash: newutche nummahche naum chekeusseunk kah aiyeutuonk ut ootanat.
55.10 Kesukodae kah nukkonae ukquinupishotamunneau ut qussukquaninneutonkanit: wonk woskehhoowaonk kah noowantamooonk na noeu ohtaash
55.11 Matchetooonk na noeu ohteau: assookekodteamooonk kah puhchuhteaonk matta amaemunooash wuteh wuttaumaiogqut.
55.12 Newutche matta Matwau noh ashpunnamukqueomp, neit woh nukkehchittahhomp; asuh matta noh sekinneaieph, noh mashehhomp wohhoguh aiyeuohkone nohhogat, neit woh nuppaputtogquehtauop.
55.13 Qut unnoh ken, wosketomp, nuttatupeyeum, nussompohshassoowaeninyeum, kah noh waetompaeuhp.
55.14 Noowekanue kenoossoowotumunonup, kah noowuhwowechatimunonup en wekit God.
55.15 Nuppooonk nag tohqunukquehhittich, kah keteae womusehtitch en chepiohkomukqut: newutche matchetooonk ohteau ne wadohkehhittit, {kah} kenuke nag.
55.16 Qut nen, pish noowehquttumau God: kah Jehovah pish noowadchonuk.
55.17 Wanunkooukish kah mohtompohkish, kah puhshaquadcheh pish nuppeantam, kah nummushontooae mau, kah noh pish nootam noowadtauatunkquissooonk.
55.18 Wunnahteae pohquohwhunop nukketeahogkou wutch aiyeutuonk aiyeuqueomp: newutche monaog noowechoohhumukup.
55.19 God pish nootam kah wuttuhkupunanuh, nux noh noadt aoiapehpoh, Selah: newutche wane wuttossooweonkaneog, newutche matta qushoooog Godoh.
55.20 Sumogunumup wunnitchegash aiyeuohkone nag wanuhkonukquitcheh: poohqunumup oonoowaonk.
55.21 Wuttoone kuttooonkash anue moosiyeupash onk ne butter, qut aiyeuittuonk ohtop wuttahhit: ukkuttooonkash anue noohkiyeupash onk ne pumme, qut onch nish kodtunosue togkodtegkanyeupash.
55.22 Unnuhkou koowean Jehovah, kah pish kukkogkanunuk: matta pish nanukqut unanumooo sampweseaenin ontsapinnat.
55.23 Qut ken, woi Manit, pish nag koowomussuunnoog en nuppooonkane passahtheganit: nehshehteaeninyeuog kah assookekodteaeninyeuog matta pish pomantamooog puhshe ukkesukodtumoooash: qut nen pish kuppabahtanumush.
56.0
56.1 MOnanumeh, woi God, newutche wosketomp nukkod mishahquonuk: aiyeuehteae nishnoh kesuk nuttuhquanumehhuk.
56.2 Nummatwomog asekesukokish nukkod mishashquonukquog: newutche nag monaog aiyeuohkositcheg, Woi ken Quanuhquabean.
56.3 Wabeseon, pish kuppabahtanumush.
56.4 Ut Godut pish noowawenotum wuttinnoowaonk, nuppabahtanumop Manit, matta pish nukquehtamoo weyaus toh woh anehhukque.
56.5 Asekesukohkish matauwuttamwehteaog nukkuttooonkash: wame wuttinantamooonkanoowoash, nuttayeuohkonukqunnash wutche machuhk.
56.6 Nag miyaeog, attahshaog wohhogkauh, kehkinneasuog nuttontanehtuonkash ashkwhitchahtit wutche nukketeahogkou.
56.7 Sun pish pahquohhamog nashpe matchetooonk? ut kummoosquantamooonkanut punnuhteash missinninuog, woi God.
56.8 Kuttogetam noowauonuonkash, poonush nussipequonash kooweshquadt: sun matta ohtanooash koosukkuhwhonganit?
56.9 Mauinnittauunon, neit pish nummatwomog quishkeog: yeu noowahteauun, newutche God noowechoohhumuk.
56.10 Ut Godut pish noowawenotum wuttinnoowaonk: Jehovahut pish noowawenotum wuttinnoowaonk.
56.11 God nuppabahtanumop: matta pish nukquehtammooh wosketomp toh woh anehhukque.
56.12 Kukquashomunooonkash nuttappehtunkqunash, woi God, pish koowowaenomish.
56.13 Newutche kuppohquohwhunop nukketeahogkou wutch nuppooonkanit: sun matta pish kuppohquohwhutteo nussetash wutch penushaonkanit? onk woh nuppompumusham anaquabit God ut oowequaiyeumooout pamontogik.
57.0
57.1 MOnanumeh, woi God, monanumeh, newutche nukketeahogkou kuppabahtanumuk: nux nuttutashpuhhoowonkanehteam kunnupwhunog wutonkauwohtomoo, napacheh yeush onkapunaonkash pamuhshemoout.
57.2 Pish nummauinittau God noh anue quonuhquabit: en Godut noh aseanushukque wame teanteaquasinish.
57.3 Pish anoohteamoo wutch kesukqut, kah pish noowadchonuk wutch wuttushpunamoowaonkanit noh kod musashquonukque; Selah. God pish anootam umonaneteaonk kah oonomwaonk.
57.4 Nukketeahogkou wetomau Qunnonoowoh, kah noowetsumoomoog nag chogaswutcheg; {nux} wunnamonauh wosketompaog, wepittooash konnukkehtoohwhegannuukish kah kouhquottooukish, kah wenannu keni togkodteg.
57.5 Mishshehhitchash. woi God, en aonkaue kesukqut: kussohsumooonk anue qunuhquohtaj mamusse ohke.
57.6 Nag mahche quaquashwunaog ahshap wutche nuttontanehtuonkash, nukketeahogkou nawanosu: wonehteopaneg anuhquabeh, ne nag nehenwonche nanoeu mahche adt pinishahhettit. Selah.
57.7 Kesantamoomoo nuttah, woi God, nuttah kesantamoomoo: pish nukketoohomam kah noowawenomoowam.
57.8 Toohkish nussohsumooonk, toohkeg Psaltery kah Harp: nen pish nunnompoae toohkem.
57.9 Pish koowawenomush, woi Lord, kenugke missinninnuut: pish kukketoohomauush kenuke wuttohtimmoinnunk.
57.10 Newutche kummonaneteaonk mussi en aongkaue kesukqut, kah koonomwaonk en mattokqsut.
57.11 Mishehhiteash, woi God, en aongkaue kesukqut: kussohsumooonk anue qunuhquohtaj mamusse ohke.
58.0
58.1 Sun wunnumuhkit kussimwoo sampwiyeuonk, woi mukkineonk? Sun kussompwe wussuttumumwoo, woi kenau wunnamonauh wosketompaog?
58.2 Nux, muttohhoowae kuttosemwoo matchetooonk: kukquokquadhumumwoo kunnitchekane chekeusseonkanoo ut ohkeit.
58.3 Matchetooog penoowohteoooog wutche otomukaut, wawonuog quenau neghittit, panoowaeyeuog.
58.4 Wutonkquoskehtuonkanoo ogqueneungquodt wutonkquoskehtuonkanit ashkook; ogqueneunkqussuog en mo nanootamooe Adder noh kobhog wehtauog:
58.5 Noh matta woh nootauont oowadtauatunkqussuonkanoo podchummooaeninuog, tokounukuhque waantamwe padchummuahtit.
58.6 Poohquehtahhash wepittuoash, woi God, ut wuttoonoowout: kuttehtahhash ukkehtomputtoomoooash wuskukqunnonoowaog, woi Jehovah.
58.7 Sobpashittich onatuh nippeit, pamuttchuwohk naquahteae: suhtukquohhoowadt pumwinneat ukkouhquadtash, onatuheyeuwehtich sokqussut.
58.8 Onatuh askequattam noh sobpasit: {nish noh pasuk} neine amaetch: onatuh wun-nussauonk muttumwossus, onk woh matta namooog nuppauz.
58.9 Kuttohkuhkoomoouh asq aammattamwehhitteup koesog, pish wutammanuh neane nashpe pemsquoh, keteae kah wonk ut ummoosquantamooonkanit.
58.10 Sampweseaenin pish mushkouantam, nak ne annootaonk: pish kutchishsitto wusseeash ooshquehhunkanoowout matchetooog.
58.11 Nemehkuh pish wosketomp unoowau, Wunnummuhkit onkquatonkanuoo wutche sampwesit: wunumuhkit unnoh God wasuttuk ut ohkeit.
59.0
59.1 Pohquohwusseh wutch nummatwomut, woi num-Manittoom: tahshineh wutch nag waabehtunkqueoneg.
59.2 Pohquohwusseh wutch anakositcheg matcheusseonk, kah wodchaneh wutch nushehteaeninyeuut.
59.3 Newutche kusseh, nag ashkuhteaoog wutche nukketeahogkou; masukkenugik nuttaiyeuohkone moehtunkquog; matta wutche nuppaneusseonk asuh nummatcheusseonk, woi Jehovah.
59.4 Nag quogqueog kah nanashweog matta wutche nummatcheusseonk: toohkish kuttanumiinneat, & moninneash.
59.5 Newutche ken, woi ahhonttanooonkane Manit, um-Manittoomoh Israel, toohkish nattauwohhonat wame penoowohteaog: ahque monanim howae matchetooe paneusseaeninyeuog. Selah.
59.6 Nag wunonkquae quishkeog: neskehtunkquissuog onatuh annum, kah qunnupuhkomog kehtootan.
59.7 Kusseh, mohmakutchuog nashpe wuttoonoo: togkodteganuoo wussussetoonoowout, newutche, {noowaog}, howan nootog.
59.8 Qut ken woi Jehovah, pish kutahanehtauoog; pish wame penoowohteaog kummommoshquohkonoog.
59.9 {Waj} ummenuhkesuonk pish kuppahtissuonish: newutche God nukqunnuhque wuhkonoos.
59.10 Monaneteae num-Manittoom pish nuttattumuskonk: God pish nuttunanumuk namunat {nukkodtantamooonk} ut nummatwomut
59.11 Ahque nag paguas, ishkont nummissinninyeumog wannantamwog: nag seaoohkau nashpe kummenuhkesuonk, kah nookin, woi Jehovah nuttogqunneganun.
59.12 Wutche muttoone ummatcheseonkanoo, kah mussistoone ukkuttooonkanoo, tohqununnaj ut uppehtuanumooonkanooout: kah wutche matcheunnaneteaonk kah pannoowaonk ne anoowahhittit.
59.13 {Nag} mahchumooah ut kummoosquantamooonkanit, mahtuppan, onk woh ohquapuog: kah wahteauhittich God nanauwunum ut Jacob, en wahquishik ohke. Selah.
59.14 Kah wunonkoouk qushkehittich, kah nehnehteahittich onatuh anumwut, kah qunnupwushahhittich kehtootan.
59.15 Nanwushahhittich wutche meechum, kah moohmooskoowahittich matta wamupwehhittit.
59.16 Qut nen nuttinnoohomom kummenuhkesuonk; nux nummishontoowaoohomom kemonaneteaonk nompoaeu: newutche koowuhkonoossinnuup, kah kuttutashpuhkoowaonkannuup, wutche nen, ut nootamehpunnae kesukodut.
59.17 Pish kukketoohomauush, woi nummenuhkesooonk: newutche God noowuhkonoos, kah moaneteae num-Manittoom.
60.0
60.1 WOi God, kuppogkesumunonup, kusseahhumunonup, kummoosquanimunonup; woi quishkish wonk en nohhoganonut.
60.2 Kukquequanehtop ohke; kuppassoogkunumun: netashkehtauush na adt poohquakish, newutche nunnukemoo.
60.3 Kunnahtunomp kummissinninnumog manuhkakish: kootattamhimunonup chepshaonkane Wine.
60.4 Kuttinnumnuopaneg muttaak nag quashukqueaneg: onk woh sepakunumun newutche wunnomwaonk. Selah.
60.5 Onk woh pohquahwunnou noh wamonadt; wadchanuash nashpe kuttinuhkou, kah nootah.
60.6 God unnoowop ut oonetuppantamweyeuonkanit, pish nummushkouantam: pish nutchupunum Shechem, kah nukquokquadhum Succothe oonauuhkoi.
60.7 Gilead nuttaihe, kah Manaseh nuttaihe, Ephraim wonk ummenuhkesuonk nuppuhkuhk; Judah nootinomatuonkannehteaeninneum.
60.8 Moab nuttahtoochukkutshohkuhkoom, woskeche Edom pish nuppumuhkon nummohkus: Philistia, mushkowaoseh.
60.9 Howan pish passoowet en manuhkak ootanat? howan pish assoowussit en Edomut?
60.10 Sun matta pish ken, woi God, noh papakenukqueogup? kah ken, woi God, matta wahwechaohp nuttaiyeuehteomunonog?
60.11 Anunummaiinean wutch wuttamehpunaonkanit: newutche wutanunosuonk wosketomp tohnoocheyeumoo.
60.12 Nashpe God pish nukkenompae ussemun: newutche nagum pish tahtaskuhkouau nunmatwomunnonog.
61.0
61.1 NOOtash noowadtauatunkqussuonk, woi God, kehkehtash nuppeantamooonk.
61.2 Wutch wahquohkeyeuuk pish kummauunitauush, nuttah kooshkoshunk: ussoowusseh qussukquanit ne anuwuhqussoomukqueh.
61.3 Newutche kutonkauwuhqussoop wutche nen, kah munnuhkiyeue wuhkonoos wutch matwaut.
61.4 Pish nuttaiin kekit micheme: pish nupbahtantam ut kunnuppohwhune onkanuhtaut. Selah.
61.5 Newutche ken, woi God, kunootamup nukquohshomuaonkash kuttinunumaiup ookompahtoonkanoo nag quahtiantogik koowesuonk.
61.6 Pish kussepe pomantamwah ketassoot: kah ukkodtumoomash neane monatash pometuonkash.
61.7 Pish appu anaquabit God micheme: woi nanashwunush monaneteaonk kah wunnomwaonk ne woh wadchanukquit.
61.8 Nemehkuh nuttinnoohomom koowesuonk micheme, onk woh asekesukohkish nutussenash nukquoshomuaonkash.
62.0
62.1 Wunnumuhkit nukketeahogkou pahtissuwonau Godoh: noowadchanitteaonk {wumoomoo} wohhagat.
62.2 Noh wepe nukqussukquanum kah noowadchanitteaonk: noh nukqunnuhquiyeuonk; matta pish nummishe onttunnitteoh.
62.3 Toh unnoohque kunnatwontamumwoo woskehhuwaonk ayeuohkone wosketomp? pish wame kunnishitteamwoo: pish kuttogquinneunkquissumwoo nawae qussukquaninneutunk, kah onatuh kuhquishqueneutunk.
62.4 Wepe wetoowotuog uppunnuhkonaout wutch ukquehtianumukqussuonkanit, tapinneamog panoowaonkash: wunnanitteaog nashpe wuttoonoo, qut unnomiyeue mattanitteaog. Selah.
62.5 Nukketeahogkou, wepe pahtissuwos Manit: newutche nuttoashkuhwhompattam wutch wohhogat.
62.6 Nagum wepe nukqussukquanum kah noowadchanitteaonk: unnoh nukqunnuhquiyeuonk: matta pish nuttontunniteoh.
62.7 Godut ohteau noowadchanitteaonk kah nussohsumooonk: munuhkiyeue nukqussukquanum, kah nuttutashpuhhoowaonk ohteau Godut.
62.8 Pabahtanumuk naquahteae, kenau missinninnuog, sookunumook kuttahhoowoash ut anuhquabit: God nootashpuhhoowaonkaninnean. Selah.
62.9 Wunnummuhkit meshananumukqussuenninnuog tahnoocheyeuog, kah wuttooanumukqussueninnuog pannoowaeyeuooog: quttuhwhut moaeu anue nunkinog onk ne tahnoocheyeuuk.
62.10 Pabahtantamoohteohk uhkquanumehhuwaonk, kah tohnoocheyeuwehteohk ut mukkookinnuwaonkanit: wenawetuonkash nano monag, ahque wuttahhoowontamook.
62.11 God pasukqut kuttoop, nesit yeu nunnootamunap, menuhkesuonk wutchaiyeumoo Godut.
62.12 Wonk monaneteaonk wutchaiyeumoo kohhogat, woi Lord: newutche kutonkquatau nishnoh wosketomp neanag wutanakausuonk.
63.0
63.1 WOi God, ken num-Manittoom, pish nompoaeu kenatinneawhush: nukketeahogkou kuhketoon wutche ken, nooweyaus kumminehke kodtanumuk ut nunnohtae kah kuhketoonooe ohkeit, ne mo napenook:
63.2 Namunat kummenuhkesuonk kah kussohsumooonk, neane nahnauunomp ut wunnetupantamwekamukqut.
63.3 Newutche wamoasue kummananeteaonk anue wunnekin onk pomantamooonk: nussussittoonash pish koowaenomukqunash.
63.4 Yeu pish kuttinne wunnanumunun, aspamantam: pish nuttashunum nunnitchegash ut koowesuonkanit.
63.5 Nukketeahogkou pish tapupoo onatuh nashpe wein kah wesuuk: kah nuttoon pish koowaenomuk nashpe wekontamwe mussissittoonash.
63.6 Mehquanumunon ut nuttappinneat, kah notwonumunon, ut {nuhkonae} ashkuhhumooonkanit.
63.7 Newutche ken mo nuttanumonteaonk: newaje ut kenuppohwhune okauuuhtaut pish nummushkouantam.
63.8 Nukketeahogkou kummenuhke ahsuhkonk: kuttinnuhkou nukkogkanunuk.
63.9 Qut nag nattinneahwoncheg nukketeahogkou wunnushonaout, pish awog wutchomukqut.
63.10 Pish nushoog nashpe togkodteg, nag pish wutch chuppaiyeumoo wonkqussissog.
63.11 Qut ketassoot pish mushkouantam ut Godut; nishnoh pasuk noh chachekeyeuadt nashpe nakum pish wawenowau: qut wuttoonoo nag panoowacheg, pish kuppohhomun.
64.0
64.1 Nootash noowadtauatunkqussooonk, woi God, ut nuppeantamooonkanit; wadchan nukketeaonk wutch qushaonkanit matwau.
64.2 Adtasheh wutch keme ukkenoonittuonkanoowout matchetooag; wutch mooshque oowapeonkanoo anakausitcheg matcheseonk:
64.3 Nag kehtattoog wenanu onatuh togkodteg, {kah} quoshuhqunumog pumwinneat ukkouhquattoo, {nux} wesogkanue kuttooonkash:
64.4 Onk woh keme pumwaog noh panuppeyeuit: teanuk uppumwouh, kah matta wapissuog.
64.5 Wuttoomaog wohhogauh ut matchitut: kenoonetuog woh ukkeme wunnahshonaout; noowaog, Howan pish noqueog?
64.6 Nag natinneahomog matcheseonkash, mahchehtoog wuttooe natinneahteaonk: nag nishnoh pasuk, naneswe wuttunomaioom kah wuttah moonoai.
64.7 Qut God pish uppumwuh kouhquodt, pish taiadtche noochumwehtahwhoog.
64.8 Nemehkuh pish punnishohtoog nehenwonche wenannu ut wohhogaout: wame nah moninnauohcheh, pish wussemooog.
64.9 Kah wame wosketompaog pish wabesuog, kah pish ontuttumwog wuttanakousuonk God: newutche pish waantamwe natwontamwog wuttiseonk.
64.10 Sampwesitcheg pish wekontamooonaog Jehovah, kah pish uppabahtanumouh: kah wame sampwetahhoncheg pish wawenowaog.
65.0
65.1 WAenomuaonk kuppahtissuonuk, woi God, ut Sionut: kah quahshowaonk pish kuttisehtontean.
65.2 Woi ken nohnootaman peuhtamooonk, wame weyaus pish kuppeyaonukqun.
65.3 Matcheusseonkash nuttomuskonkqunash: {qut} nuppaneusseonkanunonash pish kuttammapottauunash.
65.4 Wunnanumou wosketomp noh pepenauadt, kah passootshahhadt, wuttohkeontamunnat kekash: pish nuttapuppumumun nashpe oonekinnuonk kek, {nux} wunetuppantamwe kuttempleoom.
65.5 Nashpe uhqunneunkquohkish ut sompweusseonkanit, pish kunnampoohumaiumun, woi wadchanuae num-Manitoomun: uppabahtantamooonkanoo wame wahquishikish ohke, kah nag noapitcheg kehtahhanit.
65.6 Noh nashpe ummenukkesuonk manehkehtunk wadchuash, patukquabisit kenompoonk.
65.7 Noh chequinehtunk kehtahhane muhshontoowaonk, tukkooe wadtauohtunkquodt, kah muhshontoowae oowogkoueonkanoo missinninnuog.
65.8 Nag wonk wadohkecheg wahquohkeyeuuk wabissooontamog kukkehkinneasumash: koowekontamwohteo mohtompanae kah wunnonkquae sohhomooonkash.
65.9 Kenattauohtoh ohke, kah kunnippehkontamun: kah kummishe wenawekehtauun nashpe wussepeum God, ne namwohtag nippe: kukquahshawehtauoog weahchiminnash, mahche yeu inne quaquashwehtaman.
65.10 Kummishe wuttachpottoh wussauahteaiyeumash: kutasetahteanum oowonohchuwegash: kunoohkehtauun nashpe sookunnon, koonantam ne noh adt sonkik.
65.11 Kutchetuhquabehtoh kodtumoo nashpe koone-unnehhoowaonk, kah kummayash patuppashinneash wunnogkooonk.
65.12 Patuppashineash tauohkamukque tanadtupooonkanut: kah wadchuemesash mushkauantamoomooash waenu.
65.13 Tanadtupooonkash wunnuhkuhkomunau flocksog: oonauuhkoiyeuash wonk unkuhwhosuash nashpe weahchiminneash; mushkouantamwohtunkquissuog, wonk ketoohomaog.
66.0
66.1 MUshkouantamwehtunkqusseg en Godut, wame kenau ohkeash.
66.2 Unnoohomonk oowesuonkane quehtiantamooonk: sohsumwahteoook oowaenomukquissuonk.
66.3 Unnoohk God toh kuttine uhquinneunkquis ut kutanuhkosuonkanit? newutche kummushe menuhkesuonk kummatwomog pish wonkumooe kutaquehtunkquog.
66.4 Mamusse ohke pish koowauwussumuk, kah kukketoohomunk: nag pish unoohhomaog koowesuonk. Selah.
66.5 Peyunk kah naumook wuttanuhkosooonkash God: unnoh uhqunneunkqussu ut wuttinehhaonk wosketompaog wunnaumonauh.
66.6 Nunnobohteaiyeuwehteooop kehtah: mussetooe panupwushshntamupaneg tommog, nanuttut mushkouantamooonanonup.
66.7 Noh nanawunum nashpe ummenuhkesuonk micheme, wuskesukquash namoomooash wuttohtimmonash: chekehtogik ahque mishshehhahtich wohhogauh. Selah.
66.8 Woi wunnanumoohk kum-Manittoomun, kenau missinninuog, kah nootamahhoowak waenomamaonkane oowadtauatunkqussuonk.
66.9 Noh kogkanunont nukketeahogkonun pomantamooonkanut, kah matta anantamook woh ontahtaut nusseetunonash.
66.10 Newutche keen, woi God, kukqutchhimunonup: kukqutchchimunonup, silver neahhine qutchehtosik.
66.11 Kuppasooimunonup hashaput, kuppoonumup uhquanumooonk nussekonohtogqunonut.
66.12 Kunnaiyeumuohhomp wosketompaog waape nuppuhkukqunonash, nuppanupwushotamumunonup nootau, kah wonk nippe: qut kussuhhoowisumunonup en wenawetuohkomukqut.
66.13 Pish nuppetutteam kekit nashpe chikohtae magooonkash: pish kuttoadtuhkouush kukquahshomunooonkash.
66.14 Nish nussissitoonash wanoowomooukupupash, kah nuttoon anoowomooukup watamehpunaon.
66.15 Pish kussephamauush wunnogque chikohtae sephausuonkash, kah Ramse wetumunkquohk: pish nussephaus Oxinog kah Goatsog. Selah.
66.16 Nonche nootamook wame kenau quoshagish God, kah pish nuttontuttum uttuh asehp wutche nukketeahogkou.
66.17 Nummaunittauop nashpe nuttoon, kah mishehhop nashpe nenan.
66.18 Wuttooantamon matcheusseonk ut nuttahhut, Lord matta pish nunnootunk.
66.19 Qut wunnumuhkit God nunnootunkup: kuhkehtamup nuppeuhtamoe wattauatunkquissuonk.
66.20 Wunanumunnaj God, noh matta quashkunumookup nuppeuhtamooonk, asuh ummonaneteaonk wutch nohhogat.
67.0
67.1 GOd monaniminnean, kah wunnanuminnean: kah wuhsumohtunkquittuh wuskesuk. Selah.
67.2 Onk woh kummay wahtauun ut ohkeit, kah koowadchanuaonk kunnuke wame wuttohtimoinneash.
67.3 Missinninuog waenomukquish, woi God; wame missinninuog waenomukquish.
67.4 Woi wekontamwehhittich wuttohtimoinneunk, kah wekontamoohomahittich: newutche pish kussompe wussumoog missinninuog, kah kunnanawunoog wuttohtimoinneunk ut ohkeit. Selah.
67.5 Missinninuog waenomukquish, woi God; wame missinninuog waenomukquish.
67.6 {Neit} pish ohke mishummechumoomoo; {kah} God, {nux} nehenwonche kum-Manittoomun pish koonanumukqun.
67.7 God pish koonanumukqun, kah wame wahquohkeyeuukish pish ukquishouh.
68.0
68.1 MAnit omohkech, ummatwomoh sewohwhunach: nag wonk sekinneauoncheg, wussemhittitch wutch anuhquabit.
68.2 Pukkut neane toohohk, nag ne inne monchaoohkau: neane pittu sunnupohtag keshke noohtaut, matchetooog neine pagquanehtich anuhquabit God.
68.3 Qut sompwesitcheg wekontamwehhittich: mushkouantamwehhittich anuhquabit Manit, nux, mishe mushkouantamwehhittich.
68.4 Ketoohomohk God, waenomae unnoohomwontamook oowesuonk: mishehhook noh naoomukquit kesukquash, nashpe oowesuonk JAH, kah wekontamook anuhquabit.
68.5 God ooshoouh matta wadtoohshekeg, kah oostumwaeninnumoouh sekoushquaog, ut oonetuppantamwe aiyeuonkanit.
68.6 God wechinninnumuwaheau nonsiyeuoh: suhhoowunau wehwepuppissinitcheh moowohshogquohtogquash: qut chekehtogig wuttohtuog nunnopohteaiyeuut.
68.7 Woi God, ne suhwe nekonuhkouohp kummissinninnumog: panupwushaan touohkamuk, Selah:
68.8 Ohke quequanup, kesukquash wonk pinnippohshopash anaquabit God; nux nehenwonche Sinai {ontohtop} anaquabit God, um-Manittoomoh Israel.
68.9 Ken, woi God, kupponeunkquate sookinnonehteap, uttoh nashpe munnehkehtauohp sauunumooe kuttahtoonk.
68.10 Kummukkineonk ootohkeontamunap: ken, woi God, kukquahshawunumup kukkogkuttamesooonk wutche matchekoooh.
68.11 Lord makoop kuttooonk, monopaneg nag ne nootamwahhuahitteup.
68.12 Ahhontanooe kehtohsootumog kunnupshae wussemupaneg: kah nootutteae muttumwussis chachapunumup sequehtahhamooonk.
68.13 Mukkookone kussepsunumwop kunnuke ohkuhquoh, {onch pish kuttogqueneunkqussimwoo} wunnuppohwhunit wushkuhwhanan aquattuhsikish Silver, kah ummequnnoh wesoe Gold.
68.14 Wame manehkesit sawohwhont kehtahsootumwog ne ut, wompiyeup onatuh koon ut Salmonut.
68.15 OOwadchoom God ogquinneunkquat Bashane wadchuut, kussuhkoiyeue wadchu onatuh Bashane wodchu.
68.16 Tohwaj quesishaokq, kenau kussuhkoaiyeue wadchuash? {yeu ne} wadchu God kodtantog ootohkenat, nux, Jehovah na pish ootahken micheme.
68.17 Wuttatuppequanumukaash God nesnehchage muttannunkanuooash, nux muttanonkanogkussuog angelsog: Jehovah ukkunukapoomuh {neane} ut Sinai, ut wunetupantamwe aiyeuonkanit.
68.18 Koowaape uspep, kummussinohteap mussunohkontuonk; kuttatumunumup magooonkash wutche wosketompaog; nux, wonk wutche chekehtogik, onk woh Jehovah Manit oowechiyeumuh.
68.19 Wunnanumunnaj Lord, noh asekesukokish weahsehhikqueog {nashpe oonenehhoowaonkash}; {nux} wadchanuwae num-Manittoomun. Selah.
68.20 Noh wa-Manittoomeog, wadchanuae Manittoooo; kah pohquahhamooonkash wutch nuppooonkanit wutchiyeumooash Jehovah Godut.
68.21 Qut God pish chacheuhtahham ummatwomoh uppuhkuhkoo: {kah} wuhhatteaontip noh kodchittoshat ut ummatcheseonkanit.
68.22 Lord unnoowop, pish nukquishkeahuam wutch Bashan, pish wonk nuppasoowoog {nummissinninnumog} wutch kehtahhane moonoiyeuut:
68.23 Onk woh kusseet quogkunosu ut ooshqueheonkanooout kum-matwomog, {kah} wenanu kuttiog ne ut.
68.24 Naumuppaneg kuttaonkash, woi God, {nux} wuttaonkash num-Manittoom, nuk-Kehtahsootumoom, ut wunnetuppantamwakamukqut.
68.25 Ketoohomaeninuog nekonshopaneg, puhpequaeninuog wuttassuhkauoopah; ukkunnukiyeumowopaneg penompaog pahpequontogupaneg timbrelsash.
68.26 Wunnanumoohk God ut mukkuneonkannit, {nux} Lord wutch Israele tohkekamuit.
68.27 Na {wuttapin} pesisooe Benjamin {weche} wunnanawunnuaeninumoouh, Judahe sontimoog {kah} ukkenoosoowaeninnumoouh, Zebulune sontimoog, kah Naphtalie sontimoog.
68.28 Kummannittoom annootamup kummenuhkesuonk: munnehkehtauush, woi God, ne aseansheogup.
68.29 Newutche kuttempleoom ut Jerusalem, Kehtahsootumwog pish kuppatunkquog magooonkash.
68.30 Aiuskom chupwishae wakonnukkehtoohwhekonacheg, monacheg bullsog, weche calfse missinninuog, napajeh {nishnoh pasuk} wuttaquabehhonat wohhoguh nashpe kodchuhkakish Silver: sewah missininuog wekontamwontogig mattompog.
68.31 Sontimoog pish suhhomwog wutch Egypt, Ethiopia pish teanuk summogunum wunnitchegash en Godut.
68.32 Ketoohomohk God, kenau ohkee assootumooonkash: Woi waenomae unnoohomohk Lord, Selah:
68.33 Noh naiyeumukquit onkawe ohohtag kesuk, ne nanekoneyeuukup; kusseh, suhwe annootam oowadtauatunkquissooonk, {kah ne} mishe mushontoowaonk.
68.34 Sampooak ummunehkesuonk God: ukqunuhquisooonk aneuhkonk Israel, kah ummunehkesuonk ohteau mattohqussit.
68.35 Woi God, kuttuhquenunkquis wutch koonetuppantamwe aiyeuonkash: um-Mannittomoh Israel noh nakum maguk menuhkesuonk kah tapunumooonk en ummissinninumut: wunnanumunnaj God.
69.0
69.1 Wadchaneh, woi God, newutche nippeash petutteomooash nukketeahogkonit.
69.2 Nupwohkehchooam moonoiyeue pussogquanit, matta woh adt nepooomuk: nuppeom moonopagwut, uttuh adt nuhkuhkqsun.
69.3 Nusauunum nashpe nummauonk, nukquttunk nunnohteau: nuskesukquash sauunumoomooash ne papahtissuwonog num-Mannittoom.
69.4 Nag tohnooche sekeneaitcheg, anue monaog onk nuppuhkuhquash: nag kod-nushukqueoneg tohnooche wamatwomweoneg, menuhkesuog: neit nunnompinumup ne matta nemunumoouhp.
69.5 Woi God, koowahteo nummattammogooonk; kah nummatcheseonkash matta kuttassompattamoounash.
69.6 Nag pahtissuonukqueaneg, woi Lord God wattiyeuwehteomit ahhontanooonkash, ahque ogkodchhettich wutche nen: nag natinneahhukqueaneg, ahque chepshanunnaj wutche nen, woi um-Mannittoomoh Israel.
69.7 Newutche, wutche ken nunniyeutamup ushpunatuonk: Ogkodchuonk pattoghumup nuskesuk.
69.8 Nuppenoowohteau en nematut, kah nunnoahteaeninnu wutch noohkas wunnechonut.
69.9 Newutche kussop-wommontomooonk Kek nummahchuppooonuk; kah wutushpunnamuwaonkanoo nag ashpunamukqueaneg, nuppinishshoqunash.
69.10 Ne mauon, kah matta metsue {ahhohpahog} nukketeahogkou, ne nunnashppuhpunnamitteanap.
69.11 Wonk nuttogkoonuhkouomp nohhog munnootionag: kah nuttushpunamooonkannuup en wohhogaout.
69.12 Nag apehpaneg squontamut, nummamatche unnukuppaneg; kah nashpoohhumopaneg nohhog kakesippamwaeninuog.
69.13 Qut nen, kuppeuhtamauush, woi Jehovah, ut tapinnoatue ohquompiyeuut: Woi God, ut mishe kummonaneteaonkanut nootah, ut wunnummuhkitteyeue koowadchanuwaonkanit.
69.14 Pohquahwusseh wutch wunnumwiyeuut, kah ahque quttauwetuh: pohquahwunnitteatuh wutch nag sekinniitcheg, kah wutch moonopogqut.
69.15 Nippee tommogkon ahque nuhkuhkonkquttuh, kah moonoi ahque musashquonukquttuh, kah ahque pahsahtheg kupwamitch ut wuttoonit.
69.16 Nootah, woi Jehovah, newutche koowammoahsuonk wunnekin: quishkish en nohhogat neanag mataanuhkish kuttumonteaniteae monanitteaonkash.
69.17 Kah ahque attahtauish kuskesuk wutch kuttinninneumut, newutche nootamehpunam: teanuk nootah.
69.18 Pasoosuhkau nukketeahogkou, kah pohquahwhis: pohquahwhuseh newutche nummatwomog.
69.19 Koowahteop nuttushpunnamitteaonk, kah nuttogkodchuonk, kah nummeshannanumitteaonk: wame nummatwomog {appuog} anuhquabean.
69.20 Ushpunatuonk poohqunumup nuttah; kah nunnumwapehtunk tohkequnnooonk: kah nunnattauompamomp {howan} woh nohtunkinneiit, kah {na} wanne howan; kah wutche manehtimoowacheg, qut wanne howan nunnamehhomp.
69.21 Wonk nuttahsamukuppaneg weswe noomechiminneat, kah kukkuttoonon nootattamhukupaneg seanuppog.
69.22 Wuttableoomoo ahpehhanuitch anuhquabhittit: kah {ne woh} waniyeuontamwehhitteuhp nahshattekannuitch.
69.23 Wuskesukoowoash pogkunumoomooitch, onk woh mat namooog; kah naquahteae nunnikshahtauush wussekanahtogkoowoash.
69.24 Sookunnuttau kuttuhkquantamooonk, kah muttae kummooshquantamooonk tohquinukquehhittich.
69.25 Oone-kamukkoo touohtaj, kah wekoowout howan aiehkich
69.26 Newutche nooswehtahwhaog noh sasamukkuhwhadt, kah kehpunnamaog kunnoochumwehtahwhomog.
69.27 Kootinnehtauush matcheseonk en ummatcheseonkanoo: kah ahque petutteahittich kussampwesuonkanit.
69.28 Nag cheskwhunnach wutch pomantamwaeninyeue wussuhwhonkanit, kah ahque wetsuhkwhishittich sampweseaeninyeuut.
69.29 Qut nen nummatchek, kah nunnooantamweyeu: koowadchanuwaonk, woi God, qunnuhquapehhukquttuh.
69.30 Pish nowawenotum oowesuonk God nashpe unnoohomaonk, kah pish nummisheh nashpe waenomuwaonk.
69.31 {Yeu} wonk, pish an wussikkittahhukquit Jehovah onk neit ox asuh bullock noh wadaskonit kah wohkassit.
69.32 Manunnissitcheg {yen} pish wunnamunneau kah pish wekontamwog: kah ketahhoo pish pomontamoomoo kenau natinneawhagish God.
69.33 Newutche Jehovah nootauau matchekoooh, kah matta meshananumooo ukkuppuhshogunnosumah.
69.34 Kesuk kah ohke waenomahhittich, kehtoh, kah nishnoh teag na ut mamonchemoouk.
69.35 Newutche God pish wadchanum Sion, kah pish ootanahteau Judahe kehtootanash; onk woh na ootahkeneau, kah ootahtoonkaninneau.
69.36 Wonk wunnechonoouh wuttinninumoh pish wunnompohtunau: kah wamontogig oowesuonk na pish ootahkeneau.
70.0
70.1 {KUnnipish}, woi God, kuppohquahwhussinneat; kunnipish kuttanumiinneat, woi Jehovah.
70.2 Nag ogkodchhittich kah chepshahittich natinneawhoncheg nukketeahogkou: quishkeahhunnaj kah chepshanunnaj, kodwoskehqueoneg.
70.3 Nag quishkeahhunnaj onkquattantamunnat wuttogkodchuonkanoo, anoowacheg, Aha, aha.
70.4 Wame nag natinneahukqueaneg, mushkauantamwehhittich, kah wekontamwehhittich ut kohhogat: kah nag womontogig koowadchanuwaonk naquahteae unnoowahhittich, God mishshehhunnaj.
70.5 Qut nen nummatcheg kah nukquenawehhuk, kunnupshash en nohhogat, woi God: ken nuttanumonteaonk kah nuppohquohsuwaeninneum; woi Jehovah, ahque sepohteash.
71.1 WOi Jehovah, kuppabahtanumush, ahque nanukqut chepshannitteattuh.
71.2 Pohquahwhusseh ut kussampwesuonkanit, kah pohquohhomwahhe: ehquohtukquaehtah, kah wadchaneh.
71.3 Ken munnuhkukkamukkooish wutche nen, uttiyeu woh naquahteae nontshotam: kuttannoohteamup noowadchanitteanat, newutche ken nukqussukquanum kah noowohkonoos.
71.4 Pohquahwusseh, woi num-Mannittoom, wutch wunnitchekonut matchetoo, wutch wunnitchekanut noh matta sampwesit, kah noh uhkpunnohteat.
71.5 Newutche ken nuttanoosuonk, woi Lord God: ken nuppabahtantamooonk wutch nooskeninnuneat.
71.6 Nashpe ken nukkakokakannunnitteap wutch otomukaut: ken noh namunneohp wutch noohkas wunnogkusset: pish naquahteae koowowaenomish.
71.7 Neyaneyeu muhchantamooonkanit en monaog; qut ken nummunehke tashpuhhoowakamuk.
71.8 Nuttoon numwohtaj koowaenomitteaonk, kah nashpe kukquehtianumitteaonk quinne kesuk.
71.9 Ahque pakeseh kuhchiyeueon: ahque nukkahseh nummunehkesuonk mahchemoouk.
71.10 Newutche nummatwomog nummatcheunukquog: kah nag ashkuhwhonocheg nukketeahogkou, moeu kenoonittuog.
71.11 Noowaog, God wuttahquanumuh: wunnomattehthook kah tohqunoohk; newutche matta woh howan pohquohwhunukkoo.
71.12 Woi God, ahque nooosuhkah: woi num-Mannittoom kunnippe anunumah.
71.13 Chepshahhittitch, kah mahtuppa[e]hhittitch, nag matwaitcheg en nukketeahogkonut: Ogquehhittitch ushpannatuonk kah meshannantuonk, {nag} kod woskehhukqueoneg.
71.14 Qut nen pish naquahteae nuttoianoos, kah pish nano koowowaenomush.
71.15 Nuttoon pish nahtehteomoo koonomwaeseonk, kah-koowadchanuwaonk quinne kesuk: newutche matta noowahteoooh toh adtahshik.
71.16 Pish nummonchem ut ummunehkesuonkanit Lord Jehovah: pish nummisham kussampweusseonk, {nux} wepe ne wataiheean.
71.17 Woi God kukkakokuhkootummaiup wutch nooskeninnessuinneat: kah you toh pache noowowahtauwahhuwam kummuhchantamwe anuhkosuwonkash.
71.18 Wonk yeuyeu kakuhchiyeueon, kah wompuhquaon, woi God, ahque ohquanumeh-napache nunnahtuhkonat kummunehkesuonk en yeu pometuonkanit, kah kuttapunumooonk en nishnoh pasuk pish assuhkoeyeuit.
71.19 Wonk koonomwaeseonk, woi God, ahche qunnuhquohteau ken mashanuhkoseohp: woi God, howan anunkquean?
71.20 {Ken} nahtisseohp mishshe kah uhque wuttamehpunnaonkash, pish wonk kukketeaheh, kah kussuhhoowusseh wonk wutch ohkee moonoiyeuut.
71.21 Pish kukkootinnehteo nummissukkenooonk, kah kuttapheh waene.
71.22 Pish wonk koowaenomush nashpe Psaltery, {nux} koonomwaonk, woi God; pish kukketoohomauush nashpe harp woi OOnetuppantamoomoh Israel.
71.23 Nussistoonash pish mishshe wekontammoomooash ketoohomauunon: kah nukketeahogkou pohquahwhunnohp.
71.24 Kah nenan pish wonk kekuttoohkontamoomoo kussampweusseonk quinne kesuk: newutche chepshok {kah} ogkodchheog nag kod woskehikqueoneg.
72.0
72.1 UNnunumau kehtahsoot, koosittumooonkash, woi God, kah koonomwaeusseonk en kehtahsoot wunnamonut.
72.2 Noh pish wussumau kummissinninnumog nashpe sampweusseonk, kah kummatchekoomog nashpe wussuttumooonk.
72.3 Wadchuash pish pattooomooash wunnohteaonk en missinninuut, kah wadchuemesash, nashpe wunnomwaeseonk.
72.4 Pish wussumau matchekoooh ut missinninuut, pish wadchonau wunnechonoouh quenawehqutcheh, kah pish sukquishshanau noh uhkpunnahteadt.
72.5 Nag pish kukqushukquog toh sahke nuppauzaik, kah nahneposhataik, panuppe wame pometuonkanash
72.6 Pish nookeu onatuh sookunon ut sashquonkanit: onatuh chuppunnonash napehkontammoomooukish ohke.
72.7 Ut ukkesukodumut noh sampwesit pish missetu: kah {pish} monat wunnahteaonk toh sahke nahneposhataik.
72.8 Pish wonk nanawunum wutch kehtahhanit, en kehtahhanit, kah wutch sepuut, en wahquohkeyeuukish.
72.9 Nag wadohkecheg tauohkomukqut pish nawaeog ut annuhquabit, kah ummatwomoh pish noohnooshquattamog puppussi.
72.10 Tarshishe kah munnohhane Tahsootumog pish patoog magoonkash; Shebae kah Sebae, Tahsootumog pish magooog magooonkash.
72.11 Nux, wame kehtahsootumog pish nawaeog ut anuhquabit: wame wuttahtimoinnunk pish wuttinninneumuhkunk.
72.12 Newutche noh pish pohquahwhunau quenawehhikqutcheg mauwunitcheh: matcheku wonk, kah noh matta watanunossueninneumit.
72.13 Noh pish wohquanumau matchekuoh kah quenawehhikqutcheg, kah pish wadchonau ukketeahogkonoowuh quanawehhikqutcheg.
72.14 Pish pohquohwhunau ukketeahogkonoowuh wutch assookohkodteamooonkanit & chekeunnehtuonkanit: & ooshquehheonkanoo pish mishshoadtumoo ut anuhquabit.
72.15 Kah noh pish pomantam, kah Shebae gold pish ununamauon: pish wonk naquahteae peuhtamwanushau, kah pish asekesukohkish waenomou.
72.16 Na pish yonnitchaminyeuoo ut ohkeit woskeche wodchuuhkontu; mechummuonk naut pish nunnukishomoo onatuh Lebanon, kah nag wadohkecheg kehtootannat pish missetuog onatuh ohkee askasquash.
72.17 OOwesuonk pish michemohteau: oowesuonk pish oiuhhontsohteau toh sahke nuppauzaik: kah wosketompaog pish wunnanumoog ut wohhogat; wame wuttohtimoinash pish wuttissoowenouh wunnanumukqussu.
72.18 Wunnanumunnaj Jehovah Mannit um-Mannittomoh Israel, noh wepe aseet muhchantamweyeuukish.
72.19 Kah wunnantamunnaj sohsumooe oowesuonk micheme, kah mamusse ohke numwohtaj wussohsumooonk: Amen kah amen.
72.20 Uppeuhtamooonkash David wunnamonoh Jesse wohkuhquohshinash.
73.0
73.1 WUnnumuhkit God wunneetoo en Israelut, en pahketeahhoncheg.
73.2 Qut nen, nussetah aomog panushopash: nuttontannehtuonkash passittouwe toonukquishinuppash.
73.3 Newutche nutteskaonomp assookitcheg, naumon oonuhkommaiaonkanoo matchetukig.
73.4 Newutche wanne wehwe puppisseog ut wunnuppooonkanoowout: qut ummunehkesuonkanoo munnuhki.
73.5 Matta wuttamehpunoooog neane {onkatogik} wosketompaog: asuh matta unehtahwhoog neane {onkatogik} wosketompaog.
73.6 Newutche pehtuanumooonk wenuhkunkquog neane moouhshogquohtog: onkhukquog chekeusseonk onatuh ogkooonkanit.
73.7 Kogkontehchukquaog nashpe wunnogkooonk: anuetuontamog muttahhe kottantamooonk.
73.8 Aninwog, kah mamatcheyeuog {papaume} uhkpunahteaonk: pehtuwaog.
73.9 Poonumog wuttoonoo ayeuuhkone kesukquash: kah wenanu pannupwuhshomoo- ohke.
73.10 Newutche ummissinninnumoh, yeu en quishkenit: kah numwohtae nippeash senumauoneau.
73.11 Kah nag noowaog, uttuh God wuttinwahtauun? kah sun apehtunk wahteoonk anue quanuhquabit?
73.12 Kusseh, yeug matchetooog waniitcheg ut muttaohket, nag onchenaetuog.
73.13 Wunnumuhkit nuppahkehteop nuttah tahnooche, kah nukkissenitchap ut pahkesuonkanit.
73.14 Newutche quinnekesuk nuttuhkuppunnanit, kah nussahsamuhkouwhit ase mahtompohkish.
73.15 Unnoowaon, yeu pish nuttinoowon: kusseh woh nummatchenehteoh uppometuonkanoo kunnechonog.
73.16 Yeu kod wahtauon, nunnuhkoompattamunnap.
73.17 Napache nuttomp oonetuppantamwakamukqut God, {neit} noowohtamup oowohkuhquoiyeumoo.
73.18 Wunnummuhkit nag kuppoonoog toonukquiyeuonkanut: nag kuppunnuhkonog en pagquannuonkanit.
73.19 Nag toh en taiadche konkewoiyeuehheog? nag papukqunne mahtuppanok nashpe siaskishshanittuonkash.
73.20 Onatuh unnukquomooonk tohkemukish; woi Lord, toohkean, ne pish kuttinne meshannantamun wuttinsuonkanoo.
73.21 Yeu nuttine seantamwuttahhonnap, kah nukkanukkehtahwhitteap ut nuttoounnissit.
73.22 Yeu nittine ahsookinneah, kah matta noowohwohtamooonkanip: nuttogquinneunkquissip puppinashimwut ut anuhquabean.
73.23 Qut onch, naquahteae koowetomush: kuttaninnip nuttinuhkonit.
73.24 Pish kussompshaseh nashpe kukkunnoosoowaonk, kah ompehtag kuttattumineh en sohsumooonkanit.
73.25 Howan wadtihee ut kesukqut {wepe ken}? kah matta howan nutahchuanumoh ut ohkeit wepe ken.
73.26 Sauunumoomoo nooweyaus kah nuttah: {qut} God nuttahhe munnehkesooonk, kah nutchuppioom micheme.
73.27 Newutche kusseh, nag nooosukkunkqueaneg, pish pagquannuog: kuppagquannog wame nag mamositcheg wutch kohhogat.
73.28 Qut wunnegin wutche nen nuppasoosuhkauonat God: nuppabahtanumop Lord Jehovah, onk woh nuttontuttumunash wame kuttanuhkosuonkash.
74.0
74.1 WOi God, tohwache amauhkoseog micheme? {Tohwaj} kummooshquantamooonk pukkuttauk ayeuuhkone chippinnutunkane kuttissheepsumog?
74.2 Mehquantash kummukkinneonk noadt taphumohp: sauopuhquame kuttahtoonk {ne} mannoohhumohp, yeu wadchu Sion ne wadohkeohp.
74.3 Tahshinish kissetash en naquahteaiyeue konkewoiyeuonkanit: {nux} wame ne matwau ane matcheussehp ut winnetuppantamwakamukqut.
74.4 Kummatwomog neskehtunkqussuog ut noeu kummukkinneonkash: nepattoog ummittaakunnoowoash wutche kukkinneasuonkash.
74.5 Wosketomp inne mushanumop uttoh ane tahshunukup togkunkash ut kuppuhquhkodut.
74.6 Qut yeuyeu nukquitehteowe nooketahhamog monsuhkwhosue anuhkosuonkash naut, nashpe togkunkash kah hammersash.
74.7 Unnuhteopaneg noohteau koonetuppantamwakamukqut, nesketeopaneg nashpe {uppunuhteaonkanoo} ootahtuonk koowesuonk en ohkehkontu.
74.8 Unnoowopaneg ut wuttahhoowout, Nag pagquanontuh moaeu: nag mahchuhkussumog wame uppeuhtamwakamukquash God ut ohkeut.
74.9 Matta nunnamoomun nukkehkinneasuonkanunnonash, wanne quahshotumwaeninyeunoowi, asuh matta howan kunnukke nenawun noh wahtunk tohsahkee.
74.10 Woi God, tohsohkee pish matwau ushpunnamuau? sun pish matwau mamatcheuttam koowesuonk micheme?
74.11 Tohwache wuttontunnuman kunnitcheg, nux kuttinuhkou? kodtunush wutch kuppoochenauonut.
74.12 Newutche God nukkehtohsootumoom wutch noadt, wadchanuae anuhkosu ut noeu ohkeit.
74.13 Kutchachapunumup kehtah nashpe kummunehkesuonk: kuppoohquehtahham uppuhkuhkoowoash pootopaog ut nippehkontu.
74.14 Kussukquontuppohtahhop Leviathan, kah noh kummakunnap metsuonkannuinneat wutche missinninnuog wadtahkecheg tauohkamukqut.
74.15 Kuppuhshehtahhamup tohkekam kah tommog: kunnunnapehtop kussutchuwanne sepuash.
74.16 Kesukod kuttaihe, nuhkan wonk kutaihe: kukquahshawehteop wequai kah nupauz.
74.17 Koonahtop nish noh an wehkqshik ohke: kuttiimunapash kussuttau kah puppoon.
74.18 Mehquantash yeu, matwau ushpunnamuwop, woi Jehovah, kah ahsootue missinninnuog mamatcheuttamuppaneg koowesuonk.
74.19 Woi ahque magish ukketeahogkonoh turtlee-kooskuhwhannan en monacheg {matchetukig}: ahque wannantash ummukkinneonkanoo kummatchekoomog micheme.
74.20 Wuttooantash wunnoowaonk: newutche pohkunae aiyeuonkash ut ohkeit numwohtaash uhquanumwehhuae wuttohkeonkash.
74.21 Noh uhkpunadt, woi ahque ogkodchue quishketch: matchekoo kah quenawehhukquit waenotumwehhittitch koowesuonk.
74.22 Omohkish, woi God, kunnootamwontash nehhenwonche kuttuniyeuonk: mehquantash ahsootuenin toh ane ushpunnamukquean asekesukohkish.
74.23 Ahque wanantash oowadtauatunkquissuonkanoo kummatwomog: oowogkoueonkanoo nag aiyeuohkone waapehtunkqueaneg, nano mussi naquahteae
75.0
75.1 KUttabattontumauunumun, woi God; nuttabattantumumun: newutche kummuhchantamwe anuhkosuonkash unnoowomooash koowesuonk paswohteau.
75.2 Attumunnumon mukkunneonk, pish nussampwe wussuttum.
75.3 Ohke kah wame na watohkecheg saupaseuk: nukkogkonunum wunnepattuhquonkash. Selah.
75.4 Nuttunomp assookitcheg, Ahque assooke oussek, kah matchetooog, Ahque tahshunumook askon.
75.5 Qunnuhque tahshunumoohteog kuttaskonoo; kekuttoohkuhteog nashpe chetoue mussittippeg.
75.6 Newutche mushehhittuonk mat wumoounoo wompanniyeu asuh puhtadtuniyeu asuh souaniyeu.
75.7 Qut God wussuttumwaenin, noh nookunnau pasukooh, kah tahshunau onkatogeh.
75.8 Newutche wunnitchegannut Jehovah ahteau wuttattamwaetch, kah ne wine mishqui, numwae kunnittippannosu, onk ne na ootsookunumun: qut ne sakuppahshunk wame matchetukig ut ohkeit pish wussenuppanumunneau, kah ootattamunneau.
75.9 Qut nen pish nunnonahtehteam micheme: pish wawenomae nukketoohomau um-Mannittoomoh Jacob.
75.10 Wame wutaskonnoouh matchetooog pish nuttumuhtahhamunash: qut wutaskonnoouh sampwesitcheg pish tashunumunash.
76.0
76.1 GOD wahheou ut Judah: oowesuonk mussi ut Israelut.
76.2 Onk wek ohteau Salem, kah ootahkeonk Sionut.
76.3 Na wuttut poohqunnumunapash ohtompee kouhquatash, ogquinneg, kah togkodteg, kah ayeutuonk. Selah.
76.4 Kuttanue sohsum, {kah} mamuttanis onk mukkookinnuontamwe wadchooash.
76.5 Manehkittahhoncheg woskehheog, koueog ukkaueonkanoo: kah matta howae munnehkesuenin namehtau wunnitchegash.
76.6 Aiuskomuwaan, woi um-Mannittoomoh Jakob, naneswe tatuppequanumuk kah hors nuppooe koueohheoog.
76.7 Ken, ken woh kukquishit; kah howan woh nepauit anuhquabean, tohannooh mooshquantaman?
76.8 Kunnootomwahuwop wussuttumooonk wutch kesukqut; muttaohke wapissumoop kah chequnohtop.
76.9 Ne omohket God en wussuttumooonkanit, wadchononat wame manunnissuoh ut ohkeit. Selah.
76.10 Wunnummuhkit ummooshquantamooonk wosketomp pish koowawenomuk: ne asqueyeuuk mooshquantamooonk pish kootamwehtauun.
76.11 Quashomoohk, kah oadtuhkohk Jehovah kum-Mannittoomoo; wame nag weinapehtunkquitcheh patauahhittitch magooonkash noh woh quahshit.
76.12 Noh pish tummussum wunnahshauonkanoo sontimmoog: noh uhquinneunkqussu en ohkee kehtasootumwut.
77.0
77.1 NUmmauunnittauop God nashpe noowadtauohtunkqussuonk: {nux} en Godut nashpe noowadtauohtunkqussuonk, kah nukkehketunkup.
77.2 Ut nootamehpunae kesukodut nunnatinneahhomp Jehovah: nukkechesooonk pummitchoowanup nuhkonae, kah matta ahquenoop: nukketeahogkou sekinneamup tapehhonat.
77.3 Numehquanumop God, nootamantamup: nootoowop, kah nunnahshauonk nukkonchoowanup. Selah.
77.4 Kuppaquissuohto nuskesukquash: nuttunukkuhque wuttammantam matta nuttapunnumooh ketoohkon.
77.5 Nunnatwontamup noadt kesukodash, noohquompae kodtumooash.
77.6 Nummehquantam nuhkonae nuttinoohomaonk: nukkekuttookonan nehenwonche nuttah, kah nunnahshauonk wuttooatinehteop.
77.7 Sun pish Lord micheme pogkesoowau? kah sun pish matta kooche monanteooo?
77.8 Sun ukkuttummonteanitteaonk papaquanne ammaemoo micheme? sun ukquahshomuaonk micheme panishau?
77.9 Sun God wannantam monanukkonat? sun mooshquantamwe kuppohhom nohtonteannitteae ukkuttumonteanitteaonkash? Selah.
77.10 Kah nissip, yeu nunnoochummesuonk: qut pish nummehquantam unnunnuhkone ukkodtumoomash anue Quanuhquapit.
77.11 Pish nummehquontam wuttanuhkosuonkash Jehovah: wunnummuhkit pish nummehquantam noadt kummuhchantamooonkash.
77.12 Pish wonk nunnatwantam wame kuttannuhkosuonk, kah nooweogquttum kutusseonkash
77.13 Kmmay, woi God, wunnetuppantamwekamukqut ohteau: howae mannit wuttinukkenun ne anukkenuk num-Mannittoomun?
77.14 Ken noh God muhchantamwe aseet: koowahtauwahhoowop kummunehkesuonk kunnukke missinninnuut.
77.15 Kuppahquohwhunomp kummissinninnumog nashpe kuhpit, wunnamonuh Jakob kah Joseph. Selah.
77.16 Nippeash kunnoqunnapash, woi God, nippeash kunnoqunapash: nash wapissoomoopash; wonk moonoiyeuash wuttamantamoopash.
77.17 Mattohkqusash sookunnumupash nippeash, kesukquash kuttoowomooupash: kukkouhquatash wonk suhwhushshopash.
77.18 Ukkutoowaonkanoo kunneampomog tannoowomooup kesukqut: ukkutshamin wequasumoomooup muttaohk, ohke nunnukshomooup kah quequanup.
77.19 Kummay kehtahhanit ohteau, kah kuppummayeam masag nippeit, kah kuttontanehtuonkash matta wahteooounash.
77.20 Kuppummuwunomp kummissinninnuog onatuh chupwushae-sheepsut, nashpe wunnitcheg Moses, kah Aaron
78.0
78.1 WOi nummissinninnumog, kehhehtamook nuttinomatuonk: ahchusittamook nuttoone kuttooonkash.
78.2 Noowoshwunum nuttoon ut kuhkinneasuonkanit: nummushom nupwoaonkash nanekoneyeuukuppash:
78.3 Nesh nootamogupash kah wahtauogupash; kah noohshunnonog anukqueogupash.
78.4 Matta nuttattahtooounnanonash wutch wunnechonoowout, {pish} nunnahtinnonanonash pometuonk paomoouk, waenomaonkash Jehovah, kah ummenuhkesuonk, kah ummuhchantamwe anuhkosuonkash nesh asehpash.
78.5 Newutche munnehkehteooop wawaonk ut Jakob, kah kuhquttumup unnomatuonk ut Israel, uttiyeu annoonohp koohshunnonog; onk woh nesh wunnahtunnoneau wunnechonoowooh.
78.6 Pometuonk paomoouk woh {nish} oowahtouunaout, {nux} mukkiog neg woh nekitcheg: onk woh wapeog kah nish wunnahtuhkonaoash en wunnechonoowout.
78.7 Onk woh annoonaog God, kah matta wannantamooog wuttanuhkosuonkash Mannit; qut woh nanaehtoog wuttannoohteamooonkash.
78.8 Kah matta unauwoooog oohshoowuh, chetuwe kah chekehtamwe pometuonk; pometuonk matta sampwohtoookig wuttohhoo; kah wunnahshauonkanoo matta chetammanookup weche God.
78.9 Tapauwamue kah nemohtompae wunnechonoh Ephraim, quehchiphoowopaneg ut aiyeuwuttue kesukkodut.
78.10 Matta nanawehtooopaneg oonnowaonk God, kah chekewe matta ussupaneg wuttinomatuonk.
78.11 Kah wunnantamuppaneg wuttanuhkosuonkash, kah ummuhchantamoomash: nesh nahtunuhpash.
78.12 Muhchantamooonkash usseup ut anuhquapinnit ooshoowuh: ut Egypte ohkeit, ut Zoane ahteuhkonut.
78.13 Puhshunumup kehtah, kah nah uppanupwushahheuh: kah nepattauwahteop nippe onatuh kodtunkquag.
78.14 Kesukkodae wonk uppummuwunopah nashpe mattahqus: kah quinnittuppuhquae nashpe wequanae noohteau.
78.15 Passehthamup qussukquanash ut tauohkamukqut: kah nah ootattamheopah neane wutch mishshe moonoiyeuut.
78.16 Wonk suhwuttoup kussitchoowanash wutch qussukquanut, kah unnitchuwanehteop nippeash onatuh sepuash.
78.17 Kah nag nano ummomatche unnehheowopah, nashpe ummooshquehhaonkanoo anue quanuhquapit ut tauohkamukqut
78.18 Kah quitchehheopaneg God ut wuttohhoowout, nashpe kodkodtauwontamwe oowehquttummooonkanoo meetsuonk.
78.19 Nux, kuttoohkopaneg aiyeuuhkone God: unnoowopaneg, Sun woh God wunnohto ahhuttashpumuk ut tauohkamukqut?
78.20 Kusseh, togkodtomup qussuk, onk nippeash wuttutchoowahshop, kah kussitchooanash anuonchuwahshopash; sun woh wonk magoo puttukquinneg? Sun woh nanashwunum weyaus wutche ummissinninnumoh?
78.21 Newutche Jehovah yeu wunnootamunnah, kah mooshquantamup: nemehkuh noohteau nashqunnanoseup ayiyeuohkone Jakob, kah mooshquantamooonk, aiyeuuhkone waapehtunkup Israel.
78.22 Newutche matta wunnomuhtamoopaneg ut Godut: kah matta pabahtamoopaneg oowadchanuwaonk:
78.23 Tokonogque wuttanootamunapash mattohqussash wutch waape, kah oowoshwunumunapash kesukque usquontamash:
78.24 Kah wussookunonuhkouopah manna woh ummechunaout, kah wuttununumauopah kesukque eahchiminneash.
78.25 Wosketomp mechoop angelsog ummechumoo: nekuhchehhuwop nah en metsuonk en wamuppinneat.
78.26 Wutchepwoshinehteop ut mamahchekesukqut: kah nashpe ummenuhkesuonk patoup sowanishin.
78.27 Wussookunonuhkauopah wonk weyaus onatuh puppussi: kah mequnne puppinushaog onatuh kehtahhanomuhk.
78.28 Uppinishahtauun ut noeu wuttuppuhkussunooonkanoowout, quaqunnippe wekoowout.
78.29 Onk metsupaneg, kah ahche wamuppoopaneg: newutche wuttununumauopah nehenwonche ukkodtantamooonkanoo.
78.30 Matta penushehtamoopaneg ukkogkodtauontamooonkanoo: qut as ummechumoo aohtakup wuttoonoowout,
78.31 Ummooshquantamooonk God nuhkuhkonkuppaneg, kah {ne} wunnishukqunaop nekonukkomwehpaneg, kah ukkepehtuhqunaop pepenauutcheg ut lsrael.
78.32 Qut onch momatche osupaneg: kah matta wunnomehtamoopaneg wutche wame muhchantammoe wuttanuhkosuonkash.
78.33 Newutche mahtuppanumup ukesukodtumoowoash ut tohnoocheyeuoout, kah ukkodtumoowoash ut wuttamehpunaonkanit.
78.34 Nah nahshont, neit wunnatinneahukkuppah: kah quishkoopaneg, kah nompoae nattoomopaneg Godoh.
78.35 Onk mequantamuppaneg God nah ukqussukquanumoouh: kah quanuhquapit Mannit uppohquahwussuwaeninyeumoouh.
78.36 Qut onch, oowawunonuhkumowopah nashpe wuttoonoo: kah uppanoowae unnouwoopah nashpe wenanuwoash.
78.37 Newutche wuttohhoo matta sompwanoop noh weche, kah matta munnehtukkompooopaneg ut oonoowaonkanut.
78.38 Qut numwapehtunkup kuttummonteanitteaonk, ohquontamup ummatcheseonkanoowoash, kah matta uppaquanopah; nux, moochekit nompe puttukkinumup ummooshquantamooonk, kah matta wogkouunnumoop wame ummoashquantamooonk.
78.39 Newutche mehquantamup nag {wepe} weyausuooog; wapan ne pamuhshonk, kah matta wonk paomunook.
78.40 Uttoh tahshit ummomoohmooshquehhowoopah ut tauohkamukqut, kah wunnonoowehheowoopah ut touweyeuut?
78.41 Nux, quishkoopaneg, kah quitchehheopaneg Godoh, kah kogkahteanumopaneg OOnetupantamoomoh Israel.
78.42 Matta mehquantamoopaneg wunnitcheg, asuh kesukod adt pohquohwhunuhp wutch matwaut.
78.43 Uttoh ananuhkoseph ukkehkinneasuonkash ut Egypt, kah ummuhchantamooonkash ut Zoane ahtuhkonit.
78.44 Kah qunnuppunumup wussepumoowoash en wishquehhunkanit; kah wuttommogkonoomoowoash, onk matta tapunnumoopaneg wuttattamunat.
78.45 Annoonop iane unnissuoh moosuhquoh nag en kunnuke, uttuh moohhukquehhitteuhp; kah mahmoskohteaseuh, nah pogquanukhitteup.
78.46 Wonk magoop ummechumooonkanoo en moopaut, kah wuttanuhkosuonkanoo en chonsompsut.
78.47 Uppaquattouunapash oowenomissippagoowoash nashpe mussekon, kah Sycomoree-ummehtukkoomoooash nashpe toohp.
78.48 Magoop wonk uppuppinashimoomoouh en mussekonut, kah ufflockumoouh en ukkutshaminnit.
78.49 Wunnuhkehtohwhopah kussaputtae ummoshquantamooonk, uhque mooshquantamooonk, kah uhquontamooonk kah wuttamantamooonk; nashpe wuttanoonaonk matche angelsog {nah kunnuke}.
78.50 Mayehteop en ummooshquantamooonkanit, matta wohquanumooop ukketeahogkonoo wutch nuppooonkanit: qut magup ukketeaonkanoo en uhque unninneaonkanit.
78.51 Kah nushop wame mohtammekinnitcheh ut Eygpt: nakoneyeuuk ummunehkesuonkanoo ut wekash Ham:
78.52 Qut nehenwonche ummissinninnumoh wuttogque sohhoowunnopah sheepsut, kah wuttogque sompshanopah ut touohkomukqut onatuh flockut.
78.53 Kah nanouiyeue wussompshanopah, onk mat wapissupaneg: qut kehtah wunnuhkuhkunkqunnaop ummatwomoouh.
78.54 Kah uppasoowopah uhquae oonetupantamwe aiyeuonkanit, en yeu wadchuut, wuttunuhkou taphukup.
78.55 Wonk sohwhohteop penoowohteaoh ut anaquapehhittit, kah wutchatchapunumauopah, ohtoonk nashpe kuhkunonk, kah wuttahkeahhop Israele chuppanooonkash ut wekoowout.
78.56 Onch qutchehheopaneg kah moohmooshquehheopaneg anue quanuhquapit Mannit; kah matta nanauwehteooopaneg oowawaonkash:
78.57 Qut quishkeupaneg, kah matta pabahtantamwe usseupaneg onatuh ooshoouh: penishshishopaneg onatuh pemishque ohtompeit.
78.58 Newutche ummoohmooshquehhoopah nashpe ukqunnuhque aiyeuonkanoowoash; kah ummoossitteamoowahheowoopah nashpe monussosue wuttinneuhkontunkanoowoash.
78.59 Yeu notog God, mooshquantamup, kah mishshe cheshanumop Israeloh:
78.60 Nemehkuh wunnukkodtumunap Shiloe wuttohkeonk, wuttohkeakamuk ne ponukup kunnukke wosketompaut:
78.61 Kah magoop ummunehkesuonk en mussinnaunneat, kah wussohsumooonk en matwaog wunnitchekonoowout.
78.62 Magoop wonk ummissinninnumoh en togkodteganit: kah mooshquantamooontamup wuttahtoonk.
78.63 OOskeninnumoouh noohteau ummahchukkisukqunaop; kah uppenompomoouh matta wetawatheooopaneg
78.64 Wussephausuenumoouh punnishopaneg nashpe togkodteg: kah wussekouushquomoouh matta mauemoopaneg
78.65 Neit Lord toohkoop neane noh tohket wutch koueonkanit; kah ogque munehkesueninnuut noh sashquohhukquit wine.
78.66 Kah annehtahwhop ummatwomoh ut wuttammiyeuut: um-micheme ushpunnamuwaheopah.
78.67 Kah wonk, sekinneamup wek Joseph: kah matta pepenamoop wutchupanooonk Ephraim.
78.68 Qut pepenamup wutchupanooonk Judah, kah Sione wadchu ne wamontogup.
78.69 Kah wuttinukkomukquehkonap oonetuppantamwakamuk onatuh quanuhquakish aiyeuonkash, onatuh ohke ne manehkehtunkup micheme.
78.70 Wonk pepenouop Davidoh wuttinninnumoh, kah wunnemunopah wutch sheepse chippinnutunkanit:
78.71 OOsoowopah wutch ahsuhkouaonkanit wompukquaunehpah, en sohkomoononat ummissinninnumoh Jakob kah wuttahtoonk ut Israel.
78.72 Onk wussohkommoonopah neanag uppannipwuttahhaonk: kah wussompwusshanopah nashpe wunnitchekane nehtuhtoonk.
79.0
79.1 WOi God, penoowohteaog peyaog kuttahtoonkanut, mahche neskehteoog wunnetuppantamwe kuttempleoom: mahche nanomunkquattoog Jerusalem.
79.2 Nuppooe wohhogauh kuttinninnumoh ummahche assomonauh mamahchekesukque pissuhksuog, kah ooweyausoo koonetuppantamoomoh en ohkee puppinashimwut.
79.3 Ooshquehhunkanoo ummache seahhamunaeu onatuh nippe quaqunnippe Jerusalem: kah na matta howanuunoop woh posuhkinukquehhittit.
79.4 Nuttishpunnomuwaonkkanumun en netahteamonkanunonut: mannauantamooonk kah aionttuhkonittuonk en nag wenuhkunkqueogkig.
79.5 Toh sohkee, Jehovah? pish kummooshquantam micheme? sun pish kummoositteamooonk ogqunneau noohtaut?
79.6 Sookunumau kummooshquantamooonk penoowohteaog matta wahukkooaneg, kah kehtahsootumooonkanit matta wehquttummookig koowesuonk.
79.7 Newutche mahchupwaog Jakoboh, kah mahche tauishinehteoog ootahkeonk.
79.8 Woi ahque aiyeuuhkone mehquantamiinnean noadt matcheseonkash: nohtonteanitteae kukkuttumonteanitteaonkash teanuk nogkuskomwahhukquttuh; newutche ahche nukkuttumunkeyeumun.
79.9 Anunumaiinnean, woi wadchanuwae num-Mannittoomun, wutche koowesuonkane sohsumooonk: kah pohquohwussinnean, kah ammapattiinnean nummatcheseonkanunonash wutche koowesuonk.
79.10 Tohwaj woh penoowohteaog unnoowahhittit, Tonoh um-Mannitoomoouh? unnoh wahinnaj kunnukke penoowohteaut ut anuhquapeog, nashpe annootauanushontamooonk ooshquehhunkanoo kuttinninnumog ne saohhosik.
79.11 Ummushanomooonk kapuhshogunut peomooutch anuhquapean, neane mussag kummunuhkesuonk: wadchan nag kahtimitcheg en nuppooonkanit.
79.12 Kah netahteamunkanunonog nesausuk tahshe pashkinumau en uppoochinauwonoowout, wuttushpunnamuwaonkanoo nag ne nashpuhpunamukquean, woi Lord.
79.13 Nemehkuh nenauun kummissinninnumog, kah chippinnutunkane sheepsog, pish kuttabattantumauunumun micheme: pish nunnahtehteamun koowawenomitteaonk en wame pometuonkash.
80.0
80.1 NOOtash, woi Israele nanawussheepsaenin, ken pamuwunadt Joseph onatuh flockut, ken wadohkean noeu cherubimsut, wohsish.
80.2 Anuhquapit Ephraim kah Benjamin kah Manasseh, wogkouunush kummunehkesuonk, kah peyash koowadchaninneanonut.
80.3 Qunnipinninnean wonk, woi God: kah wohsumwohtouush kuskesuk, kah pish noowadchanitteamun.
80.4 Woi Jehovah Mannit wattiyeuwehteomit ahhontanooonkash, toh sohkee pish kummooshquantamooontam uppeuhtamooonkanoo kummissinninnumog?
80.5 Nag kussohkommoonoog mussippequone puttukquinneg: kah moochukit kootattamheoog mussippequonash.
80.6 Kuppenoowanittuwahhumun en netahteamunkanunonut: kah nummatwomunnonog ahhanuog kunnukke wohhogaout.
80.7 Quinnippinninnean wonk, woi God wattiyeuwehteomit ahhontanooonkash, kah wahsumwahtauush kuskesuk, kah pish noowadchanitteamun.
80.8 Kussohhoowuttop wenomwussippog wutch Egypt: kussohwhohteap penoowohteaog, kah kuttohkehkonap.
80.9 Kukquashauwe mayuhkontamunap kah kukqunomae wadchapuhteuhkonap, kah numwaontuhqunnogkodtup ohke.
80.10 Ne nashpe wadchuash onkauuhtopash, kah ootuhqunumash ogqunneunkquodtupash wunnetue chukuppeit.
80.11 Unuttuhqunaekinup kehtahhanit, kah unnuppahchatuhqunaekinup sepuut.
80.12 Tohwaje kepuhkoman uppimminnutunkash, nemehkuh wame nag pamushacheg mayut wussassakishattauunau?
80.13 Boar wutch touohkomukqut wuttoiontahkodtauun, kah tauohkamukque puppinashim ummahchipwin.
80.14 Quishkish, kunnanompassumunumun, woi Mannit wattiyeuwehteomit ahhontanooonkash: womompish wutch kesukqut, kah naush, kah nuttauwohtouush yeu wenomissippog;
80.15 Kah wenominneohteuhk ne kuttunuhkou ahkehteomooukup, kah pahchatuhk ne manehkehtauohp wutche nehenwonche kohhog.
80.16 Chukkohtai nashpe noohteau, tummehtahhamunai: nag pogquanuog nashpe kuskesukque aiuskomuaonk.
80.17 Kunnitcheg apehtunkquitch kuttunuhkoniyeue wosketomp, wunnamonut wosketomp noh manehkehheohp wutche nehenwonche kohhog.
80.18 Nemehkuh pish matta kukquishkehtouunoomun, quaquahkqhinnean kah pish noowehquttumumun koowesuonk.
80.19 Quinnippinninnean wonk, woi Jehovah Mannit wattiyeuwehteomit ahhontanooonkash, wohsumwahtauush kuskesuk, kah pish noowadchanitteamun.
81.0
81.1 MIshontoowaoohhumohk God nummunehkesuonkanun. wekontamwehtunkquisseg en um-Mannittoomoh Jakob.
81.2 Nemunumook ketoohomaonk, kah pautoook timbrel, wunnontoowae harp, weche psaltery.
81.3 Kuttooanonttamook monuppehpeg wuskunnuppauzauk, ut kuhquttosue ohquompiyeuut, ut kehche mishadttuppooe nukkesukkodtumunonut.
81.4 Newutche yeu kuhkoowaonkanuup wutche Israel, kah ootinnomatuonkaninneah um-Mannittoomoh Jacob.
81.5 Yeu ukkuhquttumunnah ut Joseph wutche wauwaonk, {ne} sohhog papashpe Egypte ohkeit; {ne adt} nootamuhp unontoowaonk, ne matta wahtomoouhp.
81.6 Nuttontohtop wuttik wutch weanut: wunnitchegash pohquahwhuttosupash wutch ohkuhqut.
81.7 Koowehquttumaiip watamehpunnaan, kah kuppohquohwhununup; kunnompoohumauunup ut nempae assompamukquodtut: kukqutchhinup ut Meribahe nippeit. Selah.
81.8 Nootamook, woi nummissinninnuog, kah pish noowauwaontam en kohhogat: woi Israel, kukkehtiean;
81.9 Wanne pish kuttapehtunkkoo penoowe mannit: kah matta pish koowauwussumoh penoowe mannit.
81.10 Nen Jehovah kum-Mannittoom, noh waj suhhoowunukqueohp Egypte ohkeit: mishe woshwunush kuttoon, kah pish nunnumwohtouun.
81.11 Qut nummissinninnumog matta nukkehketunkoopaneg: kah Israel matta nuttapeneunkoop.
81.12 Nemehkuh nummagunapaneg en nehenwonche wuttohhoowae ukkogkodtauontamooonkanoowout; {kah} pomushopaneg ut nehenwonche ukkenoosoowaonkanoowout.
81.13 Napehnont nummissinninnumog nukkakehkehtunkqunnaous; kah Israel papummushas nummayut!
81.14 Woh teanuk nuttaogquapehhopaneg ummatwomoouh, kah woh nukquaqushkunumup nunnitcheg aiyeuohkone nah sekinneunkhittitcheh.
81.15 Sakinneauuhpaneg Jehovah woh teanuk wonkumooe wutaogquapehtunkuppah: qut nag wuttohquompioomoo woh mamichemohtop.
81.16 Woh wutaassomopah wonk wanegikish wheatsash: kah nashpe honey wutch qussukquanit, woh koowawamupwehhunup.
82.0
82.1 GOD nepau ummukkinneonkanoowout manehkesitcheg: wussuttum kenugke mannittooog.
82.2 Toh sohkee pish matta kussampwe wussuttumoomwoo, kah kunnekonantamumwoo wuskesukoowoash matchetooog? Selah.
82.3 Wussuttumwanushoohk matchekoo kah matta wattooshek: sampe unnehheuhk, noh uhkuhpunadt kah quanawehhikquit.
82.4 Pohquohwhunoohk matchekoo kah quanawehhukquit; {nag} suhhoowus wutch wunnitchegkanoowout matchetooog.
82.5 Matta wahteoooog, kah matta wohtamooog, yoyatushaog pohkinnaiyeuut: wame ohkee ohpohteashikish ontohtaash.
82.6 Nissip, Kenau Mannittooog: kah kenau wame wunnechonoh anue Quanuhquapit:
82.7 Qut pish kuttogque nuppumwoo wosketompaut, kah kuttogque punishomwoo howaohsootut.
82.8 Omuhkish, woi God, wussutush ohke: newutche pish kootohtoonkan wame wuttohtimoinneash.
83.0
83.1 NEtashoowohkon, woi God: kogkopussae ussehkon, kah chequnapehkon, woi Mannit.
83.2 Newutche kusseh, kummatwomog wogkouuhtunkquissuog: kah nag sekinneunkqueaneg, tashunumuppaneg muppuhkuhk.
83.3 Ompuwussue kenoonittupaneg aiyeuohkone kummissinninnumog, kah wetoowotupaneg aiyeuohkone nag adtashatcheg.
83.4 Unnoowopaneg ehoh tummehtahwhontuh, onk woh matta wuttahtimmoneog: onk woh oowesuonk Israel matta wonk mamehquantamooun.
83.5 Newutche passukquintahhae wetoowotupaneg: mahche wunnoowaog aiyeuuhkone kohhogat.
83.6 Edome, kah Jishmalitse, Moabe kah Hagarense wetuomash.
83.7 Gebal, kah Ammon kah Amalek, Philistiansog, kah wodohkecheg Tyre.
83.8 Assur wonk oowetoowomuh: anunumauopaneg wunnamonuh Lot. Selah.
83.9 Unneh nag neanheohp Midianitesog: neanheohp Sisera, kah Jabin ut Kisone sepuut:
83.10 Uttuh pagquanehhitteuhp ut Endor: nag {ogque} munnoquohkonkanuoopaneg wutche ohke.
83.11 Okqueh wuttohtoskouwomoouh en Oreb, kah Zeebut: nux, wame wussontimmomoouh, neane Zebah, kah neane Zalmunna:
83.12 Nag anoowohpanuk, Nemunumontuh wekash God nash ohtouunnat.
83.13 Woi num-Mannittoom, nag okqueh wheelut: okque sekqussunkanit waban toanontog.
83.14 Noohteau neane chikassumoomoouk chuppuhquhk, kah neane kussompunneau nashqussumoomoouk wadchuash;
83.15 Nag ne inne wunnomattehtah nashpe kummisshehtahshinneum, kah wapissuwah nashpe kuttuhkquohquattoom.
83.16 Numwohtauush wuskesukkoowoash nashpe ogkodchuonk: onk woh nag natinneahhomog koowesuonk, woi Jehovah.
83.17 Chepushshahittich kah wuttammehpunahittich micheme: nux, ogkodchhittich, kah pagquanehhittich:
83.18 Onk woh wosketompaog unnoowahteoog, ken wepe assoowesean JEHOVAH, kuttanue qunnuhquap waape mamusse ohke.
84.0
84.1 TOh unukuhque tapinneunkquatash kekash, woi Jehovah, wattiyeuwehteomit ahhontanooonkash!
84.2 Nukketeahogkou nontweanummoo, nux, wonk sauantam wutche uppeuhtamwakomukquash Jehovah: nuttah kah nooweyaus muhshontoowomooash wutche pomantamwae God.
84.3 Nux, mameshasquish namehteo wetu, kah wapunnukquas wodush wutche wohhoguh, uttuh woh sapsumont ooskishshomoh, {nux} kut-altaroomash, woi Jehovah wattiyeuwehteomit ohhontanooonkash, nukkehtahsootumoom kah num-Mannittoom.
84.4 Wunnanumoog nag oaiitcheg kekut: nag pish keyoyatche wowaenomukquog. Selah.
84.5 Wunnanumou wosketomp noh ummunehkesuonk apehtunkquean: nag wuttohhowout ohtakish kehtouwonkash.
84.6 Nag panupwushotogik Bakae oonowuhkoi, oothamonkanuhkoneau: wonk sookunnon numwapanumoomoo nippisseash.
84.7 Nag ushqushaog wutch munnehkesuonkanit en munnehkesuonkanit; nishnoh pasuk noquissu ut Sion anuhquabit God.
84.8 Woi Jehovah Mannit wattiyeuwehteomit ahhontanooonkash, nootash nuppeuhtamooonk: kuhkehtash, woi um-Mannittoomoh Jakob. Selah.
84.9 Kusseh, woi God nuttogqunneganun, kah moninneash wuskesuk kussasequnnittoom.
84.10 Newutche pasuk kesukod ut kekut anwunnegik onk nukquit muttanununkanuash: nunnekonantam nanawusquontamonat ut wekut num-Mannittoom, onk neit aiinneat matchetooe wetuwomut.
84.11 Newutch Jehovah Mannit nuppauz kah ogqunneg: Jehovah pish magoo monaneteaonk kah sohsummooonk: matta pish kogkonunumoo ne teag wanegik wutch nag panupwuttahhae pamushacheg.
84.12 Woi Jehovah wattiyeuwehteomit ahhontanooonkash, wunnanumou wosketomp noh pabahtanumukquean.
85.0
85.1 JEhovah, koosikitteaantamup kuttohke: kukquehchoowuttop ummussinnoooonk Jakob:
85.2 Kuttohquontamup ummatcheseonkanoo kummissinninnumog, kutonkhumup wame uppaneusseonkanoo. Selah.
85.3 Kuttammanumup wame kummooshquantamooonk: kukquishkep wutch kussape kummooshquantamooonkanit.
85.4 Qunnippinninnnean, woi wadchanuwae num Mannittoomun, kah ne tahshehtauush kummoosquanummuonkanun.
85.5 Sun pish micheme kummoosquanimumun? sun pish kukquinehteo kummooshquantamooonk en wame pometuonkanit?
85.6 Sun matta pish wonk kuttompannomuwahheumun: onk woh kummissinninnumog koowekontammooonukquog?
85.7 Nahtissinnean kukkuttumonteanitteaonk, woi Jehovah, kah unninumaiinnean koowadchanuwaonk.
85.8 Nukkehkehtam Mannit Jehovah toh anoowat: newutche pish wunnahteae kunnoonau ummissinninnumoh, kah oonetuppantamoomoh: qut ahque nag wonk qushkehhittich en assootuonkanit.
85.9 Wunnumuhkit oowadchanuwaonk uppasoosuhkonkqunneau nag quashukqutcheh; onk woh sohsumooonk wuttohkemoo nutohkenonut.
85.10 Kuttumonteanitteaonk kah wunnummuhkitteyeuonk nontshoittumooit: sampweusseonk kah wunnahteaonk chupwuttoonapwuttuog.
85.11 Wanummuhkitteyeuook pish sonkin wutch ohkehkontu: kah sampweusseonk pish womompumoo wutch kesukqut.
85.12 Nux, Jehovah pish magoo {ne} wanegik: kah kuttohkein pish nekehteomoo ummechumooonk.
85.13 Sampweusseonk pish nekonukkunk: kah pish kuppoonukqun wuttontanehtuonkane mayut.
86.0
86.1 NAuwanush kehtauog, woi Jehovah, nootah: newutche nummatcheg kah nukquenawehhuk.
86.2 Wadchan nukketeahogkou, newutche noonetuppantamweyeu: woi num-Mannittoom, wadchan kuttinninneum noh pabahtanumukquean.
86.3 Kuttummonteanumeh, woi Lord: newutche kummauunnittauush asekesukohkish.
86.4 Wekontamwah ukketeahogkonoh kuttinninneum: newutche, woi Lord, kuttuspunumauush nukketeahogkou.
86.5 Newutche ken, Lord, koonetum, kah kukkakunne ohquontos: kah kummishe kuttummonteanitteam en wame wehquttumunkqueaneg.
86.6 Woi Jehovah, ahchussittash nuppeuhtomooonk: kah kuhkehtash wadtauohtunkquissue noowehquttumooonkash.
86.7 Ut nootamehpunae kesukodut pish koowehquttumauush: newutche pish kunnompoohumah.
86.8 Kunnugke wame mannittooog matta pasuk kuttinnunkkoo, woi Lord: kah wanne annuhkosuonkanunoo aquinneunkquohk kuttanuhkosuonkanit.
86.9 Wame wuttohtimoinneash nesh kesehtauohpash, pish peyaog kah wawussummuaog anuhquapean, woi Lord: kah pish sohsumoowontamwog koowesuonk.
86.10 Newutche ken kummissukken, kah kummuhchantamwe oussem: ken kunnise Mannittoo.
86.11 Kuhkootumah kummay, woi Jehovah, pish nuppumusham koonomwaonkanit: pasukquinehtauush nuttah quehtiantamunnat koowesuonk.
86.12 Pish koowawenomush, woi Lord num-Mannittoom, nashpe mamusse nuttah: pish nussohsumooontam koowesuonk micheme.
86.13 Newutche missi kummonanummuonk: kah kuppohquohwhunop nukketeahogkou wutch wutchomuhque wenohkeit.
86.14 Woi God, pahtuanumwitcheg noowaapehtunkquk, kah uhkupunahteae mukkinneonkash natinneahwhopaneg nukketeahogkou: kah matta kuppoonukkoopaneg anuhquaphittit.
86.15 Qut ken, woi Lord kummishe kuttummonteanitteae kah monanitteae Mannittoo: sepe unnanitteae kah mochukohtok kuttummonteanitteaonk kah wunnomwaonk.
86.16 Woi quishkish en nohhogkat, kah kuttummonteanumeh: unnunumau kuttinninneum kummunehkesuonk, kah wadchan wunnamonoh muttumwussisse kuttinninneum.
86.17 Nahtisseh kuhkinneasuonk wutche wanegik, onk woh nag sekinneunkqueoneg, wunnamunneau, kah woh ogkodchuog: newutche ken, Jehovah, kuttanunumiip, kah kuttapehhip.
87.0
87.1 UKquenohtakoom {ohteau} wunnetuppantamwe wadchuuhkuhtu.
87.2 Jehovah wamontam Sione usquontamash, anue onk wame ootohkeonkash Jakob.
87.3 Sohsummooeyeuukish unnoowonash papaume ken, woi wuttootan God. Selah.
87.4 Pish nummusham Rahab, kah Babilon en nag wahukqueoneg; kusseh Philistia, kah Tyre, weche Ethiopia: yeuoh {wosketomp} na wuttut nekinneah.
87.5 Kah papaume Sion pish unnoowon, yeuuh, kah unnuh wosketomp na wuttut nekinneaop: kah nehenwonche anue Quanuhquapit pish ummunehkehtauun.
87.6 Jehovah pish unogketam wussuhkquohwhont mussinninnuog, yeuuh wosketomp na wuttut nekinneah. Selah.
87.7 Neane ketoohomaeninnuog, nemehkuh kodtontoowanukig wohwunontoowohkottomukish {pish na wuttapinneau}: wame nuttohkekommuash ohtaash kohhogat.
88.0
88.1 WOi Jehovah, wadchanuwae num-Mannittoom, nummoup kesukodtae kah nuhkonae anuhquapean.
88.2 Nuppeuhtamooonk peyoumooutch anuhquapean: ahchusitash nummauonk
88.3 Newutche nukketeahogkou numwohteau wuttamehpunaonkash: kah nukketeaonk pasoosuhkom wenohk.
88.4 Noowetogkemit nag womussitcheg en passohtheganit: nuttogquinneunkquis wosketompaut noh matta manehkeseg.
88.5 Nutchipinninnu kunnuke napukig, onatuh nashitcheg sepsukig wenohkeit, nag matta wonk mamehquanumoadt: kah nag tummehtahwhoog wutch kunnitcheganit.
88.6 Kussepsumip quanonogohk passohtheganit, pohkunnaiyeuut, ut moonoiyeuut.
88.7 Kummooshquantamooonk nuttohkequssumooonukqun; kah kootamehpunnassip nashpe wame kuttukkoomog. Selah.
88.8 Kuttammanok wahwetassumoguppaneg en noadtut wutch nohhogat, kunnehchantamwahhip en wohhogaout: nukkuphos, kah matta woh nussuhhamooh.
88.9 Nuskesuk mohtuppaemoo nashpe uhquehpunnaonk: Jehovah, koowowehquttumauush asekesukohkish, nuttouspunumunash nunnitchegash en kohhogat.
88.10 Sun napukig pish kunnahtinnoog muhchantamooonkash? sun pish napukig omohkeog kah koowaenomukquog? Selah.
88.11 Sun pish wamoahsue kummonaneteaonk, ontuttumun ut wenohkeit? asuh kuppabahtanumukquissuonk ut pagwanuonkanit?
88.12 Kummuhchantamooonkash sun pish wahtaunash ut pohkunaiyeuut? kah kussompweusseonk ut wannantamwae ohkeit?
88.13 Qut kummauunnittauunup, woi Jehovah, kah nompoae nuppeuhtamooonk pish kummahche peaonukqun.
88.14 Jehovah tohwajeh ammauhteaan nukketeahogkou? tohwaj adtahtiean kuskesuk?
88.15 Nuttuhkuhpunnam kah nahen nunnup, nateoh waskeninnueon: ne waamattamon kussaiashkishohteaonkash noowanontam.
88.16 Kuttuhque mooshquantamooonk nunnuhkuhkonk; kussaiashkishohteaonkash nuttummehtahhukqunash.
88.17 Asekesukohkish noowenuhkonkqunnapash, onatuh nippeit, noowenuhkonkqunnapash moaeu.
88.18 Wamosoowadt kah wetompain kunnoepoonummiinneak, kah wahwetassumoguppaneg en pohkenaiyeuut.
89.0
89.1 NUttunnoohomom ummonanitteaonkash Jehovah micheme: nashpe nuttoon pish noowahteauwahhuwam kuppabahtanumukqussuonk en wame pometuonkanit.
89.2 Newutche nissip monaneteaonk pish wowekuhkon micheme: kesukqut kuppabahtanumukqussuonk pish kuttut munnehkehtauun.
89.3 Nuttaiumup wunnoowawaonk weche noh pepenauogup, nutchadchekeumomp David nuttinninneum.
89.4 Pish nummunehkehheoog kooskaneminneog micheme, kah noowekehteam {kehtahsootumwe} kuttapuonk en wame pometuonkanit. Selah.
89.5 Kah kesukquash pish waenotumoomooash kummuhchantamooonkash, woi Jehovah; kupabahtanumitteaonk wonk ut ummukkinneonkanoowout wanetupantogik.
89.6 Newutche howan ut kesukqut woh ogquinneunkquissehhit Jehovahut? howan kunnugke wunnamonauh masukkenukig woh agquehheomuk, Jehovahut?
89.7 God woh mishe wapissuonou ut ummukkinneonkanoowout wanetuppantogik: kah woh ukquehtianumukquoh wame wanappehtunkqutcheh.
89.8 Woi Jehovah um-Mannittoomoouh ahhontanooonkash, howan munnehkesue Jehovahooit ogque kuhhogat? asuh en kuppabahtanumukquissuonkanit wanuhkonkquean?
89.9 Kunnanawunum wuttuhqueneunkqussuonk kehtah: wuttukkoomoh waapishahhittitcheh kutchequnehtauunash.
