89.10 Kussukquehtahwhomp Rahab, neane noh nohshit: kussewohhok kummatwomog nashpe munehke kuhpit.
89.11 Kesukquash kootaiheinneash, ohke wonk kootaihe: muttaohk kah neadtahshimmechumik, nash kummunnuhkohtinnapash.
89.12 Nannomut kah soanish kutaiumunnapash: Tabor kah Hermon pish muskkouantamoomooash ut koowesuonkanit.
89.13 Kuttahto munnuhkiyeue muhpit: kunnitcheg munnuhki, kah qunnuhqui kuttinuhkou.
89.14 Sampwesuonk kah wussuttumooonk {nash} kuttappooe wuttohkeonk: monaneteaonk, kah wunnummuhkitteyeuuk pish nekonuhkomwog kuskesuk.
89.15 Wunnanumoog missinninnuog nag wahteunkig mushkouantamonteowaonk: nag pish pomishaog, woi Jehovah ut kuskesukque wequaiyeumut.
89.16 Ut koowesuonkanit pish mushkouantamwog quinne kesuk: kah ut kussampweusseonkanit pish mishshehheoog.
89.17 Newutche ken ummunehkesue sohsummooonkanoo: kah koosikkitteaantamooonkanit nuttaskonun pish tashunumun.
89.18 Newutche Jehovah nuttogqunnekanun: kah oonetuppantamoomoh Israel nukkehtahsootumoomun.
89.19 Neit kukkunoonomp koonetuppantamweyeum, ut unnammanissuonkanit, kah kissip, nuppoonummauop annunummoadtuonk noh manehkesit: nuttahshunomp papenawut wutch missinninnuut.
89.20 Nunnamehheop David nuttinninneum: nashpe noonetuppantamwe pumme nussussequnop.
89.21 Noh weche nunnitcheg pish manehkehtosik: nuhpit wonk pish munnuhkehhuk.
89.22 Matwau matta pish wuttoadtehteahheuh: kah matchetooe wunnamoniin matta pish wuttuhquanumwehheuh.
89.23 Pish nunnookehtahwhoog ummatwomoh ut anuhquapit, kah nuttuhkuhpunnanoog nag sekinneauoncheg.
89.24 Qut nuppabahtanummukqussuonk kah nukkuttummonteanitteaonk pish wetomuk: kah ut noowesuonkanit wuttoskon pish tashunnumun.
89.25 Pish nuppoonum wonk wunnitcheg kehtahhannit, kah wuttunnuhkou ut sepuwehtu.
89.26 Noh pish nummauunnittunk, ken noosh, num Mannittoom, kah wadchanuwae nukqussukquanum.
89.27 Noh pish nummohtomekeh, pish nuttanuwuhqusseh ohkee kehtahsootumwut.
89.28 Pish noowadchonumau nummonaneteaonk micheme, kah noonoowaonk pish munnehtukkompatteau noh weche.
89.29 Ooskannem wonk pish nummichemappeh, kah {kehtahsootumooe} wutappuonk neane kesukque kesukkodash.
89.30 Wunnechonoh nukkodtumwehhittit nuttinomatuonk, kah matta pomushshahhitteg noosuttumooonkanit;
89.31 Poohqunnumwehhittit nukkodteahquttumooonkash, kah matta nanauwehtauehhitteg nuttannoohteamooonkash.
89.32 Neit pish nunnattauohtoh uppanneusseonkanoo nashpe sasamatahheg, kah ummatcheseonkanoo nashpe tattogkodtuonkash.
89.33 Qut onch, kuttummonteanitteae noowammoahsuonk matta pish pabukquanne nuttammanumauoun, kah nupnabahtanumukqussuonk matta pish panishshanooh.
89.34 Matta pish nuppoohqunnumooh noonoowaonk, asuh nuppenoowehteoooh ne sohhomoomoouk wutch nussissittoonit.
89.35 Pasukqut nutchadchekewop nashpe noonetuppantamooonk, matta pish nuppannoowoh en Davidut.
89.36 OOskannem pish michemohteau, kah {assootumooe} wuttapuonk neane nuppauz ut anuhquabeh.
89.37 Pish munnehkehtauun micheme neane nahneposhad: kah onatuh pabahtanumukqussue wawaenin ut kesukqut. Selah.
89.38 Qut kuppogkenop kah kutcheshanumop, kummishe mooshquanumop kussasequnnittoom.
89.39 Kummattohentuppehtauuni oonoowaonk kuttinninneum: kunneeskehtauunni wutchetuhquab, {nashpe kuttunuhteaonk} en ohkeit.
89.40 Kukkepuhkomunnat wame uppumminnutunkash; koowoskehtauunnat munnehkiyeue oomonushkumash.
89.41 Wame {na} Paumummayacheg ummukkookunouh: noh ushpunnatuonkanyeuoo, en wetohteamonkoh.
89.42 Kuttahshunumup wuttinuhkounoo ayeuohkonukqutcheh: koowekontamwahheok wame ummatwomoh.
89.43 Kuttahsashinnehtauunni wonk an kenag wuttogkodteg, kah matta kunnepauwehheoh ayeutuonkanit.
89.44 Koowohkuhquoshittauuni wussohsumooonk, kah kuttinuhkoni assootumooe wuttapuonk en ohkeit.
89.45 Kuttiohquehtauunnat ooskeninnue kesukkodtumash: kummahche puttagooh nashpe ogkodchuonk. Selah.
89.46 Tohsohkee, Jehovah, pish kuppomputtogquem micheme? Sun pish kummoshquantamooonk ogqunneau noohtaut?
89.47 Mehquantash toh nuttinne tiohquohquompunneam: tohwajeh tahnoochehhohp wame wosketompaog?
89.48 Utteiyeuuh wosketomp {neh} pamontog kah matta pish naumook nuppooonk? sun woh pohquohwhunau ukketeahogkounoh wutch wunnitcheganut wenohke. Selah.
89.49 Lord, uttiyeush nekonaeyeue wamoahsue kukkuttummonteanitteaonkash, {nish} chachekeimohpash David ut koonummuhkitteyeuut?
89.50 Mehquantash, woi Lord, ushpunnamaonkanoo kittinninnumog; uttoh nittin naiyeutam ut nuppoochunnouonut {wuttushpunnamuwaonkannoo} wame matikkenukig missinninnuog;
89.51 Ne nashpe kummatwomog ashpunnamuwahhitteup, woi Jehovah; ne nashpe ushpunnatumwehhitteup wuttontanehtuonkash kussasequnnuttoom.
89.52 Wunnanumunnach Jehovah micheme. Amen kah amen.
90.0
90.1 Lord, noowoittiyeuonkanimun kuhhog ut wame pometuonkanit.
90.2 Wadchuash asq nanekununookup, kah asquam kakuhkenauwehtauooan ohke kah muttaohk: nux wutch michemeyeuonkanit en michemeyeuonkanit, ken kum-Mannittooh.
90.3 Kukqunnupun wosketomp en pagquannuonkanit: kah kissim, Quishkeg kenau wunnechonoowuh wosketompaog.
90.4 Newutche kuttunompattam nukquit muttanonkane kodtummooash neane wunnonkkoo mahche paamuhshunk, kah onatuh nuhkonae ashkuhwheteaonk.
90.5 Kummoncheohheoog onatuh nashpe tommogkon, nag onatuheyeuooog kawemukkish: nompoae neaneyeuooog moskehtuut ne sonkig.
90.6 Nompoae missetumoo, kah waapekin; wunnonkoouk tummehthamun kah uppoopohteau.
90.7 Newutche nummahtuppaemun nashpe kummooshquantamooonk, kah nashpe kuttuhque mooshquantamooonk nootamantamhitteamun.
90.8 Kuppoonumup nummatcheseonkanunonash anuhquapean, nukkeme matcheseonkanunnonash ut kuskesukque wequaiyeuut.
90.9 Newutche wame nukkesukodtumunnonash mahtshaitteash ut kummooshquantamooonkanit: nuttogque mahtshadtomun nukkodtumoomunnonash onchumooonkanit.
90.10 Nukkodtumooe kesukodtumunonash nesausuk tahshinehchage kodtumooooash; kah nashpe munnehkesuonk nishwosuk tashinehchagohk, onch ummenuhkesooonkanoo anuhkosuonk, kah nooehpunnaonk; newutche teanuk tummehthamun kah nuttoowemun.
90.11 Howan wahteunk kummushquantamwe menuhkesuonk? onk neaunag kukquishitteaonk ne unni kummushquantamooonk.
90.12 Kuhkootummaiinnean unnogketamunnat nukkesukodtumunonash, onk woh nuppoonumumun nuttahhunnonash waantamooonkanit.
90.13 Qushkish, woi Jehovah, toh sohke? kah aiuskoiantash papaume kuttinninnumog.
90.14 Woi nompoae tapinneauwahhinnean nashpe kukkuttumonteanitteaonk; onk woh nummushkouantamumun, kah noowekontamumun wame nukkesukodtumunnonash.
90.15 Wekontamwahhinnean, neaunagkup kesukodash {adt} uhkuhpunnaseogup, kah kodtumooash {adt} namogup machuhk.
90.16 Kuttanuhkosuonk pohkompamukquatitch en kuttinninnumit, kah kussohsummooonk en wunnechanoowout.
90.17 Kah oonetuonk Jehovah num-Manittoomun apehtunkquttuh: kah nunnitcheganne anuhkausuonkanun menuhkehteiinnean, nux, nunnitchegane anuhkausuonkanun munnuhketauush.
91.1 NOh wadohket wuttasompamukquadtoomut anue Quanuhquappit, pish appu wutonkkouuhtomut wame manuhkesit.
91.2 Pish nissim papaume Jehovah, noh nuttuttashpuhhoowaonk, kah noowohkonoos num-Manittoom, noh pish nuppabahtanum.
91.3 Wunnamuhkut pish kuppohquohwhunuk wutch wuttahpehhonut adchaenin: kah wutch uhque unninneaonkanit
91.4 Pish kupputtogkuhhuk nashpe ummequnoh, kah agwe wunnuppohwhunut pish kuppabahtantam oonomwaonk pish koowohkonoos, kah kuttogqunneg.
91.5 Matta pish koowapissuontamooh nuhkane siashkishanittuonkash: asuh kouhquadt ne pamshunk kesukodae.
91.6 Asuh wesaushaonk ne pamushshomoouk pohkenaiyeuut: asuh pagquanuonk ne pagquahteomoouk puhshahquae.
91.7 Nukqut muttanonkkanogkussuog pish punishaog keshke kuhhogkat, kah piogqut muttanonkanogkussuog kuttunuhkounit: qut matta pish kuppasoosuhkonkooun.
91.8 Webe nashpe kuskesukquash pish kummonunneam, kah kunnaum wutonkquatunkanoo matchetooog.
91.9 Newutche Jehovah noh attashpuhhoowaonkane {nux} anue Quanuhquapit kootaiyeuonkanuhkonap.
91.10 Matta pish kummatchehpunoh, asuh ne teagwe unninneaonk pasoosuhkomoomunnooh kootahtuonk.
91.11 Newutche pish mechumuhkonau wut-Angelsumoh papaume ken, woh kunnanawehhikqunaout ut wame kummayash.
91.12 Nag pish kuttashunnegkonukquog ut wunnutcheganoowout, ishkont kuttogsuttassun qussukquanut.
91.13 Pish kuttaskuhkou qunnonoo, kah addar: wuskukqunnonoo kah dragon agwe mussetut.
91.14 Newutche noowawomonukup, noh pish nuppohquohwhun: pish noh nukqunnuhquapeh, newutche wawahteoup noowesuonk.
91.15 Pish noowehkumuk, kah pish nunnompoohamau: pish noowetom wuttamehpunnaonkanut, pish nuppohquohwhun, kah nukquehtianumooe unneh.
91.16 Nashpe sepe pomantamooonk pish nuttapeh, kah nunnahtun noowadchanuwaonk.
92.0
92.1 WUnnegen tapattantumauonat Jehovah, kah ketoohomwontamunat koosuonk, woi Quanuhquappean.
92.2 Nahtuhkonat kummishe womoahsuonk mohtompanae, kah kuppabahtanumukqussuonk asenuhkohkish.
92.3 Ut Piogpeminneohtonooe wohwunnontoowohkodtomuk, kah Psalteryut; ut Harput nashpe manunontoowaonk.
92.4 Newutche ken, Jehovah, koowekontamwahip nashpe kuttanuhkausuonk: pish nummishkouantamoowontam kunnitcheganne anuhkosuonkash.
92.5 Woi Jehovah, tohen mussiyeuash kuttanuhkosuonkash! kah kuttunantamooonkash ahche moonoiyeuash.
92.6 Puppinashimwe wosketomp matta wahteooo: kah mattammog matta wohtammoo.
92.7 Matchetooog ogque waapeghittit moskehtuut, kah wame anuhkositcheg matcheusseonk musseghettit: {ne unni} onk woh nag pagquanoog micheme.
92.8 Qut ken, Jehovah, {kuttanue} Qunnuhquap micheme.
92.9 Newutche kusseh, kummatwomog, woi Jehovah kusseh kummatwomog pish pagquannuog: wame anuhkositcheg matcheseonk pish sewahwhoog,
92.10 Qut nuttaskon pish kuttashunumun onatuh {wutaskanit} nukqutyeuwun: pish nussissequnnit wuske pumme.
92.11 Nuskesuk pish wonk naum {nukkodtantamooonk} ut nummatwomut: kah nehtauogash pish nootamoomooash {nukkodtantammooonk} papaume matchetooog nag waapehtunkqueoneg.
92.12 Sampweseaenin pish kussetu onatuh palmuhtukqut: pish unnetu Lebanone utchukuppemusseit.
92.13 Nag ahketeamukkeg ut wekit Jehovah, pish mussetuog ut wutchippenutunkanit num-Manittoomun.
92.14 Nag pish aspime momechummooog mahtantamwehhittit: nag pish wunnogkooog kah askaskooog.
92.15 Nahtuhkonat Jehovah sampwesu: noh nukqussukquanum, kah wanne appehtunkoo panneusseonk.
93.1 Jehovah {assootamooe} nanawunum, ogkoo mamuttanittuonk, Jehovah ogkoo menuhkesuonk ne nashpe puttukquapunont wuhhogkuh: muttaohk wonk menuhkehtosu, onk woh matta ontahtanooh.
93.2 Assootamooe kuttapuonk noadt mamunnuhkehtauunap: koottap michemeyeuonkanit.
93.3 Tommogkonash waapunnumuppash, woi Jehovah, tommogkonash waapunnumuppash ummushontoowaonkanoo: tommogkonash waapunumwog wuttukoomoouh.
93.4 Jehovah quanuhquiit anuwunuhkesuontam ummushshontoowaonkannoo monatash nippeash, {nux}, onk kehtahhane kehtontukquog.
93.5 Koowauwaonkash ahche wunumuhkuteyeuooash: wunnetuppantamooonk tapehkontamoomoo kek, woi Jehovah, micheme.
94.1 WOi Jehovah, annootae Manit: woi annootae Manit, pahke wohsish.
94.2 Tahshin kuhhog, ken wasittuman ohke: onkquattau pahtuanumitcheg.
94.3 Jehovah, toh sohkee pish matchetooog, toh sohkee pish matchetooog mushkowaog?
94.4 Toh sohkee pish kekuttoohkontamwog, kah unnoowaog uhqueneunkquohkish? {kah} pish wame anuhkositcheg matcheseonk waenowaog?
94.5 Nag sukquishannaog kummissinninnumog, woi Jehovah, kah uhkuhpunnattoog kuttahtoonk.
94.6 Nushshaog sekouishquoh, kah penoowohteoh, kah nushaog mowadtooshookeg.
94.7 Qut onch unnoowaog, Jehovah matta pish naummoo: asuh um-Manittoomoh Jakob ootoowantamooun.
94.8 Wohtamook, kenau puppinashimweneunkquisseaquish kunnukke missinninnuut: kah kenau mattammagquog ahquompag pish koowaantammumwoo.
94.9 Noh ahkehteohp mehtauog, sunummatta pish nootammoo? noh ayikup muskesuk, sunummatta pish naumoo?
94.10 Noh sasametahwhont penoowohteoh, sunummatta pish sasamehtahhoowooo? noh kohkootumauont wosketompoh wahteoonk, {sunummatta pish wahteooo}?
94.11 Jehovah wahteo wuttunantamooonkash wosketomp, {wahteo} nash tohnoocheyeuash.
94.12 Wunnanumou wosketomp noh sasamakohwhadt, woi Jehovah, kah kohkootumauadt wutch kuttinnomatuonkanit:
94.13 Onk woh kuttunumau anwohsinooonk wutch uhquanumooe kesukkodut, napache mahche pass[a]hthomauonaout matchetooog.
94.14 Newutche Jehovah matta pish pogkenooo ummissinninnumoh, asuh matta pish nukkodtumoo wuttohtoonk.
94.15 Qut wussuttumooonk pish quinnippemoo en wunnomwausseonkanit: kah wame sampwutteahoncheg pish wuttasuhkomunneau.
94.16 Howan pish waapeanishit ayeuuhkone matchesecheg? howan pish nepauweanishit ayeuuhkone annuhkositcheg matcheseonk?
94.17 Jehovah matta annunumaiekus, nukketeahogkou woh teanuk aiyeup chequnniyeuonkanit.
94.18 Anoowaon, Nisseet toonukquishin: kukkuttumonteanitteaonk, woi Jehovah, nukkogkonunukqunnap.
94.19 Ut monatash nuttinnantamooonkash nuttinnomaiyeumut, kuttaphuwaonkash oowekontamwahhukqunash nukketeahogkou.
94.20 Sun pish matcheseonkane assootumwe appuonk koowechaiyeumuk, uttoh ayik woskehhuwaonk nashpe unnomatuonk.
94.21 Nag miaeog ayeuuhkone ukketeahogkounoh sampweseaenin, kah mahchinnuwontamwog mat woskehhuwae wishquehhunk.
94.22 Qut Jehovah noowuhkonoos: kah num-Manittoom nuttutashpuhhoowae qussuk.
94.23 Kah pish upputtogquehtahwhuh nehenwonche ummatcheusseonkanoo, kah pish wuttummehtahwhuh ut nehenwonche ummatchetooonkanoowout: {nux}, Jehovah kum-Manittoomun pish wuttummehtahwhuh.
95.1 EHoh peyonk ketoohomauontuh Jehovah: mushkouantamontoowaehtauontuh wadchanuae kukqussukquanoomun.
95.2 Tapattantamooe peontuh anuhquapit, kah wekontamontoowohkouontuh nashpe ketoohomaonkash.
95.3 Newutche Jehovah missugkenue Manit, kah missukkenue kehtassoot anue wame manittooog.
95.4 Wunnutcheganit ahtaash ohkee moonoiyeuash: wannashquadtinne munnehkesuonkash wonk ootaiheinash.
95.5 Kehtoh ootaihein, kah wuttaiumunap: kah wunnutchegash kesehteomoopash nunnopohke.
95.6 Ehoh peyonk wawussummuwatuh, kah nawaetuh: appesittukqussunuttuh anuhquapit Jehovah noh keshukqueogup
95.7 Newutche noh num-Manittoomun, kah nenauwun chippinnutunkane ummissinninnumoh, kah wunnitchegane wuttissheepsumoh: yeu kesukohk nootamokq oowadtauohtunkqussuonk,
95.8 Munnehkehteooohteokq kuttahhoo, neane utmooshkhittuonkanit, kah qutchehhuwae kesukodut ut touohkomukqut.
95.9 Kooshoowok ne quajhehhittit, kah natinneohkoshettit, kah naumhittit nuttanuhkosuonk.
95.10 Yaunnehchage kodtumwae nunnonoowehhukqunnap yeu pometuonk, kah nissip, nag missinninnuooog uttuh panne aoncheg ut wuttahhoowout, kah matta wahteooopaneg nummayash.
95.11 {Onk} nutchadchekeimopaneg ut nummooshquantamooonkanit, matta uppetutteanaout nuttanwohsunooonkanit.
96.1 Woi ketoohomohk Jehovah wuske unnoohomaonk: ketoohomohk Jehovah mamusse ohke.
96.2 Ketoohomohk Jehovah, wunnantamoohk oowesuonk: nahtehteagq oowadchanuwaonk asekesukohkish.
96.3 Ontuttumook wussohsumooonk kunnugke penoowohteaut, kah ummuhchantammooonkash kunnugke wame missinninnuut.
96.4 Newutche mussukken Jehovah, kah woh mishe waenomou: noh woh qushou anue onk wame manittooog.
96.5 Newutche wame um-Manittoomoouh wutohtimoinneunk unninneuhkontunkannuooog: qut Jehovah ayimup kesukquash.
96.6 Quhtianittuonk kah mamuttanittuonk ahtaash anuhquapit: menuhkesuonk kah wunnetuonk ahtaash oonetuppantamwakomukqut.
96.7 Unnunumohk Jehovah, woi kenau missinninnue auwatuonkash, unnunumohk Jehovah sohsumooonk kah munnehkesuonk.
96.8 Unnunumohk Jehovah oowesuonkane sohsumooonk: patoook magooonk kah peyonk uppeuhtamwakomukqut.
96.9 Wowussumoohk Jehovah ut wunnetupanatamwe wunnetuonkanit: wapissek ut anuhquapit, wame ohke.
96.10 Unnoowag kunnugke penoowohteaut, Jehovah assootumwe nanawunnum: muttaohk wonk pish munnehketauun kah matta pish ontohtanoo; noh pish sampwe wussumau missinninneuh.
96.11 Kesukquash mushkouantamoomooutch, kah ohke wekontamoomooutch: kehtoh mishontoowomooutch, kah wame ne na ohtag.
96.12 Ahteuhk mushkouantamoomooutch kah ne atashimmechumik: neit wame touohkomukque mehtukquash pish wekontamoomooash.
96.13 Anuhquapit Jehovah; newutche peyau, newutche peyau wussuttumunat ohke: pish wussuttum muttaohk nashpe sampweusseonk, kah missinninneuh nashpe oonomwaeyeuonk.
97.1 JEhovah assootamooe nanawunum, ohke wekontamoomooutch: monahkish munnohhanash mushkouantamoomooutch.
97.2 Wenuhkunkq mattohqusash kah pohkunni: assootamwe wuttappuonk munnuhkiyeumoo sampweseonkanit kah wussuttumooonkanit.
97.3 Noohtau nekonuhkunk, kah ummahchukkusukqunneau ummatwomoh waene.
97.4 Ukkutshaumunash wequasumoomoopash muttaohk: ohke naumup kah nunnukkemoop.
97.5 Wadchuash sabahtopash onatuh waxut anuhquapit Jehovah: anuhquapit noh Paohquttuk mamusse ohke.
97.6 Kesukquash ontuttumoomooash wussampweusseonk: kah wame missinninnuog naumwog wussohsumooonk.
97.7 Ogkodchhettich wame nag wawussuttukeg monuhquittunkash, kah wawenowacheg ut unninneuhkontonkanit: noh wawussumoohk wame kenau mannittooog.
97.8 Sion nootamup, kah wekontamup, kah Judae wuttoninneunk mushkouantamuppaneg; newutche koosuttumooonkash, woi Jehovah.
97.9 Newutche ken, Johovah, kuttanoowuhquapehtam mamusse ohke: kummishe tahshinit onk wame mannittooog.
97.10 Kenau wamonagquish Jehovah, sekinneamook machuhk: noh wadchanau ukketeahogkonoowoh oonetupantamoomoh, nah uppohquohwhunuh wutch wunnitcheganoowout matchetooog.
97.11 Wequai ohkehkosoo wutche sampweusseaeninnuog, kah wekontamooonk wutche sampwutteahhoncheg.
97.12 Wekontamooonoohk Jehovah, kenau sampweseaeninnuog: kah tabattontumook mahquantamaquish oonetupantamooonk.
98.0
98.1 Woi unnoohumohk Jehovah wuske unnoohomaonk, newutche mahche usseu muhchantamooonkash: wuttunnuhkou kah wunnetupantamwe wuhpit mahche sohkosuwonishuk.
98.2 Jehovah wahtauwahhuwop oowadchanuwaonk: wussampweusseonk uppohquae nahtuhkonap anuhquaphittit penoowohteaog.
98.3 Mehquantamup ukkuttumonteanitteaonk kah oonomwaonk unnogque wekut Israel: wame wahquohkeyeuukish naumoouppash oowadchanuwaonk num-Mannittoomun.
98.4 Mushkouantamontoowaehtohk Jehovah, mamusse ohke: mushontoowag, kah mushkouantamook, kah waenomuae unoohomunk.
98.5 Ketoohomohk Jehovah nashpe harp; nashpe harp, kah nashpe ketoohomae wadtauohtunkquat.
98.6 Nashpe monuppuhpequonash, kah wuttunontoowaonk cornet: mushkouantamontoowag anuhquapit Jehovah, Kehtahsoot.
98.7 Ketah mishontoowomooutch, kah wame ne noh ahtag: muttaohk, kah nag nawadtohkecheg.
98.8 Tommogkonash puhpunkunnitchahhittich: wadchuash moae wekontamwehhittich,
98.9 Anuhquapit Jehovah; newutche peyau wussuttumunnat ohke: pish wussuttum muttaohk nashpe sampweusseonk, kah missinninnuog nash tatuppeunnehhittuonk.
99.1 JEhovah assootumooe nanawunum, missinninnuog nunnukshahittich: appu {noeu} cherubimsut, ohke ontahtaj.
99.2 Jehovah mussukken ut Sion: kah anuuhquapumau wame missinninnuog.
99.3 Waenotumwehhittich masag kah uhquinneunquohk koowesuonk: {newutche} wunnetupantamweyeumoo.
99.4 Kehtahsoot ummunnehkesuonk wonk wamontamoomoo wussuttumooonk, kummunehkehteoh tatuppeunnehhittuonk: kuttissem wussuttumooonk, & somweusseonk ut Jakob.
99.5 Tahshunook Jehovah kum Mannittoomun, kah wawussumoohk ut ukquensittassumoounit: {newutche} wunnetuppantamweyeuoo.
99.6 Moses kah Aaron ut kunnugke wussephausooeninnumoh, kah Samuel kenugke nag wehquttukeg oowesuonk: wehquttumauopaneg Jehovah, kah wunnompoohumauopah.
99.7 Ukkunnoonopah ut mattohqusse nepattuhquonkanit: nanawehteopaneg oowawaonkash, kah kuhkoowaonk anumauuhpah.
99.8 Kunnompoohumauopaneg, woi Jehovah num-Mannittoomun: tokonogque kuttannootontamup wuttogkunnaiantamooonkanoowoash, kuttohquontosue Mannittooup en wohhogaout.
99.9 Tahshunoohk Jehovah kum-Mannittoomun, kah wawussummuwak ut oonetuppantamwe wadchuut: newutche Jehovah num-Mannittoomun wunnetuppantamweyeuoo.
100.0
100.1 MUshkouantamontoowaehtohk Jehovah, wame kenau ohkeash.
100.2 Wekontamwe wuttinninnumuhkohk Jehovah: ketoohomae peyunk anuhquapit.
100.3 Wahteoook Jehovah Manittoooo, unnuh nukkeshukqunnonup, kah matta nehenwonche nenauun; {nenauun} ummissinninnumoh kah chippinneutunkane wuttusheepsumoh.
100.4 Tapattontumooe petutteak oosquontamut, kah en wekut nashpe waenomuwaonkash: tapattantumohk kah wunnantamook oowesuonk.
100.5 Newutche Jehovah wunnetoo; ukkuttummonteanitteaonk michemohteau: kah oonomwaonk {naquateahteau} en wame pometuonkanit.
101.0
101.1 NUttunnoohomom kuttummonteanitteaonk kah wussuttumooonk: pish kukketoohomouash, woi Jehovah.
101.2 Pish noowaontammuwun nohhog ut pahke mayut; woi Ohquompag kuppeyaoseh? pish pahketeahhae nuppompumusham nuttunnomukkomukqut.
101.3 Matta pish nuppoonumooh neteague machuhk anuhquapeh: nussekineam wuttanuhkosuonkanoo nag pohchacheg, matta pish nummuhsogquehtunkooun.
101.4 Moohmooshque muttah pish nuttamaehtunkqun: pish matta noowaheoh matchetooenin.
101.5 Noh keme mamatcheunont wetahtamonkoh, pish nuttumehtah: noh pahtuanumwinneunkqussit, kah pahtuanumwitteahhont, pish matta nittinnea wussompomoh.
101.6 Pish nummoninneauoog pabahtanumukquissitcheg ut ohkeit, onk woh nag noowechiyeumukquog: noh pamuhshadt pahke mayut pish nootinninnumuhkonkq.
101.7 Noh assookohkodteaanuhkosit, matta pish aiyeu nekit: noh pohponoowadt, matta pish oiapu anuhquapeh.
101.8 Pish nompoae nuppogquanoog wame matchetukeg ut ohkeit: onk woh nuttumehtah wame matchesecheg wutch wuttootannat Jehovah.
102.0
102.1 NOOtash nuppeuhtamuonk, woi Jehovah, kah nummauonk peyaonukquish.
102.2 Puttoghumaiehkon kuskesuk ut nootamehpunae kesukkodut, ahchoosuttah: ne kesukod wehkummuaon, teanuk nompoohumah.
102.3 Newutche nukkesukodtumash mahtuppaemooash onatuh pukkuttaut: kah nushkonash chikohtait onatuh tanunnantunk.
102.4 Nuttah togkodtamunnai, kah mussoopohtai onatuh mosketuut: newaj wannantam mechunnat nupputtukquinneg.
102.5 Nashpe wadtauohtunkquissue nutchequttumooonk nummahchukkonaim.
102.6 Nuttogquinneunkqus pelicanut ut touohkamukqut: nuttogquinneunkqus touohkamukque weesuut.
102.7 Nuttashkwheteam kah nuttogqueneunkqus mamessashquesut noh nonussiit woske chukkomukqut.
102.8 Nummatwomog nuttushpunnamukquog quinne kesukod: kah nag mishe mooshquanimmitcheg mahche chachekeyeuwaog aiyeuuhkone nohhogat.
102.9 Newaj mechomp pukque onatuh puttukqunnonkanit, kah nukkinnittuppanumup nootatttamoonk mussippequash:
102.10 Newutche kuttuhquantamooonk kah kussope kummooshquantamooonk: newutche kuttahshinnip, kah kuppunuhkosip.
102.11 Nukkesukodtumash ogquinneunkquadash onkauuhtaut ne ammaemoouk: kah nummussoopas onatuh moskehtuut.
102.12 Qut ken, woi Jehovah, pish kummitchemap, kah kummehquanimmitteaonk en wame pometuonkanit.
102.13 Pish kuttomohkem, kah kukkuttummonteantamun Sion: newutche ohqumpi ne monantamunnat, nux kuhquttumooe ohquompi peomoo.
102.14 Newutche kuttinninnumog wussikitteaantamwog ukqussukquonumash, kah monantamwog uppuppissiyeum.
102.15 Nemehkuh penuwohteaog pish wapissooontamwog oowesuonk Jehovah: kah wame ohkee kehtahsootumwog kussohsummooonk.
102.16 Jehovah weekehteadt Sion, pish noqussu ut wussohsumooonkanit.
102.17 Pish wuttooantam uppeuhtamooonkanoo mo teag ohtoookeg, kah matta meshanantamoo uppeuhtamooonkanoo.
102.18 Yeu pish wussuhkwhosu wutche pometuonk paomoouk: kah missinninnuog nag pish keshitcheg, pish waenomaog Jehovah.
102.19 Newutche womompoop wutch wunnetuppantamwe ukqunnuhquiyeuonkanit: wutch kesukqut Jehovah moninneamup ohke:
102.20 Nootamunnat wutchequttumooonk kopshogunnut, ompunneonat nag kahtimutcheg en nuppooonkanit.
102.21 Wahtauwahhuwonat ut Sion oowesuonk Jehovah, kah waenomaonk ut Jerusalem:
102.22 Missinninnuog mahche moehetit, kah assootumooonkash wuttinninneumuhkouonat Jehovah.
102.23 Noh noochumwehtooop nummunehkesuonk ut mayut; tiohquehtooop nukkesukodtumash.
102.24 Nissip, woi num-Mannittoom ahque ommaneh ut noeu nukkesukkodtumut: kukkodtumoomash yoyatohtaash en wame pometuonkanit.
102.25 Wutch noadt kuttohpohteashinehkontamunap ohke: kah kesukquash nesh kunnitchegane anuhkosuonk.
102.26 Nash pish mohtuppaemooash, qut ken pish kummichemap: nux, pish wame nukkoneyeuooash onatuh ogkoounnut; onatuh petashqushaonk pish kuppenoowe unnehtauunash, kah pish penoowehtosuash.
102.27 Qut ken noh nan, kah kukodtumoomash matta pish wohkuhquoshinninooash.
102.28 Wunnechonoouh kuttinninnumog pish naquohteapuog, kah ooskaneamminneumoouh pish munnehkehhoog anuhquapean.
103.0
103.1 Wunnanim Jehovah, woi nukketeahogkou: kah wame ne apehtunkqueh, oonetuppantamwe wesuonk.
103.2 Wunnanim Jehovah, woi nukketeahogkou: kah ahque wannantash wame oonenehhuwaonkash.
103.3 Noh ohquontog wame kummatcheseonkash: noh netskehtunk wame kummohchinnaonkash.
103.4 Noh pohquohwhuttunk kukketeaonk wutch pagquannuonkanit: noh chatuhquapunukquean nashpe kuttumonteanitteaonk, kah nohtohteanitteae monaneteaonkash.
103.5 Noh tapehtunk kuttoon nashpe wanekukish: onk kooskeninnuonk wuskehtosoo onatuh wompsukkuhquaut.
103.6 Jehovah oisseu samweseonk, kah wussuttumooonk, wutche wame uhkuhpunnanitcheg.
103.7 Wahtauwahhuwop ummayash en Mosesu, wuttisseonkash en wunnechonut Israel.
103.8 Jehovah kuttumonteanitteau kah monaneteau, cheke mooshquantam, kah monat ummonaneteaonk.
103.9 Matta pish naquahteae aiuskomuooo; kah matta pish micheme mooshquanitteooo.
103.10 Matta kuttinhukkooun nan neanag kummatcheusseonkanunnonash: kah matta kuttinonkquattunkkoounnan neanag kuppanneusseonkanunonash.
103.11 Newutche neane kesuk anue qunnuhquohteau onk ohke: nenukuhquin ukkutumonteanitteaonk en nag quoshukqutcheh.
103.12 Neane wompanniyeu noohtag wutch maquamittinniyeu: na unukuhque nuttontohtunkqunnan nummatcheseonkanunnonash.
103.13 Neane wuttooshimou kuttumonteanumont wunnechonoh: ne Jehovah wuttine kuttumonteanumon nah quoshukquitcheh.
103.14 Newutche wahteo nuttinsuonkanun: unnummehquantam nuppuppissiyeuoomun.
103.15 {Nagum} wosketomp ukkesukodtumash ogquinneunkquadtash moskehtuut: unnummussetu ohteuhkone uppeshauonut.
103.16 Newutche wapan uppamuhkomun, neit mahtshau, kah ne ahtakup matta wonk oowahteoooun.
103.17 Qut ummonaneteaonk Jehovah, wuttohteau michemeyeuonkanit en michemeyeuonkanit ut wohhogaout nag quashukqutcheh; kah wussampweusseonk en wunneechoninneunk wunnechonoowout:
103.18 En nah nanawehtauinnitcheh oonoowaonk: kah mehquantogik wuttanooteamooonkash nesh ussenat.
103.19 Jehovah quaquashwunumup assootumooe wuttapuonk ut kesukqut: kah wuttassootumooonk nanawunumoomoo wame.
103.20 Wunnannumook Jehovah, kenau wut-Angelsumoh, mishe munehkeseogish, aseogish wuttinoowaonk, nashpe kunnootamoonkanoo wuttunnoowaonkane wattauadtunkquissuonk.
103.21 Wunnanumook Jehovah, wame kenau wuttahhontanooonkash, wuttinninnumoh aseogish uttuh annantog.
103.22 Wunnanumook Jehovah, kenau wame wuttanuhkosuonkash nishnoh adt paiohquttuk: wunnanim Jehovah woi, nukketeahogkou.
104.1 Wunnanim Jehovah, woi nukketeahogkou: woi Jehovah num-Mannittoom, kummuttae mussukken, kuttokq quhtianittuonk, kah mamuttanissuonk.
104.2 Uttuh ogquanadt {kohhog} wequai, onatuh nashpe ogkooonk: sapakunnuman kesukquash onatuh kukkunonkanit.
104.3 Noh wanohtunk wuttashikkomukquhtukkumash nippehkohtu, noh tatuppequanumuhkouont wohhoguh mattohqussash, noh pamushadt wunnuppohwhunut wapan.
104.4 Noh nohshauonkanehhont wut-Angelsumoh: wuttinninnumoh noohnoonae noohteau.
104.5 {Noh} wanohtunkup ohkee ohpohteashikish; onk woh matta ontohtanoo micheme.
104.6 Kupputtogkuhhumunnap nashpe moonoi, neane nashpe ogkooonk: nippeash anuohtopash onk wadchuash.
104.7 Ne aiuskomuwaan wussemoouppash: kottoowahittit kunneampomog kunnippe monchemoouppash.
104.8 Kuhkuhqueontamuppash wadchuash, womsuontamuppash oonowuhkoiyeuash en aiyeuonkanit ne quashauehtamauadt.
104.9 Kuppoonumup kuhkunnunk ne woh matta anoowushshahittit: onk woh matta wonk qushkemunooash nuhkuhkomunnat ohke.
104.10 Annootam tohkekommuash en oonowuhkoiyeuut, {nesh} pumutchooanash kunnuke wadchuash.
104.11 Nesh ootattamwahhukqunneau wame ahteuhkone puppinashimwog: tauohkomukque assog uhtapattoog ukkuhkuttoonooonkanoo.
104.12 Na keshke kesukque puppinishaog pish wuttiinneau, pahchatuhqunnit attannoohumacheg.
104.13 Nippehkontam wadchuash wutch wuttashikkomukqut: ohke tapehtauun nashpe kuttanuhkosuonkane mechummuonk.
104.14 Nekehteo moskehtuash wutche puppinashimwog, kah wunnepogaskeht wutche wuttauwohteaonk wosketomp: onk woh padto metsuonk wutch ohkekuhtu:
104.15 Kah wine ne wekontamwahtunk wosketomp wuttah, kah pumme wosumwehtauunnat wuskesuk; kah puttukqunneg ne manehkehtunk wuttah wosketomp.
104.16 Ummuhtugkumash Jehovah, numwae wussippeyeuooash: Lebanone utchukuppemusseash nesh ahkehteahpash.
104.17 Na wuttut wadtushahkoneau pussuhksesog: stork noh oowekuttamun firuhtukqut.
104.18 Kussuhkoe wadchuash tashpuhhoowaonkanuooash wutche touohkomukque goatsog, kah qussukquanash wutche wuhtukquasuog.
104.19 Kuhquttumup nahneposhadt wutche uttoocheyeuash; nuppauz wahteo oowayaonk.
104.20 Kuppohkinnahteam, kah nuhkanyeuoo: wame touohkomukque puppinashimwog ne wuttut suhwhompakeneau
104.21 Wuskukqunnonoowaog nehnehteaontamog wunnehtoonkanoo, kah natinneahamog ummeetsuonkanoo wutch Godut.
104.22 Pashpishonche muhmoeog, kah sepsinwog oowonogoowout.
104.23 Wosketomp suhham en wuttisseonkanit, kah en wuttanuhkosuonkanit napache wunnunkoout.
104.24 Woi Jehovah uttuh tohshinash kuttanuhkosuonkash! koowaontamwe ussenapash wame: ohke numwohteau koowenawetuonkash.
104.25 {Wonk} yeu missiyeue kah kushkiyeue kehtah, uttuh pamomhittit woh mo waogkemomukkeg, naneswe papeississitcheg kah matukkenukkeg puppinashimwog.
104.26 Na pummushshomoo kuhtoonogquash, {na wuttapin} noh pootop {uttoh} aiyeuohp na wuttut puhpinneat.
104.27 Yeug wame kuppahtissuonukquog; onk woh uttoocheyeue kuttassamonaout.
104.28 {Ne} uttuh assamadt ummukkunumunnau: koowoshwunnum kunnitcheg, nag tapheoog nash wanegik.
104.29 Kupputtogkuhhum kuskesuk, nag wuttamantamwog; kuttammanum wunnashaonkanoo, nuppooog, kah quishkeog en uppuppissiyeumoowout.
104.30 Kussuhwhe annoon kunnashauanittoom, nag kesheoog: kah kooskehteo wosketohke.
104.31 Wussohsumooonk Jehovah pish michemohteau: Jehovah pish mishkouantamoowontam wuttanuhkosuonkash.
104.32 Moninneam ohke, kah nunnuksheau; mussunnum wadchuash, kah nash qussohtaemooash.
104.33 Pish nukketoohomau Jehovoh tuhsahke pomontam: pish noowaenomaoohumau num-Mannittoom as aaieuhp.
104.34 Nunnatwonumaonk pish wekon: pish noowekontam Jehovahut.
104.35 Matcheseaeninnuog mahtuppaehhittich wutch ohkeit, kah matchetooog ohquapehhittich: wunnanim Jehovah, woi nukketeakou waenomoohk Jehovah.
105.1 WOi tapattontumohk Jehovah; wehquttumook oowesuonk: wahtauwahhuwagk wuttisseonkash kunnugke missinninnuut.
105.2 Noh ketoohumohk, unnoohumohk ketoohomaonkash: weogquttumook wame ummuhchantamwe anuhkosuonkash.
105.3 Waenowagk ut oonetuppantamwe wesuonkanit: wuttahhoo wekontamoomooutch nag natinneahwhoncheg Jehovah.
105.4 Natinneahhoohk Jehovah, kah ummunnehkesuonk: natinneahhamook wuskesuk micheme.
105.5 Mehquantamook ummuhchantamwe anuhkosuonkash nesh asehpash; ummuhchantamooonkash kah wuttoone wussittumooonkash.
105.6 Woi kenau ooskanaminneoh Abraham wuttinninnumoh: kenau wunnechonoh Jakob nah papenauuhpah.
105.7 Unnoh Jehovah num-Mannittoomun, oosittumooonkash {ahtaash} mamusse ohkeit.
105.8 Mehquantamup oonoowaonk micheme: unnoowaonk {ne} annoohteamwehp en nukquit muttanonkane pometuonkash.
105.9 {Wunnoowaonk} ne ayumauuhp Abrahamoh, kah wutchadchekeoowaonk en Isackut:
105.10 Kah ne ummunnehkehtauunnap en Jakobut wutche unnomatuonk, kah en Israelut wutche michemohtae wunnoowaonk:
105.11 Unnoowop, Pish kuttununumauush Canaane ohke; kuhkununkane kuttohtoonkanoo.
105.12 Ne {nogkoshittit} wosketompaog: nux, ahche nogkoshittit, kah panoowohteahittit naut.
105.13 Ne ayahittit wutch wuttohtimoinneat en wuttohtimoinneat, wutch {pasuk} assootummooonkanit en onkatog missinninnuut.
105.14 Matta unnanumooop {howae} wosketomp oowoskhukqunaout: nux aiuskomop kehtahsootumwog wutche nag:
105.15 {Unnoowop}, mussunnuhteohk nussussequnnittommog, kah tohhen woskehheuhteohk nukquahshotumaeninnumog.
105.16 Wonk, wehquttumup mohshogquadt ut ohkeit: poohqunnumup mamusse puttukqunonkane anwohoo.
105.17 Wunnekonannootamwanushowoopah wosketomp; {nux} Joseph {noh} magumukup wutche wuttinninnumin.
105.18 Noh wusseettash uhkuhpunnadtouhitteuhp nashpe tohtogkuppissoonash; moouhshogquohtogkuppunnop. |
105.19 Pache adt paomooukup wuttinnoowaonk: wuttinnoowaonk Jehovah ukquitchehhukqunnah.
105.20 Kehtahsoot annoohteamoop kah wuttompunopah: {nux}, noh nanawunuhp missinninnuog, kah uppohquanopah.
105.21 Wussontimmohkonuppah ut wekut, kah wunnanawunumwahheopah wame wuttohtoonk.
105.22 Tohtogkuppunnonat wussontimmomoh annantogish: kah kuhkootumauonat ukkehchiyeumoh waantamooonk.
105.23 Israel wonk peyop en Egypt: kah Jakob unneaappeup wuttohket Ham.
105.24 Kah noh muttaanheop ummissinninnumoh: kah wuttanue munnehkehheopah onk ummatwomoouh.
105.25 Qunnuppunumup wuttahhoo sekinneauonat ummissinninnumoh, ompuwissue unnehheonat wuttinninnumoh.
105.26 Annoonop Moses wuttinninnumoh, kah Aaron neh papenauuhpoh.
105.27 Nag nahtehteopaneg ukkehkinneasuonkash kunnugke nag, kah muhchantamooonkash ut wuttohket Ham.
105.28 Annootamup pohkunnai, kah uppohkunnahtauunap: onk matta chekehtamoopaneg wuttinnoowaonk.
105.29 Qunnuppunumup wunnippemoooash en mishquehhunkanit, kah nushop wunamasoomoouh.
105.30 Wuttohkemooout oochekinneaop monaog tannogkohteasuog, ut wuttashukkomukkoowout ukketassootumoomoouh.
105.31 Kutoop, kah uppeonaop aiane moosuhquoh, {kah} yeuhquoh ut wame wuttohtuout.
105.32 Wunnompunnumauopah mussekon wutche sookunnon: kah noohnoonae noohteau ut wuttohkeout.
105.33 Togkodtamup wonk oowenomsippagkoowoash, kah uffigsuhtukoowoash: kah poohquehtahhamup mehtukquash ut wuttohtuout.
105.34 Kuttoop, kah moopaog peyopaneg, kah chonsompsog, matta woh waogkemomukeg;
105.35 Kah mahchuppoopaneg wame wunnepogquaskehtuash ut wuttohkeout: kah mahchehtamuppaneg wuttohkee mechummuonk.
105.36 Wonk nushop wame mohtommeteuhpah ut wuttohkeout: ne nakoneyeuuk ummunehkesuonkanoo.
105.37 Kah nah ooweche suhhoowunopah silver kah gold: kah matta wunnukquttapeunnah noochumwesu kunnugke wutchuppanooonkanoooash.
105.38 Egypt wekontmup nemoncheh monchehhittit: newutche nag wapissuonaonkanoo wunnuhkuhkunkqunnaop
105.39 Sepakunumup matohqus wutche onkkuhwhonk: kah noohtau wassumwinneat nuhkonae.
105.40 Wehqutumuppaneg, kah uppadtauopah poohpoohqutteh: kah oowamupwehhopah kesukque puttukqunneg.
105.41 Woshwunumup qussuk, kah nippeash na wuttutchuwanup; pummutchuwanuppash nunnapohteaiyeuut onatuh sepuut.
105.42 Newutche mehquantamup wunnetuppantamwe oonoowaonk, kah Abraham wuttinninnumoh.
105.43 Kah wussuhhoowunnopah ummissinninnumoh nashpe wekontamooonk: {kah} papenauuhpah nashpe mushkouantamooonk.
105.44 Kah wuttununumauopah wuttohkemoooash penoowohteaog: kah nag nompohtouppaneg wuttanuhkosuonkanoo missininnuog:
105.45 Onk woh nag usseog ukkuhkoowaonkash, kah nanawehteoog wuttunomatuonkash. Waenomoohk Jehovah.
106.1 WAenomoohk Jehovah, woi tapattontumohk Jehovah, newutche wunetoo, newutche ummonaneteaonk michemohteau.
106.2 Howan woh ontuttuk ummogke usseonkash Jehovah? {howan} woh nahtehteadt wame waenomaonkash.
106.3 Wunnanummoog nag nanawehtunkig wussuttumooonk: kah noh sompweaset naquahteae.
106.4 Mehquanimmeh, woi Jehovah, nashpe koossikkitteaanummaonkanoo kummissinninnumog: woi nattauwahhe nashpe koowadchanuwaonk!
106.5 Onk woh nunnaum ooniyeuonkanoo papenauadtcheg, onk woh nummushkauantam ut oowekontamooonkanit kootohtimoin: onk woh noowaenowam weche kuttahtoonk.
106.6 Nummatchesemunnonup weche noohshunnonog: nuppaneussemunnonup, nummatchesemunnonup.
106.7 Noohshunnonog matta wohtamoopaneg kummuhchantamooonkash ut Egypt, matta mehquantamoopaneg mataanehkish kukkuttumonteanitteaonkash, qut ummoohmooshquehheowoopah ut kehtohhanit, {nux} ut mishque kehtahhanit.
106.8 Qut onch, oowadchonopah wutche oowesuonk: wahtauwahhuwonat ummishe munnehkesuonk.
106.9 Wonk aiuskontumup mishque kehtah, kah nunnoppiyeup: nemehkuh uppannuppuwunnopah moonoiyeuut onatuh tauohkomukqut.
106.10 Kah oowadchonopah wutch wunnitcheganit sakinneunkhitteuhp: kah uppohquahwhunopah wutch wunnitcheganit matwau.
106.11 Kah ummatwomoouh nuhkuhkunkuppaneg nippeash: kah matta pasuk wuttisqueyeuup.
106.12 Neit wunnomuhtamuppaneg ukkuttooonkash, unnoohhumopaneg waenomaonk
106.13 Teanuk wannantamuppaneg wuttannuhkosuonkash, matta pahtooopaneg ukkunnoosoowaonk:
106.14 Qut moocheke kogkodtauontamuppaneg ut touohkamukqut, kah qutchehheopaneg Godoh ut touweyeuut.
106.15 Kah wuttununumauopah oowehquttummooonkanoo, qut annootamup onauussuonk en ukketeahogkonoowout.
106.16 Nag wonk eskauwonopaneg Mosesoh ut tuppuhkussunooonkanit, {kah} Aaron oonetuppantamoomoh Jehovah.
106.17 Ohke woshwemoop kah mishashkoop Dathanoh, kah nuhkuhkomoomoop wutchassooonk Abiram.
106.18 Kah noohtau nashqunnanoseup ut wutchassooonkanoowout; matchetooog ummahchukkisukqunaop noohnooneau.
106.19 Kesheopaneg Calfoh ut Horeb, kah wawussumopaneg sunnuppohtae unninneuhkontunk.
106.20 Yeu wuttinne osoowunumunnaop wussohsumooonkanoo en wuttogquinneunkqussuonkanit ox noh machuk moskehtuash.
106.21 Wannanumopaneg God oowadchanuwaeninnumoouh, uttuh aseph makakish ut Egypt:
106.22 Muhchantamwe anuhkosuonkash ut wuttohket Ham, kah ukqunneunkquohkish keshke mishque kehtahhanit.
106.23 Newutche unnoowop, woh nuppaquanoog, Moses noh papenauuhp matta nepookus anuhquapit adt touwunnusik, ukqushkunumunat ummooshquantamooonk, eshkont woh uppaquanuh.
106.24 Nux, meshannantamuppaneg wunnaogohke: matta wunnomuhtamoopaneg wuttinoowaonk:
106.25 Qut moohmooshkoowopaneg ut wekoowout, kah matta kuhkehtamoopaneg oowadtauohtunkqussooonk Jehovah.
106.26 Newutche aiyeuohkone tashunummauuhp wunnitcheg uppaquanonat, ut touohkomukqut:
106.27 Wonk punnishohhonat ooskanemunnoouh kunnugke wuttohtimoinneunk, kah nag sewohhonat ut ohkeit.
106.28 Wonk mosogquehheopaneg wohhogauh en Baal-peor; kah mechuppaneg wussephosuonkanoo napukeg.
106.29 Yeu wuttinne mooshquehhonaop nashpe wuttogkunnaiantamooonkanoowoash: kah nuhkuhkunkuppaneg wesoshaonk.
106.30 Neit Phinehas nepoup, kah usseup wussuttumooonk: onk wesoshaonk togkogunnoseup.
106.31 Kah ne ogquantamauonah wutche sampweusseonk, en wame pometuonkanit micheme.
106.32 Nag wonk ummoohmooshquehhowoopah ut penooanittue nippeit; onk matchehpunop Moses newutche nag:
106.33 Newutche moohmooshquehteouppaneg wunnahshauonk; onk koshkommoowop nashpe wussussuttoonash.
106.34 Matta pagwanooopaneg wuttohtimoinneash, nag papaume Jehovah annoonuhpah:
106.35 Qut kunnugshopaneg penoowohteaut, kah nehtuhtooopaneg wuttanuhkosuonkanoowoash.
106.36 Kah wuttinninneumuhkouopaneg wuttinnineuhkontunkanoowooh; uttuh ahpehanuwehhitteuhp en wohhogaout.
106.37 Nux, sephosupaneg wunnamonauh kah wuttonoouh en mattannittoout.
106.38 Kah sookishquanumuppaneg matta woskehhuwae mishquehheunk, {nux}, ooshquehheunkanoo wunnamonauh, kah wuttonoouh, uttuh saposhitteuhppah en Canaane unninneuhkontunkanit: kah ohke neskehtoseup nashpe mishquehheunk.
106.39 Yeu wuttinne neskehhukquisinneaop nashpe nehenwonche wuttanuhkosuonkanoowoash, kah nannunnootsquaosupaneg nashpe nehenwonche wuttogkunniantammooonkanoowoash.
106.40 Newutche ummooshquantamooonk Jehovah nashqunnop aiyeuohkone ummissinninnumut; en wuttuhquantamunnat nehenwonche wutohtoonk.
106.41 Kah nah ummakunapah en wunnitchegkonoowout penoowohteaog; kah nag sekinneunkhitteuhp, nanawunukuppaneg.
106.42 Ummatwomoouh wonk uhquanumwehhukuppaneg, onk ogquappehheopaneg wunnitchekonoowout.
106.43 Ummochekut pohquohwhunnopah, qut ummoohmooshquehhowoopah nashpe ukkunnoosoowaonkanoo, kah noochumwehheopaneg nashpe ummatcheseonkanoo.
106.44 Qut onch, moninneamup ootamehpunnaonkanoo, notog ummauonkanoo.
106.45 Kah ummehquantamauopah oonoowaonk, kah aiuskoiantamup neane muttaanehke ukkuttummonteanitteaonkash.
106.46 Kah wuttununumauopah woh ukuttumonteanumukqunaout wame nah masunnohkonukquehhitteuhp.
106.47 Wadchaninnean, woi Jehovah num-Mannittoomun, kah muhmonunninnean wutch kunnugke penoowohteaut, tapattontumunat en koonetuppantamwe wesuonkanit, {kah} waenowonat ut koowaenomitteaonkanit.
106.48 Wunnanumunnaj Jehovah um-Mannitoomoh Israel, wutch michemeyeuut en michemeyeuut, kah wame missinninnuog unnoowahhittich, Amen. Waenomoohk Jehovah.
107.1 WOi tapattontumohk Jehovah, newutche wunnetoo: newutche ukkuttummonteanitteaonk michemohteau.
107.2 Nah Jehovah pohquohwunnahpah ne unnoowahhittich, uttuh pohquohwhunnuhpah wutch wunnitchekonut matwau:
107.3 Kah nah uppohquohwhunopah wutch wuttohtimoinneat, wutch wompaniyeu kah maquamittiniyeu, wutch nanumiyeu kah sowaniyeu.
107.4 Nanwushopaneg ut touohkomukqut ut touiyeue mayut: wanne namehtooopaneg ootan woh watohkemuk.
107.5 Kodtupwehhittit kah kuhkuttoonhittit, ukketeahogkonoouh sauunumuppah ut wuttunomiyeumooout.
107.6 Neit mauinittauopaneg Jehovah ut ootamehpunnaonkanoowout, {kah} uppohquohwhunopah wutche wuttuhquanumooonkanaowout.
107.7 Kah wussuhhoowunopah ut sompwe mayut, onk woh auog wuttohkeae ootannat.
107.8 Napehnont {wosketompaog} waenomahhittit Jehovah {wutche} oonetooonk, kah muhchantamwe wuttanuhkosuonkash en wunnechonoowout wosketompaog.
107.9 Newutche tapehhau nontweanumooe keteahogkou, kah tapupwehhau kodtuppooe keteahogkou nashpe wanegik.
107.10 Nag apitcheg pohkunniyeuut kah nuppooe onkauuhtaut, tohtogkuppissitcheg ut uhquanumooonkanut kah moouhshogqut:
107.11 Newutche chekehtamuppaneg wuttunoowoonk God, kah meshanantamuppaneg ukkunnoosoowaonk anue quanuhquapit:
107.12 Newutche hohpahteop wuttahoo nashpe anuhkosuonk, kepshopaneg kah {na} matta howanuunnoop woh anunoset.
107.14 Neit mauinnittauopaneg Jehovah ut ootamehpunaonkanoowout: kah uppohquohwhunopah wutch wuttuhquanumooonkanoowout.
107.14 Wussuhhoowunopah wutch pohkuniyeuut, kah wutch nuppooonkane onkauuhtaut, kah pashkishsthattooop wuttohtogkuppissunoowoash.
107.15 Napehnont {wosketompaog} waenomahhittit Jehovah {wutche} oonetooonk, kah ummuhchantamwe anuhkosuonkash en wunnechonoowout wosketompaog.
107.16 Newutche poohkshadtoup wompuhshogque kuppehhegash, kah tummehthamup moouhshogque punmettomppontegash.
107.17 Mattammagwog ukkuhpunnaog, wutche uppaneusseonkanoo, kah wutche ummatcheusseonkanoo.
107.18 Ukketeahogkonoouh uhquantamwog nishnoh unnummechumogkod, onk pasoosuhkomwog nuppooonkane usquontamash.
107.19 Neit mauinnittauaog Jehovah ut ootamehpunaonkanoowout; {kah} oowadchonuh, wutch wuttuhquanumooonkanoowout.
107.20 Anootamup wuttunoowaonk, kah nah wunnetskehheopah, kah uppohquohwhunopah wutch uppagquanuonkanoowoash.
107.21 Napehnont {wosketompaog} waenomahhittit Jehovah {wutche} oonetooonk, kah ummuhchatamwe anuhkosuonkash en wunnechonoowout wosketompaog.
107.22 Kah sephoshittich tapattontumooe sephosuonkash, kah muskouantamwe wahtouwahhuwahttich wuttanuhkosuonkash.
107.23 Nag aoncheg kehtahhanit ut kuhtoonogquehtu, anuhkositcheg ut mishe nippehkuhtu:
107.24 Yeug naumwog wuttanuhkosuonkash Jehovah, kah ummuhchantamooonkash ut moonoiyeuut.
107.25 Newutche anoohteamoo kah mishehtashinehteo, uttuh tahshunuk ketahhanontukquoh.
107.26 Nag tahsheog en kesukqut, womussuog wonk en moonoiyeuut; ukketeahogkonoouh mahtupaeoh nashpe wuttamehpunaonk.
107.27 Kehkeetukquoog, kah kotkehkepshaog onatuh kakesuppadt; kah wohkuhquoianumooog.
107.28 Neit mauinnittauwaog Jehovah ut ootamehpunaonkanoowout; kah nah wussuhhoowunuh wutch wuttuhquanumooonkanoowout
107.29 Auwepunehteo mishehtashin, onk kehtahhanontukquog mohkoemooash.
107.30 Neit wekontamwog newutche mohkoemooit; nemuhkuh uppasoouh aiyeuonkanit ne kodtantamwehittit.
107.31 Napehnont {wosketompaog} waenomahhittit Jehovah {wutche} oonetooonk, kah ummuhchantamwe anuhkosuonkash en wunnechonoowout wosketompaog.
107.32 Nag wonk mishehheahhittich ut ummukkinneonkanoowout missinninnuog, kah waenomahhittich ut ummoeonkanoowout kehchehhiog.
107.33 Tauohkomukquehteau sepuash, kah nunnoppohteaiyeuehteau tohkekamuash:
107.34 Mehcheyeuehteau mahmussekuk ohke wutche ummatchetooonkanoo nag na watohkecheg.
107.35 Nuppissippaquehteau touohkomuk, kah tohkekommuehteau nunnopohteai.
107.36 Kah na ootahkeaheon kodtupwunitcheh, onk woh quohshaweteoog ootan woh watohkemuk;
107.37 Kah woh ohteuhkonehteaog, kah wenominneahteuhkonehteoog, uttoyeu woh mashimmechummoouk.
107.38 Nah oonanumuh wonk, onk nag muttaanoowahheoog, kah matta unnanumooo wunnetohsoomoouh nano wunnagkosunaout.
107.39 Wonk, nagkosehheoog kah nawaehheoog nashpe uhquanumwehhittuonk, wuttamehpunnaonk kah noowehpunnaonk.
107.40 Sookunumauau sontimuh meshananittuonk, kah wunnanwushshahheuh ut touohkomukqut, uttuh mo adt maynook.
107.41 Qut onch qunnuhquapehheau machekoooh wutch wuttamehpunnaonkanit, kah wutteashinninneonkanehheuh, onatuh flockut.
107.42 Sompweseaeninyeuog pish wunnamunneau, kah pish mishkouantamwog; kah wame matcheusseonk pish kupputtoonaemoo.
107.43 Howan noh waontog, kah pish yeush kahkinneasit, kah nag pish wahtomwog ummonaneteaonkash Jehovah.
108.0
108.1 WOi God, nuttah kesantamoomoo, pish nukketoohumom kah noowaenomuam, nux nashpe nussohsumooonk.
108.2 Toohkeg Psaltery kah Harp: nehenwonche nen pish nompoaeu nuttookkem.
108.3 Pish koowaenomush, woi Jehovah, kunnugke missinninnuut pish ketoohomae koowaenomush kunnugke wuttohtimoinneunk.
108.4 Newutche kummonanitteaonk mussi en aonkkaue kesukqut: kah koonomwaonk en matokqsut.
108.5 Misshehhitteash, woi God, waape kesukqut: kah kussohsumooonk anue qunnuhquohtaj mamusse ohke.
108.6 Onk woh pohquohwhunou noh wamonadt: wachanuash nashpe kuttunnuhkou, kah nompoohumah.
108.7 God unnoowop ut oonetuppantamooonkanit, pish nummushkouantam; pish nutchupunum Shechem, kah nukquokquadhum Succothe oonouuhkoi.
108.8 Gilead nuttaihe, Manasseh nuttaihe, Ephraim wonk ummunehkesuonk nuppuhkuhk, Judah nootinomatuonkannehteaeninneum.
108.9 Moab nuttohtoochukkutshohkuhkoom, woskeche Edom pish nuppumuhkon nummohkus: pish nummishkouantam waape Philistia.
108.10 Howan pish passoowit en manuhkak ootannat? howan pish assoowussit en Edomut?
108.11 Sun matta pish ken, woi God, {noh} papogkenukqueogup? kah {sun} matta {pish} ken, woi God, matta wahwechaohp nuttahhontannooonkanunonash?
108.12 Anunummaiinnean wutch wuttamehpunaonkanut: newutche wuttanunosuonk wosketomp tohnoocheyeumoo.
108.13 Nashpe God pish nukkenompae ussemun: newutche nakum noh pish tahtaskuhkouont nummatwomunnonog.
109.0
109.1 Chequnapehkon, woi Mannit noh waenomog.
109.2 Newutche wuttoon matchetuk, kah wuttoon assookehkodteadt nuttaiyeuohkonittue woshwunnummonteanash: nuttaiyeuohkonittue kekuttoohkonkquog nashpe panoowae menan.
109.3 Noowenuhkonkuppaneg wonk nashpe sekinneoatue kuttooonkash: kah nuttaiyeukuppaneg tahnooche.
109.4 Wutche noowamoahsuonk, nag noomatwominneunk: qut nen nuppompeuhtam.
109.5 Kah nag nuttunkquatunkuppaneg machuhk wutche wanegik, kah sekinneoadtuonk wutche noowamoahsuonk.
109.6 Noh wussontimmomuhkau maatchetuk: kah Mattannit nepauitch wuttunuhkounit.
109.7 Wussumut mahchinnuwonunnaj, kah uppeuhtamooonk matcheseonkkanuitch.
109.8 Ukkesukodumash nagkosinnuitch, kah wuttunashketompoooonk onkatog neminitch.
109.9 Wunnechonoh matta wuttooshhittitch, kah ummuttumwussusoh sekouushquaitch.
109.10 Wunnechonoh naquahteae nanwaihittitch, kah wenshahhitich: natinneahamwehhittich {upputtukquinnunkanoo} wonk wutch touweyeue wuttiyeuonkanoowout.
109.11 Unnuhtukquohhoowaenin tohquinitch wame ne ahtunk: kah penoowoht matchehtauitch wuttanuhkosuonk.
109.12 Ahque howanuooitch woh kodtumonteanumukquit: howan tohhen monanumuhkitch wuttauwaesumoh.
109.13 Wuttontusseonk tummehthamunnaj, {kah} ut ne nahohtoeyeuuk pometuonk oowesuonkanoo cheskhamunnaj.
109.14 Ummatcheusseonkanoo oohshog mehquantamunnaj anuhquapit Jehovah: kah uppaneusseonk oohkasoh cheskhosunoohkitch.
109.15 Nash naquahteahtaj anuhquapit Jehovah, onk woh tummehtham mehquanumaonkanoo wutch ohkeit.
109.16 Newutche matta mehquantamoop monanukkonat, qut wunnomattehtwhop matchekoo kah quenawehkooenin, onk woh wunnushonat pohqueteahhonitcheh.
109.17 Neane wommontogup mattanitteaonk, neunne nuhkuhkunkquitch: neane matta tapinueamookup wunnanitteaonk neunne nooosuhkunkquitch.
109.18 Neane ogquannuhp wohhogkuh mattanitteaonk onatuh nashpe ogkoo: neunne petutteamooutch en wunnogkusseit onatuh nippeit, kah ogque pummeit en wuskkonut.
109.19 Tatuppeyeuitch en wohhogkat ogkooonkanit {ne} onkhukquit, kah wutche puttukquapus ne padtukquapissit naquahteae.
109.20 Yeu ununkquattunkanahhittitch nummatwomog wutch Jehovahut, kah nag aiyeuohkone matche unnoche nukketeahogkou.
109.21 Qut usseanisheh, woi Jehovah Mannit, newutche koowesuonk: Newutche kummonanitteaonk wunnegen, pohquahwhusseh.
109.22 Newutche nummatchek kah nukquenawehhuk, kah nuttah noochumwehtahwhou ut nuttunnomiyeumut.
109.23 Nummahche ammaem onatuh onkauuhtaut ne watonchemoouk: nuppoppomuhkonit onatuh chansomsut.
109.24 Nukkuttukquash noochumwiyeuash ne mo mametseon: kah nooweyaus wanehteooomoo wunnogkooonk.
109.25 Wonk nuttushpunamuaonkanyeuup en wohhogaout: ne monuneihittit nunnukkuhquohshopaneg.
109.26 Anunumah, woi Jehovah num-Mannittoom: wadchaneh neanag kummonanitteaonk:
109.27 Onk woh nag unnoowahteoog, yeu kunnitcheg: onk ken, Jehovah, kuttissenap.
109.28 Mattanitteahittich, qut ken wunnanitteash: nag omuhkehhittit, ogkodchhittich: qut kuttinninneum mashkouantaj.
109.29 Nummatwomog ogquehhittich ogkodchuonk: kah onkuhwhahhittich wohhogauh nashpe wutchepshaanumooonkanoo, neane nashpe ogkoo.
109.30 Pish nummishe waenom Jehovah nashpe nuttoon: nux, pish noowaenom kunnugke manacheg.
109.31 Newutche pish nepau wuttunuhkounit matchekoo, noh wadchononat wutch nah mahchinnuonocheg uketeahogkonoh.
110.0
110.1 JEhovah unnop nussontimmom, appish nuttunnuhkonut, napajeh kummatwomog kuttahpanehtuonkanuhkouununat.
110.2 Jehovah pish annootam kummunehkesue pogkomunk wutch Sionut: nanawinyeuash ut noeu kummatwomut.
110.3 Kummissinninnumog {pish} wuttunantamunneau ut munnehkesue kukkesukodumut, ut wunnetue wunnetuppantamooonkanit wutch nompoe otomukut: kuttohto kooskeninnue nehchuppog.
110.4 Jehovah chadchekeyeuop, kah matta pish aiuskoiantamoo, kussephosuaeninyeu micheme, neanakup wussephosueninyeuonk Melchizedek.
110.5 Lord ut kuttunuhkounnut pish pannuppehtahwhau kehtassootumwog ut mooshquantamwe ukkesukodumut.
110.6 Pish wussuttum kenugke penoowohteaog, pish numwohteo {aiyeuonkash} nuppooe mohhogash: pish noochumwehtham muppuhkuhquash wahwame mishe wuttohtimmoinneash.
110.7 Pish oochehpissimin sepuut ut mayuhkontu: newajeh pish tahshunuk muppuhkuhk.
111.1 WAenomuhk Jehovah. pish noowoenom Jehovah nashpe mamusse nuttah, ut ummoeonkanoowout sampwutteahhoncheg, kah ut mukkinneonkanut.
111.2 Wuttanuhkosuonkash Jehovah missiyeuash, wunnattinneahkontamunnaoash wame nag wekontamoowontogig.
111.3 Wuttanuhkosuonk quhtiantamweneunkquat kah sohsumooweneunkquat: kah wussampweusseonk michemohteau.
111.4 Mehquantamwahhuwop muhchantamwe wuttanuhkosuonkash: Jehovah monanitteau kah kogkuttummonteanitteau.
111.5 Unnunumauop metissuonk nah quahshukqutcheh: pish micheme momehquantam oonoowaonk.
111.6 Nahtinop ummissinninnumoh munnehkesue wuttanuhkosuonkash; onk woh wuttunumauuh wuttahtoonkanoo penoowohteaog.
111.7 Wunnitchegane anuhkosuonkash wunnomwwaeyeuooash, kah wussuttummooonkanyeuooash; wame wuttannoohteamooonkash wunnummuhkiteyeuooash.
111.8 Munnehtukkompattaash micheme kah micheme, {kah} ussenash ut wunnomwaeyeuut kah sampwiyeuut.
111.9 Annootamup mannoohwhuttuonk en ummissinninnumut, annooteamoop oonoowaonk micheme: wunnetuptamweyeumoo, kah quehtiantamweyeumoo oowesuonk.
111.10 Qushaonkanit Jehovah ut kutchishin waantamooonk: winne oowohwohtamooonkanyeuog wame nag asecheg wuttannoohteamooonkash: waenomaonk michemohteau.
112.1 WAenomoohk Jehovah. Wunnanumou wosketomp quohshont Jehovah, {noh} mishe wakontamoowontog wuttannoohteamooonkash.
112.2 OOshkanneminneoh pish matikkenwoh ut ohkeit: uppometuonkanoo sampwesitcheg pish wunnanumoog.
112.3 Moochukahtoonk kah wenawetuonk, {pish ohteau} wekut: kah wussampweusseonk michemohteau.
112.4 Sampwutteahhoncheg wapehtunkquog wequai ut pohkenaiyeuut: noh monanitteau, kah mishe kuttumonteanitteau, kah sampwesu.
112.5 Wunnetooenin monaneteae unnehhuwau, kah namohkouwehhuwau; pish nanawunum wuttuniyeuonkash nashpe waantamooonk.
112.6 Wunnumuhkit matta pish ontapehhou micheme: sampwesuenin pish micheme momehquanumou.
112.7 Pish matta quehtamoo matonchumooonkash: wuttah kesantamoomoo, pabahtanumau Jehovah.
112.8 Wuttah chetamwehtosoo, matta pish wapissu, napajeh wunnamunnat ukkodtantamooonk ut ummatwomut.
112.9 Chadchapunumup, unnunumauop matchekoooh; wussampweusseonk michemohteau; wuttaskon pish tashunumun nashpe quehtianittuonk.
112.10 Matchetoo pish wunnamun, kah eskauontam; pish chuhquanussun, kah mohtuppaeu: ukkodtantamooonkanoo matchetooog pish wohkuhquoemoo.
113.1 WAenomoohk Jehovah. Waenomuwak, woi kenau wuttinninnumoh Jehovah, waenotumoohk oowesuonk Jehovah.
113.2 Wunnantamunnaj oowesuonk Jehovah, yeu wutch yoyatche kah micheme.
113.3 Wutch adt pashpishont en na adt waiont, oowesuonk Jehovah woh waenotumun.
113.4 Jehovah anuuhquaputam wame wuttohtimmoinneash, kah wussohsumooonk waape kesukquash.
113.5 Howan aquinneunkquissit Jehovah num-Mannittoomun, noh quanuhquiit?
113.6 Noh ohhohpaheont wohhogkuh namunnat {nesh ohtakish} kesukqut kah ohkeit.
113.7 Omuhkunau matchekoooh wutch puppissiyeuut, kah tahshunau quenauwehhukquinnitcheh wutch anohquontamut;
113.8 Onk woh oowetapehheuh sontimout, nux weche wussontimmomoouh ummissinninnumoh.
113.9 Nanauukkamukquahheau mehchetumwussussoh, {kah} ummushkauantamwe wunnechonooe wuttoohkasinneahheuh. Waenomoohk Jehovah.
114.1 NE suhhog Israel wutch Egyptut, wek Jacob wutch penooontoowae missinninnuut.
114.2 Judah oonetuppantamweyeuinneapah, kah oonanawunnumooonkaninneah Israeloh.
114.3 Kehtah wunnamunnap, kah wussemooup; Jordan ahsohthomunnah.
114.4 Wodchuash quehquesishopash onatuh ramsut, kah wadchuemesash onatuh lambsut.
114.5 Toh kuttushpunnamus, woi kehtoh, waj wussemweoph? ken Jordan, waj ahsohtahwhitteaohp?
114.6 Kenau wadchuash, waj quehquesishaogus onatuh ramsut; kah kenau wadchuemesash onatuh lambsut?
114.7 Nunnukishshash ken ohke anuhquapit Lord, anuhquapit um-Mannittoomoh Jacob.
114.8 Noh ohtootopaquehtadt qussuk, tahkekommuehteadt sogohtonkanompusk.
115.1 Matta en nohhoganonut, woi Jehovah, matta en nohhoganonut, qut makush sohsumooonk en koowesuonkanit, wutche kummonaneteaonk, {kah} wutche koonomwaonk.
115.2 Toh waj woh penoowoteaog unnoowahhittit, Tonoh yeuyeu um-Mannittoomoouh?
115.3 Qut num-Mannittoomun oppu kesukqut: mahche usseu nishnoh annantogup.
115.4 Wuttinneuhkontunkanoouh silveruoowoh kah golduoowoh, wunnitchegane anuhkosuonkanoo wosketompaog.
115.5 Wuttoonuog, qut matta kuttooog; wuskesukkooog, qut matta namooog.
115.6 Wehtauogkooog, qut matta nootamooog; wutchonnuog, qut matta munnontamooog.
115.7 Wunnitchegannuog, qut matta weogkunutchontamooog; wussetuog, qut matta pumuhshoooog; asuh matta kuttooog ut ukquttunkanoowout
115.8 Nag kesheoncheg wuttogquinneunkquissinneauh; {wonk} nishnoh pasuk nah pabahtanumoncheh.
115.9 Woi ken Israel, pabahtanum Jehovah: noh nah wuttanunnosueninnumoouh, kah wuttogqunnegkonoouh.
115.10 Woi wek Aaron, pabahtanum Jehovah: noh nah wuttanonosuaeninnumoouh kah wuttogquinneganoouh.
115.11 Kenau quahshaquish Jehovah, pabahtanumoohk Jehovah: noh wuttanunnosueninnumoouh kah wuttogquinnegannoouh.
115.12 Jehovah kummomehquanumukqunonup, pish koonanumukqun, pish wunnantam wek IsraeI, pish wunnantam wek Aaron.
115.13 Pish wunnanumau nah quohshoncheg Jehovah, matikkenitcheg kah papesissesitcheg.
115.14 Jehovah pish nano kukkokootinnehhukkoo, kenau kah kunechonoowoog.
115.15 Koonanumukoo Jehovah, noh kasehtunkup kesuk kah ohke.
115.16 Kesukque kesukquash ootiheinneash Jehovah: qut ohke wuttununumauonaop wunnechonoouh wosketompaog.
115.17 Napukig matta waenomoooog Jehovah, asuh matta pasuk nag womsitcheg en chequnniinneat.
115.18 Qut nenawun pish noonanumomun Jehovah, yeu wutch yoyache kah micheme. Waenomoohk Jehovah.
116.1 NOOwomon Jehovah: newutche nootamup noowadtauohtunkquissuonk, {kah} noowehquttumooonkash
116.2 Newutche nuttahchuissuttunkup, newaje pish wowehquttumauog toh sohke pomantam.
116.3 Nuppooe nooantamooonkash noowenuhkunkqunnapash, chepiohkomukque uhquommomooonkash nuttohqunukqunapash: nummushkomup wuttamantamooonk kah nooantamooonk.
116.4 Neit noowehquttumup oowesuonk Jehovah; woi Jehovah, kunnanompassumush, pohquahwhus nukketeahogkou.
116.5 Monaneteau Jehovah, kah samwesu: nux num-Mannittoomun kogkuttumonteanitteau.
116.6 Jehovah wadchonau pasukquinutteahhoncheh: nukkuttumunkhitteap, kah nuttanumunkup.
116.7 Quishkish en kuttanwosunooonkanut, woi nukketeahogkou: newutche Jehovah kukkogkuttame unnehhukup.
116.8 Newutche kuppohquohwhunomp nukketeahogkou wutch nuppooonkanit, nuskesukquash wutch mussuppegquonut, {kah} nussetash wutch punishonat.
116.9 Pish nuppompummusham anuhquapit Jehovah, ut tanuppomantamwe ohkeit.
116.10 Noonomuhtamup, newaje kuttoouhp: nummishe uhkuhpunap.
116.11 Newutche nissip ut noowopantamooonkanit, Wame wosketompaog pannoowaeninyeuog
116.12 Teaguas woh ompontunumauog Jehovah, wutche wame nooneunnehkukooonkash?
116.13 Pish nunnemunnum wadchanittue wuttattamaetch, kah noowehquttum oowesuonk Jehovah.
116.14 Pish nuttoadtuhkou Jehovah nukquashomaonkash, yeuyeu ut anuhquapunnit wame ummissinninnumoh.
116.15 Ut anuhquapit Jehovah, mushoadtumoo wunnuppooonkanoo oonetuppantamoomoh.
116.16 Woi Jehovah, wunnumuhkit nen kuttinninneum, nen kuttinninneum, kah wunnnamonoh muttumsisse kuttinninneum: kuttompunnumup nukkinippissuonkash.
116.17 Pish kussephamauush tappattontumooe sphosuonk, kah pish noowehquttum oowesuonk Jehovah.
116.18 Pish nuttoadtuhkou Jehovah nukquashomaonkash, yeuyeu ut anuhquapunnit wame ummissinninnumoh:
116.19 Ut wutchadchapukkomukqut Jehovah, ut noeu ken, woi Jerusalem. Waenomoohk Jehovah.
117.1 WOi waenomoohk Jehovah, wame kenau wuttotimonneunk: waenomoohk, wame kenau missinninnuog.
117.2 Newutche womoassue ukkuttumonteanitteaonk missi en kohhogkanonut: kah oonomwaonk Jehovah michemohteau. Waenomoohk Jehovah.
118.1 WOi tapatantumohk Jehovah, newutche wunnetoo: newutche ukkuttumonteanitteonk michemohteau.
118.2 Israel yeuyeu unnoowaj, ukkuttumonteanitteaonk michemohteau.
118.3 Wek Aaron yeuyeu unnoowomooutch, ukkuttumonteanitteaonk michemohteau.
118.4 Nag quohshoncheg Jehovah yeuyeu unnoowahhittitch, ukkuttumonteaneteaonk michemohteau.
118.5 Noowehquttumauop Jah ut nootamehpunnaonkanit: Jah nunnompoohumonkup, kah nuppoonukup pabahchaiyeuonkanit.
118.6 Johovah noowetchoohhumuk, matta pish noowapissu: Toh woh nuttinnehhuk wosketomp?
118.7 Jehovah nunnontumunk weche nag anunumunkqueoneg: newutche pish nunnaum {nukkodtantamooonk} ut wohhogaout sekinaiutcheg.
118.8 Anue wunnegin pabahtanumonat Jehovah, neit pabahtanumonat wosketomp.
118.9 Anue wunnegin pabahtanumonat Jehovah, neit pabahtanumonat sontimoog.
118.10 Wame wuttohtimoinneash noowenukkunkuppaneg: qut ut oowesuonkanit Jehovah pish nuppagquannoog.
118.11 Noowenuhkunkuppaneg, nux noowenuhkunkuppaneg: qut ut oowesuonnkait Jehovah pish nuppagquanoog.
118.12 Nuttogque wenuhkunkuppaneg aohkeomuasit, uhtwhog neane koesue nootaut: newutche ut oowesuonkanit Jehovah pish nuppaquanoog.
118.13 Kummunnehke kutchittuhkonip onk woh nippinishonat: qut Jehovah nuttanummunkup.
118.14 Jah nummunehkesuonk kah nuttinoohhumaonk: kah {noh} noowadchanitteaonkanunneai.
118.15 Mushkouantamwe kah wadchanittue wadtouohtunkquissuonk {ohteau} wekoowout sompwesitcheg: wuttunuhkou Jehovah kenompae ussemoo.
118.16 Wuttunnuhkou Jehovah tahshunnosu: wuttunuhkou Jehovah kenompae ussemoo.
118.17 Matta pish nunnuppoo, qut {pish} nuppomantam, kah pish nuttontuttum wuttanuhkosuonkash Jah.
118.18 Jah nuttuhque sassamuhtuhhukup, qut matta makoop nohhog en nuppooonkanit.
118.19 Washwunnummiegq sampweseonkane usquontamash: pish nuppetuteaontamunnash, kah noowaenom Jah:
118.20 Yeu oosquontam Jehovah, uttuh pish petutteaontamwehittit sampwesitcheg.
118.21 Pish koowaenomush, newutche kunnootaiip, kah noowadchanitteaonkanunneai kohhog
118.22 Qussuk ne wekehteaninyeuog matta tapinneamhitteup, muppuhkuhkoomooai adt nashik.
118.23 Yeu wuttusseonk Jehovah; muhchantamwinneunkquat ut nuskesukqunnonut.
118.24 Yeu ne kesukod Jehovah kesehtunkup, pish na nuttut mushkauantamunnan kah wekontamunnan.
118.25 Woi Jehovah, koowehquttumauush, yeuyeu wadchanuash: woi Jehovah koowehquttumauush, yeuyeu wunnuhkommaiahhuwash.
118.26 Wunnanumou noh paont ut oowesuonkanit Jehovah: koonannumunumunonup wutch wekut Jehovah.
118.27 Mannit {unnuh} Jehovah, uttuh nahtunukqueogup wequai; ogkupputtoook sephosuonkash nashpe peminneahtoneash, ut Altare askonut.
118.28 Ken num-Mannittoom pish koowaenomush; ken num-Mannittoom, pish kuttahshunush.
118.29 Woi tapattantumohk Jehovah, newutche wunnetoo: newutche ukkuttumonteanitteaonk michemohteau.
119.1 Wunnanumoog panuppe pahkesitcheg ut mayut, nag pomshacheg wuttunomatuonkanit Jehovah.
119.2 Wunnanumoog nag nanawehtunkig oowauwaonkash, {kah} natinneahwoncheg nashpe mamusse wuttohhoo.
119.3 Nag wonk wanne matcheusseog: pomuhshaontamog ummayash.
119.4 Kuttannoosumunnonup wuttooe nanawehteauunnat kukkodteahquttumooonkash.
119.5 Woi nummayash sompwehtosik nanawehteauunnat kukkuhkoowaonkash!
119.6 Neit pish matta nuttogkodchuh, wuttooontamon wame kuttannoohteamooonkash.
119.7 Pish koowaenomush nashpe sampwutteahhaonk, mahche nehtuhtauon kussompwe wussuttumooonkash.
119.8 Pish nunnanawehteo kukkuhkoowaonkash: woi papukquane ohquanumehkon.
119.9 Teag woh wuskenin wunnashpe pahkehteauun ummay? nashpe wunnunukquissuontamooonk neanag kuttunoowaonk.
119.10 Nashpe mamusse nuttah kunnatinneahwhunup: woi ahque waonutti wutch kuttannoohteamooonkanit.
119.11 Nuttattohtauunnap kuttinnoowaonk ut nuttahhut, onk woh mat kummatcheunnehhunooh.
119.12 Koonanimit, woi Jehovah: kuhkootumah kukkuhkoowaonkash.
119.13 Nashpe nussissittoonash nuttontuttumup wame kuttoone wussuttumooonkash.
119.14 Nuttunukkuhque mushkouantamup ut koowauwaonkane mayut, neane ut wame wenawetuonkanit.
119.15 Pish nunnatwontam ut kukkodteahquttumoonkanit, kah nootooantam kummayash.
119.16 Pish noowekontamwah nohhog ut kukkuhkoowaonkanit: matta pish noowannantamooh kuttinoowaonk.
119.17 Kogkuttame unneh kuttinninneum; {onk} woh nuppomontam, kah {woh} nunnanawehteo kuttinnoowaonk.
119.18 Woshwunush nuskesukquash, onk woh nunnaum muhchantamweyeuukish wutch kuttinnomatuonkanit.
119.19 Nuppenoowohteau ut ohkeit; adtohtaiehkon kuttannoohteamooonkash.
119.20 Nukketeahogkou poohkshau nashpe wunnontweantamooonk wutche koosuttumooonkash naquahteaeu.
119.21 Kuttaiuskomomp pahtuanumitcheg nag mattanumitcheg, yeug panne aocheg wutch kuttannoohteamooonkanit.
119.22 Ontohtauush wutch nohhogat ushpannatuonk kah meshannanittooonk: newutch nunnanawehteop koowauwaonkash.
119.23 Sontimmoog wonk nummattapue nummammatcheunnukuppaneg: qut kuttinninneum natwantamup ut kukkuhkoowaonkanit.
119.24 Koowauwaonkash wonk nootapinneamooonkaninneash, {kah} nookunoosuwaeninneuminneash.
119.25 Nukketahogou pussogquamoo en puppussiyeuut: quaquahkqheh neanag kuttinnoowaonk.
119.26 Noowahtauwahhuwop nummayash, kah kunnootaiup: kuhkootummah kukkuhkoowaonkash.
119.27 Wahtamwahhe kukkodteahquttumooe may: onk pish nooweogquttum kummuhchantamwe anuhkosuonkash.
119.28 Nukketeahogkou mahtuppaemoo nashpe tohkequnnooonk: munnehkheh neanag kuttunowaonk.
119.29 Ammanumah panoowae may: kah monanitteae unnunumah kuttunomatuonk.
119.30 Nuppepenamup wunnomwae may: nuppoonumup koosittumooonkash anuhquapeh .
119.31 Nummosogquehtamup koowauwaonkash: woi Jehovah, ahque ogkodchehheh.
119.32 Pish nummuttumaomashontam kuttannooteamooe may, mishshehtauan nuttah.
119.33 Kuhkootumah, woi Jehovah, kukkuhkoowaonkane may; kah pish nunnanawehtauun en wohkuhkuhquoshik.
119.34 Unnunumah wohwohtamooonk, kah pish nunnanawehtauun kuttunomatuonk; nux, pish nunnooswehtamun nashpe mamusse nuttah.
119.35 Pomushahhe kuttannoohteamooe mayut, newutche ne noowekontamooontamun.
119.36 Unnitteahhahhe en koowauwaonkanit, kah matta en iahchuontamunat.
119.37 Qunnupunush nuskesukquash wutch namunnat tahnoocheyeuuk: kah quaquahkqhe ut kummayut.
119.38 Munnehkehtauush kuttunoowaonk en kuttinninneumut, noh {aniit} kukquoqushukqunnat.
119.39 Qunnuppunnumah nuttushpunnamitteaonk ne quahtam: newutche koosittumooonkash wunnekunash.
119.40 Kusseh, nunnontweantamup kukkodteahquttumooonkash: quaquahkqhe ut kussompweusseonkanit.
119.41 Kukkuttumonteanitteaonkash wonk nuhkuhkonkquttti, woi Jehovah; {nux} koowadchanuwaonk neanag kuttinoowaonk.
119.42 Neit pish nuttohto uttoh woh nashpe nompoohumauog noh ashpunnamit: newutche nuppabahtantam kuttinnoowaonk.
119.43 Kah ahque papukquane ammanush wunnomwae kuttooonk wutch nuttoonut; newutche nuttanoosip ut koosittimooonkanit.
119.44 Nemehkuh pish nunnanawehto kuttunomauonk naquahteae, micheme kah micheme.
119.45 Kah pish pabahchiyeue nuppumusham: newutche nunnattinneahhom kukkodteahquttumooonkash.
119.46 Pish wonk nooweogquttum koowauwaonkash anuhquabhittit kehtassootumwog, kah matta pish nuttogkodchuh.
119.47 Kah pish noowekontamwah nohhog ut kuttannoohteamooonkanit, nish wamontamuhpash.
119.48 Nunnitchegash wonk pish nuttashinununash en kuttannoohteamooonkanit, nesh wamontamuhpash: kah pish nunnatwontam ut kukkuhkoowaonkanit.
119.49 Mehquantash ne kuttooonk en kuttinninnumit uttuh annoontamwahheuhp.
119.50 Yeu ne tapehhukqueh ut nootamehpunnaonkanit: newutche kuttinnoowaonk nukquaquahkqhukqunnap.
119.51 Pahtuanumwitcheg nummishe mamoshquohkonukuppaneg: {qut} asq nunnukkodtumoo kuttunomatuonk.
119.52 Nummehquantamup nukoneyeue koosittumooonkash, woi Jehovah; kah nuttapehhomp nohhog.
119.53 Uhquehpunnaanumooonk nunnuhkuhkunkup, newutche matchetooog nag ohquantogig kuttunnomatuonk.
119.54 Kukkuhkoowaonkash nooketoohomaonkanninneapash, ut nuppenoowohteakomukqut.
119.55 Nummehquantamup koowesuonk, woi Jehovah, nuhkonae, kah nunnanawehtop kuttunomatuonk.
119.56 Yeu nuttunohtauunnap, newutche nunnanawehtop kukkodteahquttumooonkash.
119.57 {Ken} nutchuppioom, woi Jehovah, nissip, pish nunnanawehteo kuttinnoowaonkash.
119.58 Nunnanompassuttumup kuskesuk nashpe mamusse nuttah: kuttumonteanumeh neanag kuttinnoowaonk.
119.59 Nunnatwontamup nummayash, kah nukqunnupunumup nussetash en koowauwaonkanit.
119.60 Nukkunuppep kah matta nupputchinwooop nanawehteauunnat kuttannoohteamooonkash.
119.61 Matchetooe chuppissuonkash nummukkookunukuppaneg: qut matta noowannantamoop kuttinomatuonk.
119.62 Poshutipuhkodae pish nuttomohkem kuttapatontumauununnat: newutche sampwe koosittumooonkash.
119.63 Noowechiyeumoog wame nag quashukqueaneg; kah nag nanawehtunkig kukkodteahquttumooonkash.
119.64 Ohke, woi Jehovah numwohteau kukkuttumonteanitteaonk: kuhkootumah kukkuhkoowaonkash.
119.65 Kooneunnehhomp kuttinninneum, woi Jehovah, neanag kuttinnoowaonk.
119.66 Kuhkootumah wunnekin wussuttumooonk, kah wahteoonk: newutche noonomuhtamup kuttannoohteamooonkash.
119.67 Asquam auhkuhpunnauhp, noowauwonip: qut yeuyeu nunnawehteo kuttinnoowaonk.
119.68 Ken koonetum, kah kooneosem; kuhkootumah kukkuhkoowaonkash.
119.69 Pahtuanumwitcheg nuttaiyeuohkone kesehtunkuppaneg panoowaonk: qut nunnanawehteo kukkodteahquttumooonkash nashpe mamusse nuttah.
119.70 Wuttohhoo wunnogkoomoo onatuh pumme; qut noowekontamooontam kuttinnomatuonk.
119.71 Wunnegen wutche nen ne nuttuhkuhpunnonap; onk woh nunnehtuhto kukkuhkoowaonkash.
119.72 Kuttoone unnomatuonk anue wunnekin en nohhogat, onk muttanonkanogkodtash gold kah silver.
119.73 Kunnitchegash nukkeshukqunnapash kah nukkehkenawehhukqunapash: unnunumah wohwohtamooonk, onk woh nunnehtuhto kuttannoohteamooonkash.
119.74 Nag quoshukqueaneg pish wekontamwog nauwehhittit: newutche nuttannoontamup kuttinnoowaonk.
119.75 Noowahteo, woi Jehovah, koosittumooonkash sampwiyeuash; kah wonk ut pabahtanumukquissuonkanit kuttuhkuhpunnasip.
119.76 Koowehquttumauush Kukkuttummonteanitteae wamoahsuonk taphukqutti, neanag kuttinnoowaonk en kuttinninneumut.
119.77 Nohtonteanitteae kukkuttummonteanitteaonkash peyaonukqutti, onk woh nukketeam: newutche kuttinomatuonk noowekontamooonkanin.
119.78 Pahtuanumwitcheg ogkodchhittitch, newutche nuttahchue mammatche unnehhukuppaneg tahnooche: qut pish nunnatwontam ut kukkodteahquttumooonkanit.
119.79 Nag quoshukqueaneg qunnippehhittich en nohhogat, kah nag wahteunkuppaneg koowauwaonkash.
119.80 Nuttah pasquaj ut kukkuhkoowaonkanit; onk woh matta nuttogkodchuh.
119.81 Nukketeahogkou sauantam wutche koowadchanuwaonk: qut nuttannoontam kuttinnoowaonk.
119.82 Nuskesukquash sauompattamoomooit wutche kuttinnoowaonk, unnoowomooash, Ohquompag kuttapheh?
119.83 Newutche nuttogqunneunkquis weshquat ut pukkuttaut: {onch} matta noowannantamoo kukkuhkoowaonkash.
119.84 Tahtashunash ukkesukodtumash kuttinninneum? ohquompag pish kuttissem wussuttumooonk ut wohhogaout noswehtuhhukqueoneg?
119.85 Pahtuanumwitcheg noowonuhkunkuppaneg wonogquash, uttuh matta yaninneunquohk en kuttinnomatuonkanit.
119.86 Wame kuttannoohteamooonkash pabahtanumukquatash: nag tohnooche nunnooswehtuhquog; anunumah.
119.87 Nahhen nummahtuppanukuppaneg ut ohkeit: qut matta nunnukkodtumoop kukkodteahquttumooonkash.
119.88 Quaquahkqhe neanag koowammoahsue monaneteaonk; nemehkuk pish nunnanawehto kuttoone wauwaonk.
119.89 Micheme, woi Jehovah, kuttinnowaonk munnuhkohteau ut kesukqut.
119.90 Kuppabahtanumukquissooonk {yatahteau} en wame pometuonkanit: kummunnehkehtauunnap ohke, kah nonepatteau.
119.91 Nash naquahteahtaash pache yeu kesukkod neanag kukkuhquttummooonkash: newutche nesh wame kootinninneuminneosh.
119.92 Matta wuttapinneamooonkaneos kuttunomatuonk, woh nummamahchumup ut nootamehpannaonkanit.
119.93 Matta pish noowaannantamoo kukkodteahquttumooonkash: newutche nesh nashpe kukquahkqhip.
119.94 Nen kuttaihe, wadchaneh: newutche nunnattinneahhamup kukkodteahquttumooonkash.
119.95 Matchetukeg nuttashkuhwhonukuppaneg nunnushukqunaout: {qut} pish nunnatwontam koowauwaonkash.
119.96 Nunnaumup adt wohkuhquoshik wame panuppeyeuonkash; qut kuttannoohteamooonk mishe kushki.
119.97 Woi toh nuttunukkuhque wamontam kuttumomatuonk! ne nummussontamooonk qunnikesuk.
119.98 Nashpe kuttannoohteamooonkash kuttanue waantamwahhe onk nummatwomog: newutche naquahteae noowetomukqunash.
119.99 Nuttanue wohwahtam onk wame kohkootumaiutcheg: newutche noonatwontamooonkan koowauwaonkash.
119.100 Nuttanue wohwohtam onk kohchiyeuitcheg: newutche nunnanawehteoup kukkodteahquttumooonkash.
119.101 Nukquehtohkodtauunapash nussetash wutch nishnoh pannoowae mayut; onk woh nunnanawehteo kuttinoowaonk.
119.102 Matta nuttammaoop wutch koosuttumooonkanit: newutche kukkuhkootumaiip.
119.103 Toh unukuhque wekanash kukkutooonkash en nukqutchehtamooonkanit! {nux, anue wekonash} onk hony ut nuttoonut.
119.104 Nashpe kukkodteahquttumooonkash nuttohteo wohwohtamooonk: newutche nussekinneam nish pannoowae may.
119.105 Kuttinnoowaonk wequannanteg en nussetut: kah wequaiyeumoo en nummayut.
119.106 Nutchadchekewop, kah pish nutissen, nunnanawehtauunnat kussampwe wussuttumooonkash.
119.107 Nummishe wuttamehpunam: quaquahkqhe, woi Jehovah, neanag kuttunoowaonk.
119.108 Attumunush, koowehquttumauush, nanoue ummagooonkash nuttoon, woi Jehovah, kah kuhkootumah koosuttumooonkash.
119.109 Nukketeahogkou naquahteahteau ut nunnitchekonut: onch matta noowannantamoo kuttinomatuonk.
119.110 Matchetooog noonohtunkuppaneg ahpeh: qut matta nuppaneop wutch kukkodteahquttumooonkanit.
119.111 Nunnemunnumunnateash koowauwaonkash wutche ohtoonk micheme: newutche nesh oowekontamooonkaninneash nuttah.
119.112 Nummommoncheohtoup nuttah ussenat kukkuhkoowaonkash naquahteae, na en wohkuhquhshik.
119.113 Nussekinneam {tohnooche} unnantamooonkash: qut noowommontam kuttinnomatuonk.
119.114 Ken nupputtogqueae aiyeuonk, kah nuttogquinneg: nuttannoontam kuttinnoowaonk.
119.115 Ammaehtiekq, kenau matcheseaquish; newutche pish nunnanawehteo wuttanoohteamooonkash num-Mannittoom.
119.116 Chetaninne neanag kuttinnoowaonk, onk woh nuppomomtam: kah ahque ogkodchuontamutti nuttanoosuonk.
119.117 Pabahtinneh, onk pish nunnannauai: kah pish numomussontam kukkuhkoowaonkash naquahteae.
119.118 Kuttahtaskuhkouok wame panneaocheg wutch kukkuhkoowaonkanit: newutche wuttahsookehkodteamooonkanoo pannoowaonkannumoo.
119.119 Wame ohkee matchetukeg kuttogque mahtuppanoog sekuppasunkanit: newutche noowamontam koowauwaonkash.
119.120 Neyaus nunnukishshau wutche kukquishinnooonk, kah noowapissuontam koosittumooonkash.
119.121 Nummahche issem wussittumooonk kah sampweusseonk: nukkosehkon en nag uhkuhpunnanukqueoneg.
119.122 Kunnippaos kittinninneum wutche waneguk: pahtuanumwitcheg ahque uhquanumwehhukqutti.
119.123 Nuskesukquash sauompattamoomooash wutche koowadchanuwaonk, kah wutche kussampwesuonkane unnoowaonk.
119.124 Unneh kuttinninneum ne anag kukkuttumonteanitteaonk, kah kuhkootumah kukkuhkoowaonkash.
119.125 Nen kuttinninneum, unnunumah wohwohtamooonk, onk woh noowahteo koowauwaonkash.
119.126 Ohquompiyeuai kuttannahkosinneat, Jehovah, newutche nag mateaqunnehteoook kuttinnomatuonk.
119.127 Newutche nuttanue wamontam kuttannoohteamooonkash onk gold, nux anue onk wanegik gold.
119.128 Newutche wame kukkodteahquttumooonkash {papaume} wame {teaquasinish} nussompwontamunnash, {kah} nussekinneam nishnoh pannoowae may.
119.129 Koowauwaonkash muhchantamweyeuooash: uewutche nukketeahogkou wunnanawehtauunash.
119.130 Patutteamooukish kukkuttooonkash wequaiyeuhtoamooash: oowohwohtamhukqunnash assootu.
119.131 Noowoshwunumup nuttoon, kah nummishmishanomup: newutche nunnontweantamup kuttannoohteamooonkash.
119.132 Moninneah, kah kuttumonteanumeh: ne ahhannehheadt nag wamontogik koowesuonk.
119.133 Wunnohtauush nuttontannehtuonkash kuttinoowaonkanut: kah ahque nanawunukqutti neteagwe matcheusseonk.
119.134 Pohquahwhusseh wutch wuttuhkuhpunahteaonk wosketomp: nemehkuh pish nunnanawehteo kukkodteahquttumooonkash
119.135 Wohsumwohtauush kuskesuk ut kuttinninnumut: kah kuhkootumah kukkuhkoowaonkash.
119.136 Sepuppogquash wuttutchuanash nuskesukqut: newutche nag matta nanawehteoooog kuttinnomatuonk.
119.137 Kussompwes, woi Jehovah, kah pabahtanumukquatash koosittumooonkash.
119.138 Koowauwaonkash nesh annoohteamweohpash, sampwiyeuwash, kah pabahtanumukquatash.
119.139 Nukkussapwutteahhaonk nummohchummooonukqun: newutche nummatwomog wannantamook kuttinnoowaonkash.
119.140 Kuttunnoowaonk ahche pohki: newutche kuttinninneum oowamontamun.
119.141 Nuppesisses kah nummeshananimit: onch matta noowannantamoo kukkodteahquttumooonkash.
119.142 Kussompweusseonk ne michemohtae sompweseonkanuoo, kah kuttinnomatuonk ne wunnomwaonkanuoo.
119.143 Wuttamehpunaonk kah uhquammomooonk nunnamhukqunash: {onch} kuttannoohteamooonkash nuttapinneamooonkash.
119.144 Koowauwaonkane sampweusseonk michemohteau: unnunumah wohwohtomooonk, onk woh nuppomontam.
119.145 Nummoup nashpe mamusse nuttah; nootah, woi Jehovah: pish nunnanaweteo kukkuhkoowaonkash.
119.146 Kummauinnittauunup, wadchaneh, onk woh nunnanawehteo koowauwaonkash.
119.147 Nunnekonuhkomup utchuompan, kah nummoup; nuttanoontamup kuttinnoowaonk.
119.148 Nuskesukquash wunnekonuhkunkqunneau nuhkonae ashkuhwositcheg, onk woh nunnatwontam ut kuttinnoowaonkanit.
119.149 Nootash noowadtauohtunkquissuonk neanag koowamoasue monaneteaonk: woi Jehovah, quaquahkqhe neanag koosittumooonk.
119.150 Pasootshaog nag assuhkogik woskehhuwaonk: nooosuhkomwog kuttinnomtuonk.
119.151 Kuppassootap, woi Jehovah, kah wame kuttannoohteamooonkash wunnomwaonkanuooash.
119.152 Papaume koowauwaonkash nowadt noowawahteoup, nesh kummunnuhkohtauunopash micheme.
119.153 Natwontash nuttuhkuhpunnaonk, kah pohquahwhusseh: newutche matta noowannantamoo kuttunnomatuonk.
119.154 Kunnootamwansheh kah pohquahwusseh: quaquahkqhe neanag kuttinnoowaonk.
119.155 Wadchanittuonk wunnooosuhkunkqunneau matchetukig: newutche matta nattinneahhomooog kukkuhkoowaonkash.
119.156 Mogkiyeuash nohtonteanitteae kukkuttumonteanitteaonkash, woi Jehovah: quaquahkqhe neanag koosittumooonkash.
119.157 Monaog nag noswehtuhhukqueoneg, kah nummatwomog: {onch} matta nuppaneoh wutch koowauwaonkanit.
119.158 Nunnauomp panneusseaeninnuog, kah nunnooantomup: newutche matta nanawehteooopaneg kuttinnoowaonk.
119.159 Natwontash toh nuttinne wamontam koowauwaonkash: quaquahkqhe, woi Jehovah, neanag kukkuttumonteanitteae wamoahsuonk.
119.160 Kuttinnoowaonk wunnomwaonkanuoo {waj} kutchissik: kah wame kussampwewussuttumooonkash michemohtaash.
119.161 Sontimoog noonomattehthukuppaneg tohnoooche: qut nuttah quehtiantam kuttinnoowaonk.
119.162 Noowekontamoowontam kuttinnoowaonk, neane noh mashkog mishe sequehtahhamooonkash.
119.163 Nussekinneam kah nutcheshontam pahpanoowaonk: qut noowamontam kuttinnomatuonk
119.164 Nesausuk kuttahshit waenomush nukquitkesukquae: wutche kussamwe wussutumooonkash.
119.165 Mishe wunnohteaonkanuog nag wamontogik kuttinnomatuonk: kah matta pish teag wuttamhukkooog.
119.166 Jehovah, nuttannoontamup koowadchanuaonk kah nuttissep kuttannoohteamooonkash.
119.167 Nukketeahogkou nanawehteoup koowwauwaonkash: kah nesh nummishe wamontamunapash.
119.168 Nunnanawehteoup kukkodteahquttumooonkash kah koowauwaonkash: newutche wame nummayash {ohtaash} anuhquapean.
119.169 Nummoooonk passootshoomooutch anuhquapean, woi Jehovah: unnunumah wohwohtamooonk neanag kuttinnoowaonk.
119.170 Noowehquttumooonk peyomooutch anuhquapean: pohquahwhusseh neanag kuttinnoowaonk.
119.171 Nussissittoonash pish waenomuwaash, mahche kuhkootummaiean kukkukkoowaonkash.
119.172 Nenan pish weogquttumoomoo kuttinnoowaonk; newutche wame kuttannoohteamooonkash sompwesuonkanuash.
119.173 Kunnitcheg anunummonkqutti: newutche nuppepenamup kukkodteahquttumooonkash.
119.174 Nunnontweantamup wutche koowadchanuwaonk: kah kuttinnomatuonk ne noowekontamooonk.
119.175 Nukketeahogkou pomontamoomooutch, kah pish koowaenomukqun: kah koosittummooonkash anunummunkqutti.
119.176 Nunnanwushshop onatuh wawonue shepsut, natinneah kuttinninneum; newutche matta noowanantammooh kuttannoohteamooonkash.
120.0
120.1 UT nootamehpunnaonkanit nummauinnittauop Jehovah, kah nunnootunkup.
120.2 Pohquahwhus nukketeahogkou, woi Jehovah, wutch pannoowae mussussittoonut, kah wutch assookohkodteamooe menannuit.
120.3 Teaguas pish kuttununumont? asuh toh pish kuttinhit, ken pannoowae menan?
120.4 Kene ukkouhquodash nuh masukkenuk, weche junipere mohkossaash.
120.5 Mishe notuhkuhpunnam, newutche nuttoiap Mesech kah nuttain Kedare wetuwomut.
120.6 Nukketeahogkou mahche sepe weche aiyeumau noh sakinneok wunnohteaonk.
120.7 Nummussontam wunnohteaonk: qut kodtoowonish nag mussontamog aiyeuwuttuonk.
121.0
121.1 PIsh nuttashunum nuskesukquash en wadchuut, na wamoouk nuttanunumonteaonk.
121.2 Nuttanunumonteaonk wumoooo Jehovahut, noh ayukup kesuk kah ohke.
121.3 Pish matta unnantamoo kusseet woh ontahtaut: noh nanawehhukquean matta pish kouwequooo.
121.4 Kusseh, noh nanawehhont Israel, matta pish kouwequooo asuk kouwe.
121.5 Jehovah kunnanawehhukkoowaeninneum: Jehovah kuttuhqunnuhtom ut kuttunuhkounut.
121.6 Nuppaz koowoske unnehhukkoo kesukkodae, asuh nahneposhad nuhkonae.
121.7 Jehovah pish kunnanwehhuk wutch wame matchutut: pish nanawehhau kukketeahogkou.
121.8 Jehovah pish nanawehteo kussohhamooonk, kah kuppetutteaonk, yeu wutch kah micheme.
122.0
122.1 NOOwekontamup ne ashittit, petutteatuh wekut Jehovah.
122.2 Nussettunonash pish ohtaash unnome koosquontamut, woi Jerusalem.
122.3 Jerusalem unnikehkosu oque kehtootanut, uttuh muhsogquehtosig:
122.4 Uttuh aiyahhittit chuppanooonkash, wutchuppanooonkash Jah, en Israele wauwaonkanut, tapattontumunnat oowesuonk Jehovah
122.5 Newutche na kuhkenaue wussuttumooonkanuoo: wussittumooe wuttapuonkash wek David.
122.6 Peuhtamook woh oonahteaonkkaninneat Jerusalem: pish wunniyeuog nag wamonukqueaneg.
122.7 Wunnohteaonk ohtaj kuttunnomenutunkanit, kah wunniyeuonk kuttunnomukkomukqut.
122.8 Wutche nemattog kahwechaiyeumogik, yeuyeu nissim wunnohteaonk apehtunkquish.
122.9 Newutche wek Jehovah num-Mannittoomun, pish nunnattinneahham kooniyeuonk.
123.0
123.1 Kuttahshinumauush nuskesukquash, woi keen apean kesukqut.
123.2 Kusseh, neane wuttinninnuminneunk wuskesukkoowoash kunnompattamoomoouk wussontimmomoouh wunnitchegannoo, & neane wuskesukquash nunkiskq kunnompattamoomoouk wunnitcheg wussunkishquomoh: nuskesukqunnonash ne wuttinne pahtissuononeau Jehovah num-Mannittoomun, napajeh nukkuttumonteanumukqunnanonut.
123.3 Kuttumonteaniminnean, woi Jehovah, kuttumonteaniminnean: newutche ahche nummishe numwamechumumun meshananittuonk.
123.4 Nukketeahogkonunnonog ahche numwamechummuog nashpe ummeshananimmuwaonkanoo nag waniitcheg, {kah} nashpe ummeshannanitteaonkanoo pahtuanumwitcheg.
124.0
124.1 WAnnepeh Jehovah noh wechuhhumukqueogup yeuyeu woh Israel unnoowau:
124.2 Wannepeh Jehovah noh mechuhhumukqueogup, ne wosketompaog wapehtunkqueogkup:
124.3 Neit woh keteae nummishashquonukqunonuppaneg, ne ummooshquantamooonkannoo nashqunnag aiyeuohkone nohhogknonut.
