124.4 Neit woh nippeash nunnanuhkuhkunkqunnanonuppash, kussittuan woh papamuhkomup nukketeahogkonun.
124.5 Neit pehtuanumwe nippeash woh uppamuhkomunaop nukketteahogkonun.
124.6 Wunnanumunnaj Jehovah noh asquam maginninnuog nohhoganonog metsuonkanninnuinneat en wepittuwout
124.7 Nukketeahogkonun wuttinne pohquahhamun neane pussehkis wutch wuttahpehhanoowout adchaeninnuog; ahpeh poohkshau kah nuppohquohhomumun.
124.8 Nuttanunumonteaonkanun ohteau oowesuonkanit Jehovah, noh ayukup kesuk kah ohke.
125.0
125.1 NAg pabahtanumoncheg Jehovah {pish} ogquinneunkquissuog Sione wadchu, {ne} matta woh ontahtanook, {qut} machemohtog.
125.2 {Neane} wadchuash qunnupohtaash Jerusalem, Jehovah ne wuttine qunnupuhkouon ummissinninnumoh, yeu wutch yoyatche nux micheme.
125.3 Newutche uppogkomunkannoo matchetooog matta pish sepohtanoo wuttohtoonkanoowout sampwesitcheg: eshkont sampwesitcheg woh summogunumog wunnitcheganoowoash en matcheusseonkanit.
125.4 Woi Jehovah wunne unneh {nag} wanetugik, kah nag sampwuttahhoncheg.
125.5 Qut nag pohchacheg en wonke ummayeuout, Jehovah pish oowechuwunnuh nah anuhkotsicheg matcheusseonk: {qut} wunnohteaonk pish ohteau Israelut.
126.0
126.1 JEhovah ne quanuppunuk ummussunoonk Sion, nuttogquinneunkquissimunonupnag anukquokik.
126.2 Neit nuttoonun numwohteop ahanuonk, kah nenanun unoohumaonk: neit unnoowopaneg ut kenugke penoowohteaut, Jehovah ummishanuhkosuwehtauuh.
126.3 Jehovah nummahche mushanuhkosuwehtunkqun: waj wekontamog.
126.4 Qunnupunush wonk nummussunnoonkanun, woi Jehovah, ogque sowane kussutchuanit.
126.5 Nag mussippequone ahkehteacheg pish muskauantamwe kepunumog.
126.6 Noh suhhog kah mog, nashpet mushshoatue wuskanem, pish wonk moohche mushkouantamwe peau, {pish} pato wuttasseputtunkash.
127.0
127.1 JEhovah matta ayimook wetu, tahnootanuhkosuog nag ne ayikig: Jehovah matta nanawehtoook ootan, ashkuhteaenin tohnooche paquissu.
127.2 Tohnoocheyeuoo kuttomuhenaout nompoae, kutcheke kouenaout, kummechunnaout nooantamwe puttukqunneg: {newutche} ne wuttinne unnunumauon wamononche koueonk.
127.3 Kusseh, nechonog ohtoonkanuooog wutch Jehovahut: kah otomukae mechumooonk wuttunkquattosuonk.
127.4 Neane kouhquatash ut wunnitcheganit nummukquomp: ne wuttogquinneunkquissinneau wuskeninnue wunnamoniinneunk.
127.5 Wunniyeu wosketomp noh uppetanwon namwapinit: matta pish ogkodchuog, qut pish kenoonaog matwaog ut squontamut.
128.0
128.1 WUnnanumou wosketomp noh quahshont Jehovah: noh pamuhshaontog ummayash.
128.2 Newutche pish kummech kunnitchegane anuhkosuonk: pish kooni, kah pish kooniyeuontamun.
128.3 Kummuttumwus pish ogquinneunkquissoo mishimmechumooe wenomsuppog ut kuttohquanukkamukqut: kunnechonog pish ogquinneunkquissuog olive uhtukquesit, quinnippe ohhuttashpean.
128.4 Kusseh, yeu inne wunnanumon noh quahshont Jehovah.
128.5 Jehovah pish koonanumuk wutch Sionut: kah pish kunnaum oonetuonk Jerusalem toh sahke pomantaman.
128.6 Nux, pish kunnau kunnechonog wunnechonoouh; kah wunnahteaonk Israelut.
129.0
129.1 MOOchikit nuttuhkuhpunnanukquog wutch nooskeninnuinneat, yeuyeu woh Israel unnoowau:
129.2 Moochikit nuttuhkuhpunanukquog wutch nooskeninnuinneat: onch matta nussohkunkooog.
129.3 Noohkohteaquamaeninnuog noohkohteaquamuppaneg ut nuppishquanit: nag quaquonitchaquomuppaneg.
129.4 Jehovah sampwesu: noh poohqussumup uppeminneohtonoowoash matchetukig.
129.5 Nag wame ogkodchhittich, kah qushkehhittitch sekinneogik Sion.
129.6 Ogquinneunkquissehhittich moskehtuut ut woskechekomukqut, ne napoohtag asq wawamekinnookup:
129.7 Uttuh nashpe tassasquaenin matta namwohtoook wunnitcheg; asuh washpununk ahseputtunkash uppuchunou.
129.8 Asuh nag na pamuhshacheg unoowoooog, oonanitteaonk Jehovah apehtunkook: koonanumunumun ut oowesuonkanit Jehovah.
130.0
130.1 Wutch moonoiyeuut kummauunittauunup, woi Jehovah.

130.4 Qut kootohquontosuonkan; onk woh kukquishit.

131.0
131.1 JEhovah, nuttah pehtuanumoomunnooh, asuh nuskesukquash pehtuompamukquadtunooash: asuh nooweakehtooo makakish, asuh wassome qunuhquohkish wutche nen.
131.2 Wunnummuhkit nuttunniyeuwahhomp kah nummanunnehhomp nohhog neane oochinnunnahit mukkies wutch oohkasut: nukketeahogkou neaneyeuoo oochinnunae mukkiesit.
131.3 Israel annoononch Jehovah, yeu wutch kah micheme.
132.0
132.1 JEhovah mehquanim David, {kah} wame wuttuhkuhpunnaonkash:
132.2 Toh ane chachekemuhp Jehovah, kah quahshomuhp munnehkesue ummannittoomoh Jakob;
132.3 Wunnumukkit matta pish nuppetutteoh noowekuttamukkomukqut, asuh nuttoh nuttapinneat:
132.4 Matta pish nukkoueohto nuskesukquash, asuh nukkouequohto nannatteaskesukquash:
132.5 Napache nummushkomun aiyeuonk wutche Jehovah, wuttohkeonk wutche munnehkesue um-Mannittomoh Jakob.
132.6 Kusseh, nunnootamunnanonup ut Ephratah: nummushkomunnanonup ut touohkomukque ohteuhkonut.
132.7 Pish nuppetutteaontamumun ootohkeakomukquash: pish noowauwussummuwamun ut ukquensuttasummoounut.
132.8 Omohkish, woi Jehovah, en kuttanwossunnooonkanut: ken, kah kummunnehkesuonkane arkum.
132.9 Kussephosueninnumog ogquehhittitch wunnomwaeseonk: kah koonetuppantamoomog mushkauantamwe mushontoowahhittich.
132.10 Wutche kuttinninneum David, ahque amanush wuskesuk kussissequnittoom.
132.11 Jehovah wunnomwae chachekeimop Davidoh, matta pish ukquiskehtamooun: Ummechumooonk kohhog pish nuppoon {assootumwe} kuttapuonkanit.
132.12 Kunnechonog nanawehtauehhittit noonoowaonk kah noowawaonk, ne pish kohkootumauog; wunnechonoouh pish wonk appuog {assootumwe} kuttapuonkonut micheme.
132.13 Newutche Jehovah pepenamup Sion: ukkodtontamunap wutche ootahkeonk.
132.14 Yeu nuttanwosunooonk micheme: yeu pish nootohken, newutche nukkodtontamunnap.
132.15 Pish nummoocheke wunnantam ummechumum: pish nuttapeh ummatchekoomoh nashpe puttukqunneg.
132.16 Pish wonk nuttogquan wussephosueninyeumoh nashpe wadchanittooonk: kah oonetuppantamoomoh pish wekontamwe mushontoowaog.
132.17 Na pish nuttut sonkhetuwahtauun wuttaskan David: nukkuhquttumup wequannanteg wutche nussussequnnittoom.
132.18 Pish nuttogquan ummatwomoh nashpe ogkodchuonk: qut ut wohhogkat wutchehtukquap pish mussetumoo.

135.1 WAenamoohk Jehovah, waenotumook Jehovah oowesuonk, waenomoohk, woi kenau wuttinninnumoh Jehovah.
135.2 Kenau nepaueaquish wekut Jehovah, ut wutchadchapukkomukqut num-Mannittoomun.

135.4 Newutche Jehovah pepenauop Jakob en wohhogat, {kah} Israel wutche nehenwoncheyeue oonadchasoom.
135.5 Newutche noowahto Jehovah mussukken, kah nul-Lordoomun anoohkauau wame mannittooog.

135.14 Newutche Jehovah pish wussumau ummissinninnumoh, kah pish aiuskoiantam papaume wuttinninnumoh.
135.15 Wuttinninneuhkontunkanoouh penoowohteaog Silverooog kah Goldooog, wunnitchegane anuhkosuonkanoo wosketompaog.
135.16 Wuttoonuog, qut matta kuttooog; wuskesukooog, qut matta namooog.
135.17 Wehtauogkooog, qut matta nootamooog, asuh wanne nahshaonkanunnoo wuttoonoowout.
135.18 Nag kashoncheg wuttogquinneunkquissinneauh: {ne wuttuniinneau} wame papahtanumoncheg.

135.21 Wunnanumunnaj Jehovah wutch Sionut, noh watohket Jerusalem. Waenomoohk Jehovah.

138.0
138.1 PIsh koowaenomush nashpe mamusse nuttah, anuhquaphittit mannittoog pish waenomae kukketoohomauush.
138.2 Pish noowauwussummuam unnogque wunnetuppantamwe kuttampleumut, kah noowaenotum koowesuonk, wutche koowomoahsue monaneteaonk, kah wutche koonomwaonk: newutche kummishehtoup kuttunoowaonk anue onk wame koowesuonk.

138.6 Tokonogque Jehovah ukqunuhquapin, onch moninneauau ohhohpanitcheh: qut wahheau pahtuanumitcheg en noattut.
138.7 Tokonogque pomushaon noeu wuttammehpunnaonkanut, ken pish kukquahquahkqhe: pish kussumogkunum kunnitcheg ayeuohkone ummooshquantamooonkanoo nummatwomog; kah kuttunuhkou pish noowadchonukqun.

139.0
139.1 WOi Jehovah, kunnatinneahkosip, kah koowahip.
139.2 Koowahteo nunnummattapuonk, kah nuttomohkeonk, koowahteo nuttunantamooonk en noadut.
139.3 Kukqunupuhkom nummay, kah nussepsunnooonk, kah kuppahkwahteo wame nummayash.
139.4 Newutche matta kuttooonkanunoo nenanuut, {qut} kusseh, woi Jehovah, kummoeu wame wahtauunash.
139.5 Kunnannohkosuhkah nekonmiyeu, wah wutomiyeu, kah kuppoonum kunnitcheg nohhogat.
139.6 {Yeu} wahteoonk wussome muhchantamweyeumoo wutche nen: qunnuhquat matta woh nootuhtunumooun.
139.7 Tonoh woh nutton wutch kunnahshauanittoomut? asuh tonoh woh nuttushphoowam wutch anuhquapean?
139.8 Uspeon en kesukqut, na kuttiin, ayimon nuttappin chepiohkomukqut, kusseh, na kuttiin.
139.9 Nemunumon mohtompanae munnupohwhunash, kah ieon uttuh wahkqshik kehtoh:
139.10 Na wonk pish kunnitcheg nuttussoowunukqun, kah kuttunuhkou pish nukkogkanunukqun.
139.11 Unnoowaon wunnumuhkit pohkunnai pish nunnuhkuhkunkqun: nuhkon ne pish wequaiyeumoo quinnippe nohhogat.
139.12 Nux, pohkunnai matta kuttassompattamooun; qut nuhkon wohsumoomoo onatuh kesukod: pohkunnai kah wequai tatuppeyeuooash en kohhogat.
139.13 Newutche kuttaoiinneapash nuttoonussog: kupputtogkuhhip ut noohkas wuttotomukqut.
139.14 Pish koowaenomush, newutche wapissue kah muhchantamwe nukkeshitteap; kuttanuhkosuonkash muhchantamweyeuooash, kah nukketeahogkou ne pahke wuttunoowahtauun.
139.15 Nohhog matta attahtosunoop wutch kohhogkat, ne keme kashumuk, kah wunnuhteae kahkenawehhimuk ut ohkee appesunut.
139.16 Kuskesukquash naumuppash nohhog asquam pasqueseon, kah koosuhquahhunkanut wame nuppompahchaiyeumash tanussuhquahwhosupash, nesh ompuhtag kahkenawehtosukuppash, nesh wanne pasuk asq aohtanookup.
139.17 Uttoh wonk unukuhuhque muhshoatuash kuttunantamooonkash en nohhogat, woi God: nesh toh unoohque monatash?
139.18 Nesh aketamon anue monatash onk naguht: toohkeon as koowowetomush.
139.19 Wunnumuhkut pish kuppaguan matchetukig, woi God: newutche amaehtiekq kenau nishshehteaeninnuog.
139.20 Newutche matchetooe kuttaiyeuohkone unnukquog; kah kummatwomog tohnooche nemunumwog koowesuonk.
139.21 Sunummatta nussekinneauoog, woi Jehovah, chashanumukqueaneg? kah sunummatta nunnoowehhukooog nag ayeuohkone wapehtunkqueaneg?
139.22 Nussekinneauoog nashpe panuppe sekinneoatuonk: nuttogquanumoog nummatwomog.
139.23 Natinneahkoseh, woi God, kah wahtauush nuttah: qutchehhe, kah wahtauush nuttunantamooonkash:
139.24 Kah kehkinneash sun matche may nuttappehtunk, kah ussoowusseh mayut ne machemohtag
140.0
140.1 POhquohwhusseh, woi Jehovah, wutch matchetooeninnuut: wadchaneh wutch chekeunnehhuwaeninnuut.
140.2 Nag annantogik woskehhuwaonk ut wuttohhoowout; naquahteae momoeog wutche aiyeuwuttuonk.
140.3 Nag mahche kenehteoog wenanu onatuh ashkookut; addere uhquohskeht ohteau aque wussuttoonoowout. Selah
140.4 Wadchaneh, woi Jehovah, wutch wunnitchekonoowout matchetukig: nanawehhe wutch chekeunnehhuwaeninnuut; nag kod kepuhteahpaneg nuppomuhshaonkash.
140.5 Pahtuanumwitcheg attahshopaneg ahpeh, kah peminneohtonash wutche nen, sepakunopaneg ahshop keshke mayut: nuppoonummunkuppaneg nahshattekash. Selah.
140.6 Nuttunomp Jehovah, Ken nummannittoom: nootash wadtauohtunkquissue noowehquttumooonkash, woi Jehovah.
140.7 Woi Jehovah Lord, noowadchanuwae munnehkesuonk; kupputtogkuhhumup nuppuhkuhk, ut ayeutooe kesukodut.
140.8 Woi Jehovah, unnunumauuhkon matchetuk ukkottontamooonk: annunumwontamoohkon matchetooe wunnatwontamooonk, eshkont {woh} nag mishshehheaog wohhogauh. Selah.
140.9 Wapuhkuhkooitcheg nag wanuhkiitcheg, nehhenwonche wussissittoone oowaskehhuwaonkanoo nuhkuhkunkquehhittich.
140.10 Chukohtae mohkossaash punnishshokqhittich, unnuhkonunnaj noohtaut; en moonoe possahtheganut, onk woh matta wonk omohkeog.
140.11 Mamatcheunnoowaenin ahque munnehkhunnaj ut ohkeit: chekeunnehhuwaenin, machuhk pish oonomattoohkunkqun, ukkepuhkonukqunnat.
140.12 Noowahteo Jehovah pish kunnootamwontam wuttunnomakom noh uhkuhpunadt, & wussompwiyeum matchekoo.
140.13 Wunnummuhkut sompwesitcheg pish tapattontumog en koowesuonkanut; sampwuttahhoncheg pish wuttohkeog anuhquapean.
141.0
141.1 JEhovah kummauunittauush, kunnippe peaoseh; ahchusuttash noowadtauohtunkquissuonk, mauinnittauunon.
141.2 Nuppeuhtamooonk sampshattositch anuhquapean onatuh incense; kah uspunumooonk nunnitcheganash onatuh wunnunkquae sephosuonk.
141.3 Poonush ashkuhwhosuonk, woi Jehovah, anuhquahtag nuttoon: nanawehtauush usquontamwe nussussittoonash.
141.4 Unnogquehtooohkon nuttah en ne machuhk, ussenat mattanuhkosuonkash, weche matcheseaeninnuog: kah ahque mechitti oowekmechummoooash.
141.5 Sampwesuenin togkomukqutti, ne pish wamoahsuonk: kah aiuskomitch, {ne pish} wunnekin pumme, {ne} matta pish soquehtahhamoomunook nuppuhkuhk: newutche pish onch nuppompeuhtam wonk ut ootamehpunnaonkanoowout.
141.6 OOsuttumwaeninumoouh kepuhteamuk ut qussukquanohteaiyeuut, pish nootamog nukkuttoonkash, newutche wekanash.
141.7 Nushkonunonash nanwonkquaash at woshwog wenohk, onatuh howan tamuhtahog kah passehtahhog mehtukquash woskeche ohkeut.
141.8 Qut nuskesukquash unnogquahtaash hohhogat, woi Jehovah Lord: ken kuppapahtanumush, tauwiyeueh tauehkon nuketeahogkou.
141.9 Wadchaneh wutch ahpehhonut ne poonummiehhittitcheh, kah wutch wuttahpehhaoowout nag anuhkositcheg matcheusseonk.
141.10 Matchetooog punushahhititch en nehhenwonche wuttohshoppoowout, ne nan adt pohquohhomon.
142.0
142.1 Nummauunittauop Jehovah, nashpe noowadtauohtunkquissuonk: nashpe noowadtauohtunkquissuonk nuttaiumup noowehquttumooonk en Jehovahut.
142.2 Nussookunumup nootoowaonk ut anuhquapit: anuhquapit nunnahtihteap nootamantamooonk.
142.3 Nunnahshaonk ne kooshkoet ut nuttunnomiyeumut, neit koowahteop nummay: mayut ne pamuhshauhp keme nuppoonummunkuppeneg ahpeh.
142.4 Nuttunuhquaep nuttunuhkonut kah nunnattauompip, qut wanne howan nukkod wahukkoop; wanne nootashpuhhuwaonkanneup; wanne howan tuppanumop nukketeahogkou.
142.5 Kummauinittauunup, woi Jehovah, nissip, Ken nuttuttashpuhhuwaonk, kah nuttahtoonk ut tanuppomontamooe ohkeit.

142.7 Sohhoowus nukketeahogkou wutch kuppushaginittuonkanit, onk woh noowaenotum koowesuonk: sampweseaeninuog pish nukqunupuhkunkquog; ne wutche pish kukkogkuttame unnehhe.
143.0
143.1 NOOtash nuppeuhtamooonk, woi Jehovah, ahchusuttash noowehquttumooonkash: ut kuppabahtanumukquissuonkanit nompoohumah, kah ut koonomwausseonkanut.
143.2 Kah ahque pasoo kuttinninneum en wussuttummooonkanut: newutche anuhquapean matta pish howae wosketomp noh pomontog sompweogquanumou.
